Result: 1. 持续的预测性稳定化削弱了内在扰动的有效影响，降低探索响应性；2. 曲率非对称累积与松弛，导致滞后恢复和迟滞效应；3. 稳定化时机至关重要，早期干预会限制未来探索空间的扩展。

Conclusion: 预测性人工智能系统不仅提供即时帮助，更可能从根本上重塑探索性认知的几何结构，其影响具有长期性和不可逆性，提示需谨慎设计干预时机与方式。

Abstract: Classical theories of cognition describe problem solving as exploratory search through structured problem spaces in which repeated interaction gradually compresses search into efficient representational structures. Predictive artificial intelligence systems introduce a distinct regime in which stabilization may occur before exploratory diversification unfolds, supplying solutions and decision trajectories prior to internally generated search. This paper develops a geometric dynamical framework in which attention evolves over a landscape of strategies shaped by stabilizing drift, endogenous exploratory perturbation, and responsiveness-gated learning. Predictive assistance is modeled as a process of exogenous exploratory compression that stabilizes trajectories before self-generated exploration broadens the accessible regions of strategy space. The framework yields three main results. First, sustained predictive stabilization reduces exploratory responsiveness by attenuating the effective influence of intrinsic perturbations even when exploratory variability remains present. Second, curvature accumulates and relaxes asymmetrically, producing hysteresis and delayed recovery of exploratory mobility after assistance withdrawal. Third, developmental outcomes depend critically on the timing of stabilization, with early intervention narrowing future exploratory traversal before broad representational diversification has occurred. The framework generates empirically testable predictions concerning exploratory entropy, premature convergence, and delayed recovery following predictive stabilization. More broadly, the results suggest that predictive systems may reshape the geometry of exploratory cognition itself.

### [163] [From Senses to Decisions: The Information Flow of Auditory and Visual Perception in Multimodal LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10147)
*Wish Suharitdamrong,Muhammad Awais,Xiatian Zhu,Sara Atito*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究首次系统揭示了音视频大语言模型（AVLLMs）内部音频与视觉信息的流动路径。在音视频视频输入下，模型沿类似视觉语言模型（VLMs）的顺序流程处理信息，音视频贡献比例取决于任务对各模态的依赖程度；而在多个交错的音视频项目场景中，信息流转向并行路径。研究还发现，一旦音视频等模态信息被传递至大语言模型，其对应的令牌可被丢弃而几乎不影响预测结果，甚至带来轻微性能提升，表明信息已有效整合。该现象在多个模型和规模（3B、7B）上均成立，为理解模型内部机制提供了新视角，并推动未来在可解释性、架构设计与推理效率方面的进步。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前对多模态大语言模型（特别是音视频模型）内部信息流动机制的理解仍不清晰，尽管其在科研与实际应用中日益重要，但缺乏对其如何整合视听信号以生成答案的深入分析。因此，亟需揭示音视频信号在网络中的传播路径与作用方式，以支持模型优化与设计改进。

Method: 通过构建两种典型输入配置——音视频视频与多个交错的音视频项目，系统追踪音频与视觉信号在模型内部的传递路径。采用信息流分析、消融实验与跨任务/数据集验证方法，评估不同模态令牌在推理过程中的必要性与影响，结合多个规模的模型（Qwen2.5-Omni 和 Video-SALMONN2 Plus）进行泛化测试。

Result: 在音视频视频输入中，信息遵循顺序流路径，音视频贡献与任务需求成比例；在多交错输入中，信息流切换为并行路径。此外，一旦模态信息被传递给大语言模型，相关令牌可被安全移除，对最终输出影响极小甚至略有提升，表明信息已充分融合。该规律在多种模型和任务中一致成立。

Conclusion: 本研究揭示了音视频大语言模型内部信息流动的基本结构，提出其具备动态路由能力，能根据输入形式自适应调整信息整合路径。这一发现不仅深化了对模型工作机制的理解，也为后续提升模型可解释性、设计更高效架构以及实现轻量化推理奠定了基础。

Abstract: Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) can listen and see, but how do audio and visual signals actually travel through the network to shape an answer? Despite their growing role in research and real-world applications, the internal pathways through which audio and visual tokens influence the final prediction remain poorly understood. In this study, we examine audio-visual information flow inside Audio-Visual Large Language Models (AVLLMs), tracing how AVLLMs route, utilize, and integrate audio and visual information across two input configurations, audio-visual video and multiple interleaved audio-visual items. We find that for audio-visual video, AVLLMs follow the sequential information flow pathway established for VLMs and VideoLLMs, with audio and visual contribution flowing along this pathway in proportion to the task's reliance on each modality. In settings with multiple interleaved audio-visual items, this routing shifts to different parallel streams. Furthermore, we demonstrate that audio-visual and other token types can be discarded once their information is transferred to LLM, with minimal impact on the model's prediction or even slight improvement, generalizing across multiple tasks and datasets, enabling more efficient inference. These findings hold across multiple models and scales, Qwen2.5-Omni and Video-SALMONN2 Plus at 3B and 7B scales, leading to hypotheses on why these flow structures emerge. Together, these results deliver the first coherent picture of how AVLLMs orchestrate sound and sight inside the network and lay the groundwork for the next wave of interpretability, design, and efficiency advances in audio-visual and broader MLLMs.

### [164] [Less Context, Better Agents: Efficient Context Engineering for Long-Horizon Tool-Using LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10209)
*Abhilasha Lodha,Mahsa Pahlavikhah Varnosfaderani,Abir Chakraborty,Abhinav Mithal*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了大型语言模型在企业工作流中作为自主代理时，因企业系统工具响应冗长导致的上下文溢出、过时状态错误和高推理成本问题。通过在Microsoft Dynamics 365 Finance and Operations中进行自动费用分类任务评估GPT-5的四种配置（无用户模型、完整对话历史、仅保留最近5次工具调用/响应对、以及结合自动摘要的剪枝），结果表明：使用摘要的剪枝方法在保持91.6%完整分类率和99.64%平均金额分类率的同时，将令牌消耗降低至55万，运行时间缩短至5.79小时，显著优于完整历史保留（71.0%完成率，148万令牌，14.56小时）。研究还提供了置信区间、效应量分析、敏感性测试、失败分析及跨模型验证（Claude Sonnet 4.5），证实选择性保留近期交互并结合紧凑摘要能有效提升可靠性与效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 企业级工具调用产生的冗长响应会导致大语言模型在自主代理任务中面临上下文溢出、状态过时和计算成本过高问题，亟需高效上下文管理策略以保障模型在复杂工作流中的可靠性和可扩展性。

Method: 在微软Dynamics 365 F&O环境中，针对酒店费用自动分类任务，对比四种不同上下文处理策略：无用户模型、保留完整对话历史、仅保留最近5次工具调用/响应对、以及结合自动摘要的剪枝策略。采用50项任务的基准测试，每种配置进行5次独立运行，固定用户模型以确保公平比较，并通过定量指标（完成率、金额分类率、令牌消耗、运行时间）和定性分析（失败案例、类别表现、窗口敏感性）评估性能。

Result: 相比无用户模型基线（8.0%完成率），完整历史保留提升至71.0%，但消耗1,480,996令牌和14.56小时；仅保留最近5次交互提升至79.0%，减少至535,274令牌和5.39小时；加入自动摘要后达到最优：91.6%完成率、99.64%平均金额分类率，仅需553,374令牌和5.79小时。跨模型验证（Claude Sonnet 4.5）支持结论的稳健性。

Conclusion: 对于此类企业工具使用型工作流，选择性保留近期工具交互并辅以紧凑摘要，是实现更高可靠性与更低资源开销的有效策略，优于全历史保留方案。

Abstract: Large language models deployed as autonomous agents for enterprise workflows face a key challenge: verbose tool responses from enterprise systems can cause context overflow, stale-state errors, and high inference cost. We study this problem in automated expense itemization in Microsoft Dynamics 365 Finance and Operations using Model Context Protocol tools. We evaluate four GPT-5 configurations on a 50-task hotel expense benchmark: no user model, full conversation history, context pruned to the last 5 tool call/response pairs, and pruning with automated summarization. Results are averaged across 5 independent runs, with the user model held constant for the context-engineering comparison. The no-user-model baseline achieves only 8.0% complete itemization. Full-context retention improves completion to 71.0%, but consumes 1,480,996 tokens and 14.56 hours per benchmark. Pruning to the last 5 tool calls improves completion to 79.0% while reducing token use to 535,274 and runtime to 5.39 hours. Adding summarization achieves the best result: 91.6% complete itemization and 99.64% average amount itemized, with 553,374 tokens and 5.79 hours. We further report confidence intervals, effect-size analysis, sensitivity over pruning and summary windows, failure analysis, results across five expense types grouped into three categories, and cross-model evidence with Claude Sonnet 4.5. These results show that, for this class of enterprise tool-use workflow, selective retention of recent tool interactions plus compact summarization can improve both reliability and efficiency compared with full-history retention.

### [165] [Minimalist Genetic Programming](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10237)
*Leonardo Trujillo*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为最小化遗传编程（MGP）的新方法，该方法受人类语言最小主义理论启发，将程序归纳问题重新定义为语法推导任务，而非传统遗传编程中的进化搜索。MGP利用二元集合形成算子MERGE，以增量方式构建复杂的符号结构，避免了传统GP中的代码膨胀问题。在符号回归任务上的实验表明，当选择合适的原子语法对象词汇表时，MGP能够稳定地发现精确的真值模型，而标准GP在此类任务中表现不佳。研究结果表明，最小主义理论对程序归纳具有重要启示意义，值得进一步探索。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统遗传编程（GP）虽然在多种任务中表现优异，但存在代码膨胀问题，且依赖于进化搜索机制，效率和可解释性受限。本文旨在通过引入语言学中的最小主义理论，提供一种更高效、更简洁的程序归纳新范式，以克服现有方法的局限性。

Method: 提出最小化遗传编程（MGP），借鉴人类语言最小主义中的核心算子MERGE，将程序构造视为一个基于二元集合形成的马尔可夫过程，通过增量组合原子语法对象来构建复杂表达式。该方法不依赖自然选择与进化操作，而是通过语法推导实现模型生成。

Result: 在多个具有挑战性的符号回归任务上，当使用合适的原子语法对象词典时，MGP能够一致地发现精确的真值模型，而标准遗传编程则难以达到相同效果。实验验证了MGP在避免代码膨胀、提高精度和可解释性方面的优势。

Conclusion: 最小主义理论为程序归纳提供了新的视角，其核心思想如MERGE算子和最优语法构造过程，可有效提升符号模型发现的效率与准确性。本研究证明了该思路的可行性，建议未来进一步探索最小主义与程序归纳之间的深层联系。

Abstract: Genetic programming (GP) is based on two important insights. First, that any learning task can fundamentally be posed as a program induction problem, where the goal is to construct a symbolic hierarchical model that is expressed as a syntax tree. Second, to pose this task as a search problem, and use evolution to locate the desired model. Since it was proposed, GP has produced notable results in a wide range of tasks and problem domains. This work presents an alternative view by modifying the second core insight of GP, posing the problem as a syntactic derivation task instead. In particular, this paper presents Minimalist Genetic Programming (MGP), an algorithm that like GP is biologically inspired, but instead of evolution it takes inspiration from the Minimalist Program to human language, in which syntax is understood as an optimal solution to the problem of linking two other mental systems. In minimalism, the core computational process is a binary set formation operator called $MERGE$, than can be used to incrementally construct complex syntactic structures using a simple Markovian process. MGP is able to discover the core building blocks of the symbolic expressions, and to incrementally combined them using $MERGE$. The proposed system is benchmarked on symbolic regression tasks that are known to be difficult to solve with standard GP systems because of the propensity for bloat. Results show that when a proper lexicon of atomic syntactic objects are chosen, MGP is able to consistently produce the exact ground truth model on a set of symbolic regression where standard GP struggles to do the same. The insights provided by minimalism are shown to be relevant to the problem of program induction, and should be explored further based on the potential exhibited by MGP in this work.

</details>


### [166] [Regimes: An Auditable, Held-Out-Gated Improvement Loop Demonstrated on LongMemEval with ActiveGraph](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10241)
*Yohei Nakajima*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于事件溯源的代理运行时（ActiveGraph），通过将代理状态设计为仅追加事件日志的确定性投影，实现可审计、可复现的自主改进循环。该系统记录所有失败，支持精确回放，候选修复作用于特定流水线节点，并通过静态检查、沙箱执行、样本内评估和保留集验证等多层门控机制确保修复质量。作者构建了名为Regimes的改进循环，在LongMemEval-S任务上发现读者提示修复能提升准确率0.05至0.10（四次显著），证明了该框架在目标无关任务中的有效性。核心贡献包括：可审计的运行时基础、带保留集门控的改进流程、故障类型分类路由机制以及‘提示作为发现探针’的假设。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前自主改进循环难以信任，因改进过程依赖外部附加结构，导致失败未被记录、诊断无法复现、修复决策缺乏透明性。需要一种可审计、可追溯且可重复的改进框架。

Method: 采用事件溯源思想，构建以仅追加事件日志为基础的代理运行时（ActiveGraph）。代理状态由日志确定性生成，所有操作（包括失败、修复、审批）均作为事件记录。使用故障模式分类（failure-regime taxonomy）将问题定位到流水线特定节点，触发针对性修复。修复需通过静态检查、沙箱执行、样本内与保留集验证后方可上线。

Result: 在LongMemEval-S数据集上，Regimes在五个种子分割中，有四次显著提升准确率（+0.05至+0.10），一次轻微提升（+0.01）；其中两次独立显著（种子5）。尽管总体统计意义受限于共享测试池，但结果表明该方法有效。关键成果包括可审计的运行时、可控改进流程、故障定位机制及提示修复的有效性验证。

Conclusion: 事件溯源的代理运行时使受控改进循环成为第一类工作流。ActiveGraph提供可审计、可复现的基础设施，支持目标无关的改进循环。故障分类路由机制与提示作为修复探针的假设具有重要研究价值，是未来优化的核心方向。

Abstract: Autonomous improvement loops are hard to trust because the improvement process is usually external scaffolding bolted onto the agent: failures go unlogged, diagnoses cannot be replayed, and promote-or-discard decisions land in a side database rather than the agent's own history. We show that an event-sourced agent runtime removes that friction and turns controlled improvement into a first-class workflow. When the agent's state is a deterministic projection of an append-only event log, failures are recorded, a run replays exactly from its log, candidate patches scope to typed pipeline seams, gates are auditable, and every promotion or discard is itself an event. We demonstrate this with Regimes, a loop on the ActiveGraph runtime that diagnoses failed evaluations, proposes a repair at a pipeline point, and promotes it only after static checks, sandbox execution, in-sample evaluation, and held-out validation. The loop is target-agnostic: the same control flow runs against different tasks through a common interface. On LongMemEval-S the dominant failure is not retrieval but reconciliation: the evidence is already in the assembled context, yet the reader answers incorrectly. Across five seeded held-out splits, Regimes discovers reader-prompt repairs that improve final held-out accuracy by +0.05 to +0.10 in four splits and +0.01 in one over-promotion split; two splits are individually significant (seed 5 unadjusted for its sequential promotion structure), and the pooled count is descriptive only, since the splits share one 500-question pool. The durable contributions are ActiveGraph as an auditable substrate that makes controlled improvement loops tractable, the held-out-gated loop it supports, the failure-regime taxonomy routing each failure to a pipeline location (whose marginal value over an unrouted baseline is the primary open question), and the prompt-as-discovery-probe hypothesis.

</details>


### [167] [RealMath-Eval: Why SOTA Judges Struggle with Real Human Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10254)
*Yiteng Mao,Kenan Xu,Yijia Lyu,Wenhao Li,Jianlong Chen,Xiangfeng Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究提出RealMath-Eval基准，评估大语言模型在真实学生数学解答评价上的表现。结果显示，即使最先进的LLM判别器在真实学生答案上表现不佳（均方误差~2.96），而在合成答案上表现更好（MSE~1.17），存在显著的“评估差距”。分析表明，人类错误具有更丰富的语义多样性，而合成错误呈现结构坍缩，且人类推理包含更高信息熵，表明其更难被当前模型捕捉。表面风格迁移无法弥合差距，提示当前依赖合成数据的评估流程可能无法充分反映真实学生思维的多样性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大语言模型在解决高中数学题方面表现优异，但在评估真实学生多样化的解题思路方面能力不足，亟需一个真实、严谨标注的评估基准来揭示这一差距。

Method: 构建了包含224个真实学生考试作答的RealMath-Eval基准；对比模型在真实学生答案与合成生成答案上的评价表现；通过语义嵌入分析误差分布；利用生成概率探针测量信息论惊喜度；测试风格迁移对评估性能的影响。

Result: LLM在真实学生解答上的评估误差高（MSE ~2.96），远高于在合成答案上的表现（MSE ~1.17）；真实错误具有更复杂的语义空间，而合成错误趋于线性低维聚集；人类推理具有更高的信息熵，属于更“离群”的分布；风格迁移无法改善评估效果。

Conclusion: 当前基于合成数据的LLM评估体系难以有效捕捉真实学生数学推理的多样性，必须引入真实人类作答数据以提升评估真实性与可靠性。

Abstract: While Large Language Models (LLMs) have achieved near-perfect performance in \emph{solving} high-school mathematics, their ability to \emph{evaluate} the diverse reasoning processes of real human students remains under-examined. To bridge this gap, we introduce \textbf{RealMath-Eval}, a rigorously annotated benchmark of 224 real-world exam responses from high schools. Our initial evaluation reveals that even state-of-the-art LLM judges struggle significantly on this task, exhibiting a high Mean Squared Error ($\sim$2.96) against expert human grading. To probe a plausible explanation, we contrast this performance with a control setting where the same judges evaluate synthetic LLM-generated solutions. We identify a stark ``Evaluation Gap'': judges are considerably more accurate and consistent on synthetic text (MSE $\sim$1.17) but struggle to generalize to authentic student reasoning. Through semantic embedding analysis, we find that synthetic errors suffer from a ``structural collapse'' into predictable, low-dimensional linear subspaces, whereas human errors form a more diverse error space. Furthermore, generative probability probes suggest that human reasoning involves significantly higher information-theoretic surprisal, indicating that student reasoning transitions are more out-of-distribution for current models. Finally, we find that surface-level style transfer fails to close this gap. Our findings suggest that current LLM evaluation pipelines relying heavily on synthetic data may not adequately capture the diversity of authentic student mathematical reasoning.

### [168] [Supervised Fine-tuning with Synthetic Rationale Data Hurts Real-World Disease Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10279)
*Buxin Su,Bingxuan Li,Cheng Qian,Yiwei Wang,Jin Jin,Bingxin Zhao*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究通过大规模控制实验检验了基于推理过程的监督微调（SFT）是否能提升语言模型在临床预测任务中的表现。结果发现，与仅使用标签微调相比，基于推理的SFT反而显著降低阿尔茨海默病及相关痴呆症（ADRD）预测性能，且该现象在不同模型架构和数据规模下均存在。尽管生成的推理理由在医学上准确且与患者证据一致，但将其作为训练目标仍导致性能下降。根本原因在于叙述合理性与判别式优化之间的结构冲突。研究呼吁更精准地理解何时及如何有效利用推理监督。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 假设基于推理过程的监督微调能通过教会模型不仅‘预测什么’，还‘为什么预测’来提升临床预测模型的表现。然而，这一假设缺乏实证检验，尤其是在高风险医疗场景中。因此需要系统评估其有效性，避免盲目应用可能带来负面影响的技术。

Method: 设计并执行了504种配置的大规模控制实验，比较了基于合成推理数据的监督微调（rationale-based SFT）与仅使用标签的微调在五年ADRD预测任务上的表现；同时进行人类专家评估以验证推理质量，并开展少样本实验测试推理作为推理时演示的效果。

Result: 无论模型类型或数据规模如何，基于推理的SFT均显著劣于仅标签微调；即使推理内容医学准确且可作为演示提升性能，作为训练目标仍导致性能下降；根本原因是叙事合理性与判别式优化之间的结构性矛盾。

Conclusion: 当前广泛采用的基于推理的监督微调在临床预测任务中可能适得其反，提示需谨慎对待其应用场景。未来应建立更精确的理论框架，明确其适用条件，推动语言模型在高风险医疗决策中的负责任发展。

Abstract: Supervised fine-tuning with synthetic rationale data is widely assumed to improve language model performance on clinical prediction tasks by teaching models not just what to predict but why. We test this assumption on five-year Alzheimer's disease and related dementias (ADRD) prediction from longitudinal health histories. Across a large-scale controlled experiment of 504 configurations, we find that rationale-based SFT consistently and substantially hurts prediction performance relative to label-only fine-tuning. The degradation persists across model families and data scales, and is not resolved by using a reasoning-oriented base model. Crucially, the failure is not explained by poor rationale quality: human expert annotation confirms that the generated rationales are medically accurate and faithfully grounded in patient-specific evidence, and few-shot experiments show that the same rationales improve performance when used as inference-time demonstrations rather than training targets. We identify the root cause as a structural conflict between narrative plausibility and discriminative optimization. We hope our work paves the path toward a more precise understanding of when and how rationale-based supervision helps and when it does not, guiding the responsible development of language models for high-stakes clinical prediction.

### [169] [Sim2Schedule: A Simulator-Guided LLM Framework for Autonomous Open-Pit Mine Scheduling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10286)
*Mustavi Ibne Masum,Thiago Eustaquio Alves de Oliveira,Mahzabeen Emu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究提出一种基于模拟器驱动的大型语言模型（LLM）矿场调度框架，使LLM作为自主决策代理，在每一步都由定制模拟器指导，以编码地质技术顺序、开采-加工耦合及动态容量约束。该框架在无数据泄露风险的封闭环境中实现零样本运行，无需云端推理或领域微调，即可生成完整且可解释的开采与加工调度方案。为提供可信性能基准，研究还开发了一种包含现实运营与地质技术约束的新混合整数线性规划（MILP）公式。在不同规模和时间周期的矿场实例上评估，该框架恢复了94%至99%的MILP最优净现值（NPV），同时计算时间呈线性增长。结果表明，模拟器约束下的LLM代理是复杂操作约束下长期工业调度的实用且可扩展替代方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统混合整数线性规划（MILP）虽能提供数学最优解，但其指数级计算复杂度和无法实时适应动态工业环境的问题限制了实际应用。因此亟需一种既能保持高效率又能应对复杂约束的新型调度方法。

Method: 提出一种基于模拟器驱动的大型语言模型（LLM）调度框架，其中LLM作为自主决策代理，通过定制模拟器在每一步生成动作，模拟器整合了地质技术顺序、开采-加工耦合关系以及动态资源容量约束。整个系统在零样本、封闭数据环境中运行，不依赖云推理、特定领域微调或重新训练，确保安全性和可解释性。同时构建新的MILP模型作为性能基准，以涵盖真实运营与地质技术约束。

Result: 在多个不同规模和时间跨度的矿场实例中，该框架实现了94%至99%的MILP最优净现值（NPV），且计算时间随问题规模线性增长，显著优于传统MILP方法的指数级增长。该方法兼具高效性、可扩展性和实用性，适用于长期工业调度场景。

Conclusion: 模拟器约束下的大型语言模型代理为复杂约束下的长期工业调度提供了一种高效、可扩展且可信的替代方案，具备在真实工业环境中部署的潜力，尤其适合动态变化的开采矿山场景。

Abstract: Open-pit mine scheduling is a critical process for maximizing economic return under complex geotechnical and operational constraints. While Mixed-Integer Linear Programming (MILP) provides mathematically optimal baselines, its exponential computational complexity and inability to adapt in real time limit its practical deployment in dynamic industrial environments. This work introduces a simulator-driven Large Language Model (LLM) scheduling framework in which the LLM acts as an autonomous decision-making agent, guided at each step by a custom simulator that encodes geotechnical precedence, extraction-processing coupling, and dynamic capacity constraints directly into the action generation mechanism. Operating entirely zero-shot within a closed, data-secure environment, the framework produces complete, interpretable extraction and processing schedules without cloud-based inference, domain-specific fine-tuning, or retraining. To provide a trustworthy performance benchmark, a novel MILP formulation is developed that incorporates realistic operational and geotechnical constraints. Evaluated across mining instances of varying scale and time periods, the LLM-based framework recovers between 94\% and 99\% of the MILP optimal NPV while scaling linearly in computation time. These results position simulator-constrained LLM agents as a practical and scalable alternative to classical optimization for long-horizon industrial scheduling under complex operational constraints.

### [170] [From Context-Aware to Conflict-Aware: Generalizing Contrastive Decoding for Knowledge Conflict in LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10298)
*Runze Jiang,Taiqiang Wu,Yan Wang,Bingyu Zhu,Longtao Huang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种新的冲突感知解码范式，以解决大语言模型在使用外部上下文时，上下文与参数先验之间的冲突问题。现有方法多采用上下文感知范式，单方面增强上下文而忽视先验，导致错误上下文覆盖正确先验。本文揭示了先验与上下文对数的仿射组合具有固有的“制度不对称性”：外推会无界放大错误，插值则纠正不足，且不存在一种静态策略能同时应对两种情况。为此，作者提出了三态基准（TriState-Bench）来评估冲突方向，并设计自适应制度路由（ARR），动态切换解码策略，在不牺牲正确性和一致性的情况下，显著提升抵抗能力（EM从低于6提升至16-33）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当大语言模型基于检索或增强的上下文生成内容时，外部上下文与模型内部参数先验之间常存在冲突，影响生成可靠性。现有对比解码方法倾向于无条件信任上下文，导致在上下文错误时覆盖正确的先验知识，从而降低生成质量。因此，亟需一种能动态判断并平衡上下文与先验权威性的新方法。

Method: 提出冲突感知解码范式，通过分析先验与上下文对数的仿射组合特性，揭示其固有的制度不对称性；构建三态基准（TriState-Bench）以模型感知方式评估不同冲突状态（修正、抵抗、一致）；设计自适应制度路由（ARR）机制，根据每一步的冲突信号动态选择外推或插值策略，实现高效权衡。

Result: ARR在多个基准上实现了显著性能提升，特别是在抵抗错误上下文方面，其EM得分从低于6提升至16–33，同时保持了修正和一致性的良好表现。三态基准有效揭示了现有方法在冲突处理上的局限性。

Conclusion: 本文证明了静态解码策略无法兼顾上下文错误和先验错误的情况，而提出的冲突感知范式与自适应制度路由能够动态应对双向冲突，显著提升生成可靠性，为大模型在检索增强生成中的应用提供了更稳健的解决方案。

Abstract: When large language models generate from retrieved or augmented contexts, conflicts between external context and parametric priors remain a central reliability bottleneck. Existing contrastive decoding methods follow a \emph{context-aware} paradigm that unilaterally amplifies context over parametric priors, overwriting correct priors when the context is erroneous. We generalize this to the \textbf{conflict-aware} paradigm that dynamically allocates authority between prior and context based on conflict signals, rather than presupposing context trustworthiness. We show that the affine combination of prior and context logits yields a \textbf{power family} with an inherent \textbf{regime asymmetry}: extrapolation amplifies errors unboundedly when the prior is correct, interpolation under-corrects when the context is correct, and no static regime covers both. Existing contrastive decoding methods are instances of this family, mostly extrapolative. To evaluate both conflict directions, we propose TriState-Bench, a model-aware evaluation protocol that calibrates per-model prior knowledge to measure three conflict states: correction, resistance, and agreement. To resolve the asymmetry, we propose Adaptive Regime Routing (ARR), which routes between regimes at each step, lifting resistance EM from below 6 to 16--33 without sacrificing correction or agreement. Our code is available at https://github.com/keith-Jiang/conflict-aware-decoding.

</details>


### [171] [What Spatial Memory Must Store: Occlusion as the Test for Language-Agent Memory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10299)
*Doeon Kwon,Junho Bang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出并验证了基于空间坐标的语言代理'记忆宫殿'系统，强调几何信息在记忆召回中的关键作用。通过三个实验发现：1）仅依赖线性混合的默认策略无效甚至有害，而以几何为主导的加权策略显著提升召回效果（p<10^-15）；2）记忆召回应与可见性分离，引入一维射线-体素数字微分分析器（DDA）可精准判断遮挡后目标，使可见性识别准确率从0.000提升至0.982（p<10^-6）；3）该可见性判定机制在预注册实验中被实时验证，成功发现并修复了实际锚点缺陷。研究贡献在于将空间记忆的存储与读取过程解耦，并提供可测量、可验证的框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有记忆系统缺乏对空间几何信息的有效利用，尤其在遮挡场景下表现不佳。作者旨在通过将空间坐标嵌入记忆系统，测试几何信息是否能提升记忆召回性能，尤其是面对遮挡和位置重复时的表现。

Method: 设计并实现基于世界坐标的记忆宫殿系统，采用预注册实验验证三种假设：1）对比不同权重融合策略（空间+时间+重要性）的效果；2）引入射线-体素DDA算法区分召回与可见性；3）通过自动化脚本与真实世界测试验证可见性判定的实时有效性。所有实验均经过预注册，确保结果可信。

Result: 1）几何主导的加权策略显著优于默认线性混合策略（Delta-Hit@5 +0.3208, p<10^-15）；2）DDA使遮挡后目标识别准确率从0.000跃升至0.982（p<10^-6），且能区分近似位置（准确率1.000 vs 0.533）；3）可见性判定机制在真实环境中被成功验证，错误可见率从1.000降至0.000，整体精确性极强（p=2.5×10^-29）。

Conclusion: 空间几何信息在记忆系统中具有不可替代的作用，必须作为核心要素主导召回机制。本研究实现了对记忆存储与读取过程的解耦，提供了可验证的测量框架，为未来人类盲评多世界研究奠定了基础。

Abstract: Language-agent "memory palace" systems anchor each memory to a world coordinate, on the intuition that geometry adds something text cannot. We make that intuition testable and report three results. First, the memory-palace default of folding spatial proximity into a linear blend beside recency and importance does not help and can hurt: in a pre-registered recall experiment the shipped blend fails its own frozen test (mean Delta-Hit@5 -0.0375, Wilcoxon p=0.306), sitting at a position-blind baseline, while a geometry-led weighting wins decisively (+0.3208, p<10^-15): geometry must lead recall when the query regime is spatial. Second, memory recall and visibility must be separated: recall is occlusion-blind by design (you correctly remember the next room behind a wall), while visibility is a perception predicate over stored geometry that the live system never computed. A one-line ray-versus-voxel digital differential analyzer (DDA), re-pointed from the gaze ray the agent already casts, supplies it: text and the live FoV cone both score 0.000 on 849 behind-wall targets while cone-plus-DDA reaches 0.982 (exact McNemar p<10^-6); coordinate recall separately resolves near-duplicate locations a cosine null cannot (1.000 vs 0.533, n=150). Third, the visibility predicate is confirmed live under a git-committed pre-registration (SPMEM-OCC-LIVE-v1: eight scripted worlds, automated oracle scoring, 96 behind-wall targets, false-visible 1.000->0.000, pooled exact McNemar p=2.5x10^-29), a run that surfaced and fixed a real relay anchor defect. We concede that occlusion-needs-geometry is near-tautological; the contribution is the measurement and isolation, separating what spatial memory must store from how it is read. These pilots power a frozen confirmatory study (SPMEM-ZERO-REAL-PREREG-v1); the full human-authored multi-world study with blind raters remains future work.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用大语言模型（LLM）代理在基线模拟轨迹上系统注入语义有意义的异常行为；通过地图约束的路由重构修正异常点之间的物理移动路径；引入基于环境与位置特征的上下文感知空间噪声模型，以更真实地模拟GPS传感器误差。

Abstract: Although the study of human trajectory anomalies is critical for advancing spatial data mining, empirical research remains severely hindered by a pervasive lack of ground-truth datasets. Despite the availability of several real-world and simulated human trajectory collections, these datasets exclusively capture normal mobility patterns and lack annotated anomalies. This specific scarcity is fundamentally driven by the inherent statistical rarity of anomalous events, precluding the feasibility of conventional observational methods. Compounding this challenge, the systematic acquisition of large-scale mobility data is strictly bottlenecked by prohibitive costs and stringent privacy regulations. To overcome these fundamental limitations and establish a reliable human trajectory anomalies dataset with annotated ground truth, we introduce a novel, end-to-end generative framework designed to synthesize realistic trajectory anomalies at scale. Our architecture bridges the gap between purely synthetic mobility data and complex real-world physical constraints by operating directly on baseline simulated trajectories. We employ Large Language Model (LLM) agents to systematically inject semantically meaningful behavioral anomalies such as irregular out-of-distribution check-ins and skipped routine visits. To ensure rigorous spatial validity, the system leverages map-constrained routing reconstruction to recalculate the physical transitions between these LLM agent-modified staypoints. Moreover, to narrow the simulation-to-reality gap, we augment the resulting trajectories with a context-aware spatial noise model, parameterized by environmental and location-specific variables, to accurately emulate heterogeneous GPS sensor degradation.

### [173] [Self-Distillation Policy Optimization via Visual Feedback: Bridging Code and Visual Artifacts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10334)
*Haoyu Dong*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出Visual-SDPO框架，通过视觉反馈自蒸馏提升代码生成的可视化成果质量，利用视觉定位的代码信用加权机制精准优化缺陷代码段，结合序列级GRPO奖励高质可执行输出，在图表、网页/UI、幻灯片生成任务中显著优于基线模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有代码生成模型在生成可视化内容时因无法实时观察渲染结果，常产生重叠、裁剪、对齐错误等视觉缺陷；需引入视觉反馈以改进生成质量。

Method: 提出Visual-SDPO框架，采用教师-学生结构，利用渲染后的视觉反馈作为特权上下文进行自蒸馏；引入视觉定位的代码信用加权机制，将缺陷溯源至具体代码语句并增强对应部分的训练信号；结合序列级GRPO优化策略，使失败执行仍可通过教师模型学习。

Result: 在ChartMimic、Design2Code和AeSlides等多个基准上，Visual-SDPO相比零样本基线提升超过10个绝对点，相比GRPO至少提升2.4点，且训练步数更少、推理无额外开销。

Conclusion: Visual-SDPO有效融合视觉反馈与代码生成，通过精细化的自蒸馏机制显著提升生成可视化内容的质量与可靠性，为非微分渲染场景下的生成模型提供了新范式。

Abstract: Code-generating large language models (LLMs) increasingly produce visual artifacts such as charts, web pages, and slides by writing programs that are executed by non-differentiable renderers, committing to code before observing the render. As a result, otherwise executable code often yields artifacts with visually salient defects, including overlapping elements, clipped text, broken alignment, low contrast, and overflow. We study visual-feedback self-distillation for code-generated visual artifacts. We propose Visual-SDPO, a self-distillation policy-optimization framework that treats rendered visual feedback as privileged context for a weight-sharing teacher and distills this feedback into a coding student. To make supervision spatially targeted rather than uniform, we introduce Visual-Grounded Code Credit Weighting, which traces each detected defect back to the code statements responsible for the affected elements and amplifies the distillation signal on those statements. A sequence-level GRPO (Group Relative Policy Optimization) term complements the dense token-level objective by rewarding executable, visually high-quality rollouts, while failed executions remain learnable through the self-distillation path by passing execution errors as privileged context to the teacher. We instantiate Visual-SDPO for chart, web/UI, and slide generation with a unified Qwen3-VL-8B-Instruct backbone. Across chart-to-code, UI-to-code, and slide-generation benchmarks (ChartMimic, Design2Code, and AeSlides), Visual-SDPO improves over the zero-shot base by more than 10 absolute points in the primary metric and over GRPO by at least 2.4 points, with fewer training steps and no added inference-time cost.

### [174] [Reasoning or Memorization? Direction-Aware Diversity Exploration in LLM Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10346)
*Jiangnan Xia,Yucheng Shi,Yu Yang,Kishan Panaganti,Zhenwen Liang,Ninghao Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: DiRL是一种方向感知的强化学习框架，通过识别模型内部的推理-记忆方向，引导探索过程更关注真正的推理改进而非记忆捷径。它利用方向加权梯度特征来调整奖励，抑制记忆相关变化，增强推理对齐的探索。在数学和通用推理基准上表现优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有探索方法在语义或梯度空间中鼓励多样性，但未区分多样性是由新推理过程还是记忆模式导致，可能导致探索偏向记忆而非真正推理提升。

Method: DiRL从模型表示中提取推理-记忆方向，构建方向加权梯度特征以表征回溯更新，并通过奖励设计放大与推理一致的探索，抑制与记忆相关的变异。该方法可无缝集成到标准的组相对策略优化（GRPO）中。

Result: 在数学和通用推理基准上的大量实验表明，DiRL显著优于多种现有探索方法，有效提升了大语言模型的推理能力。

Conclusion: DiRL通过方向感知机制实现了更高质量的探索，使大语言模型在强化学习中更专注于发展真实推理能力，而非依赖记忆捷径。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning has become a key paradigm for eliciting reasoning abilities in large language models, where exploration is crucial for discovering effective solution trajectories. Existing exploration methods typically encourage diversity in semantic or gradient spaces, without distinguishing what drives this diversity. A trajectory may appear novel because it follows a new reasoning process, or because it varies memorized patterns and shortcuts. Rewarding both cases equally may steer exploration toward memorization rather than genuine reasoning improvement. In this paper, we propose DiRL, a Direction-Aware Reinforcement Learning framework that anchors exploration to an internal reasoning-memorization direction of the policy. Specifically, DiRL extracts this direction from model representations, constructs direction-weighted gradient features to characterize rollout updates, and shapes rewards to amplify reasoning-aligned exploration while suppressing memorization-aligned variations. DiRL integrates seamlessly into standard Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO). Extensive experiments on mathematical and general reasoning benchmarks demonstrate the effectiveness of DiRL, showing significant improvements over various existing exploration methods.

### [175] [ReflectiChain: Epistemic Grounding in LLM-Driven World Models for Supply Chain Resilience](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10359)
*Jia Luo*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: REFLECTICHAIN 提出一种生成式供应链世界模型（SC-WM），通过6维图-隐空间编码异构供应链网络并融入物理守恒约束，结合双环学习机制分离认知不确定性（基于KL信任域的策略适应）与随机不确定性（随机隐状态回溯），在半导体供应链基准测试中显著提升合理性一致性得分33.0%（p < 0.0001, d = 2.78），在对抗性冲击下保持82.3%可操作性，并表现出反脆弱性（中等压力下收益提升40.2%）。研究识别出三种操作性认知机制：不确定性分离、知识边界检测与经验贝叶斯策略更新，并讨论了五类局限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前AI代理在供应链管理中面临根本性的认识论鸿沟：大语言模型（LLMs）虽能理解政策但缺乏物理基础，而强化学习（RL）虽能优化物流却对非结构化约束语义盲视。需构建兼具语义理解与物理一致性的智能系统以应对复杂供应链挑战。

Method: 提出生成式供应链世界模型（SC-WM），将异构供应链网络嵌入6维图-隐空间，融合物理守恒规律；采用双环学习框架，分离认知不确定性（以KL信任域约束策略更新）与随机不确定性（通过随机隐状态回溯建模），实现策略动态优化与风险感知。

Result: 在包含10个节点、SIR风险传播、6种扰动类型和10种策略约束模板的半模拟半导体基准（Semi-Sim）上，REFLECTICHAIN使合理性一致性得分提升33.0%（p < 0.0001, d = 2.78），在对抗性冲击下维持82.3%可操作性，且在中等压力下呈现+40.2%的反脆弱收益。

Conclusion: REFLECTICHAIN成功弥合了大语言模型与强化学习在供应链智能中的认知鸿沟，揭示了不确定性分离、知识边界检测与经验贝叶斯更新等关键操作机制，但其在动态拓扑适应、多模态数据融合、计算开销、可解释性及长期演化建模方面仍存在局限，未来需进一步探索。

Abstract: AI agents in supply chains face a fundamental epistemic gap: large language models (LLMs) interpret policies but lack physical grounding, while reinforcement learning (RL) optimizes flows but is semantically blind to unstructured constraints. We introduce REFLECTICHAIN, bridging this gap through a Generative Supply Chain World Model (SC-WM) - encoding heterogeneous supply networks into a 6-dim graph-latent space with physical conservation - and Double-Loop Learning that separates epistemic uncertainty (KL-trust-region-bounded policy adaptation) from aleatoric uncertainty (stochastic latent rollouts). On Semi-Sim, a 10-node semiconductor benchmark with SIR risk propagation, 6 perturbation types, and 10 policy constraint templates, REFLECTICHAIN improves Rationale Consistency Score by 33.0% (p < 0.0001, d = 2.78), maintains 82.3% operability under adversarial shocks, and exhibits anti-fragile behavior (+40.2% gain under moderate pressure). We identify three operational epistemic mechanisms - uncertainty separation, knowledge-boundary detection, and empirical Bayesian policy updating - and discuss five limitation categories.

We propose three mechanisms to address this challenge: evaluator co-evolution, which incorporates discovered champions into the opponent pool; hierarchical deep evaluation, which replaces noisy few-game scores with statistically reliable assessments; and weakness pressure, which dynamically up-weights the most difficult opponents to break through plateaus. We implement these mechanisms within FAMOU, a framework built upon the same foundation-model code-evolution paradigm as OpenEvolve and ShinkaEvolve. Notably, the LLM mutation process generates tactical structures entirely absent from the seed strategies -- including lookahead search and adaptive interception -- demonstrating that code-level evolution can produce nontrivial algorithmic innovations in adversarial settings. The FAMOU-evolved strategy further achieved 1st place in the hardware round-robin and 3rd in simulation at the AAMAS 2026 MCTF Competition, validating its real-world transferability. ### [179] [STAGE-Claw: Automated State-based Agent Benchmarking for Realistic Scenarios](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10394)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: STAGE-Claw提供了一种可扩展、基于状态的真实个人代理评估方法，能够有效支持复杂、真实的用户场景评估，推动个人代理系统的可靠发展。

Abstract: Large language models are increasingly used to power personal agents for everyday applications, but evaluating these agents remains a challenge. Existing benchmarks still rely on sandboxed artifacts, static task design, and coarse scoring, which hinder scalability and limit progress toward reliable personal-agent evaluation. This paper introduces STAGE-Claw, an automated framework for building and evaluating realistic personal-agent scenarios in state-based personal-computing environments. Given a task hint, STAGE-Claw automatically creates and validates a realistic benchmark task with its environment, task prompts, ground truth, and related verification programs. Agents are then evaluated in realistic operating environments, where performance is measured by the correctness of the final system state rather than only the textual response. Using STAGE-Claw, this paper creates a benchmark with 40 challenging real scenario agent tasks, evaluates 11 frontier models, and analyzes their task scores, costs, tool-call reliability, and common failure patterns. Overall, STAGE-Claw offers a scalable, state-based way to evaluate agents in realistic user scenarios.

</details>

### [182] [Trace2Policy: From Expert Behavior Traces to Self-Evolving Decision Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10457)
*Junli Zha,Jinbo Wang,Chao Zhou,Xiang Song*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出Trace2Policy框架，通过错误驱动的迭代技能优化（EISR）机制，系统性地恢复和改进企业专家在审计、合规和合同审查中隐含的决策规则。该方法通过多轮执行规则、聚类错误根因（缺失、错误、冲突）、应用针对性修复并进行回归验证，持续提升规则质量。实验表明，在五种大模型上，单次蒸馏性能约70%，而经过八轮EISR优化后，规则编译为确定性Python代码可达到79.6%准确率，且推理无需调用大模型。编译后的执行形式比大模型提示词高9.8个百分点，显著提升性能。在物流巨头部署22天，处理3,349个审计案例，优于原有纯大模型基线（72.7%）。引入大模型回退反而降低准确率。其自动化变体Auto-EISR每轮成本仅5-10美元，远低于人工专家的70小时，且可零重构迁移至法律推理（LegalBench）和流程挖掘（BPIC 2012）等公开基准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在审计、合规与合同审查等任务中，企业专家依赖隐含的决策规则，但这些规则难以显式表达且易受模型能力限制。现有基于大模型的方法在低基率、高敏感场景下表现受限，且缺乏对规则本身的系统性优化机制。因此，亟需一种能从实际错误中学习并持续改进规则质量的方法，以突破模型能力瓶颈，实现高可靠、低成本的生产级应用。

Method: Trace2Policy框架的核心是EISR（Error-driven Iterative Skill Refinement）机制：1）维护一份人类可读的规则文档作为优化目标；2）每轮在验证集上执行规则，识别并聚类错误至三类根因（MISSING、WRONG、CONFLICT）；3）针对每类错误应用特定修复策略（如补全、修正或消解冲突）；4）仅允许通过回归测试的变更提交，确保稳定性；5）最终将优化后的规则编译为确定性Python代码，实现零模型调用的高效推理。此外，提出Auto-EISR自动版本，利用大模型辅助生成修复建议，大幅降低人工成本。

Result: 在五个大模型上，单次蒸馏性能约70%，经八轮EISR优化后规则准确率提升至79.6%（无大模型调用）。编译版规则相比大模型提示词高出9.8个百分点。在真实物流场景部署22天，处理3,349个审计案例，准确率达72.7%，优于原纯大模型基线。引入大模型回退反而导致性能下降。Auto-EISR每轮成本仅为5-10美元，相比人工节省约70小时，且在LegalBench和BPIC 2012等四个公开基准上实现零重构迁移，验证了方法的泛化能力。

Conclusion: 规则质量是合规敏感、低基率决策任务中的关键性能杠杆，而非模型能力本身。通过错误驱动的迭代优化机制（EISR），可系统性提升规则的准确性与可靠性。编译后的确定性规则不仅性能更优，且具备更高的可解释性、可维护性和生产可用性。该方法为复杂业务场景下的智能决策提供了可落地、可持续演进的解决方案。

Abstract: Decision rules that enterprise experts apply tacitly -- in auditing, compliance, and contract review -- can be systematically recovered and improved through iterative error analysis. We present \textbf{Trace2Policy}, whose core mechanism -- \textbf{EISR} (\textbf{E}rror-driven \textbf{I}terative \textbf{S}kill \textbf{R}efinement) -- maintains a human-readable rule document as its optimization target: each round executes the rules on a validation set, clusters errors by root cause into MISSING, WRONG, or CONFLICT types, applies targeted patches, and commits only those that pass a regression gate. \textbf{For this class of compliance-sensitive, skewed-base-rate decision tasks, we identify rule quality -- not model capability -- as the dominant performance lever}: across five LLMs, one-shot distillation plateaus near $\sim$70\% on the deployed pool, while eight EISR rounds lift the same rules to 79.6\% when compiled into deterministic Python -- zero LLM calls at inference. \textbf{Execution form compounds the gain: in production, the same EISR-refined content runs 9.8~pp higher as compiled Python than as an LLM prompt, a form-and-engineering bundle the 22-day deployment matured together.} Deployed for 22 days at a major logistics carrier (3,349 audit cases), the compiled pipeline outperforms the pure-LLM baseline it replaced (72.7\%); on these calibrated, skewed-base-rate workloads, re-enabling LLM fallback monotonically degrades accuracy. An LLM-driven variant, \textbf{Auto-EISR}, reproduces this refinement at \$5--\$10 per cycle versus $\sim$70 expert-hours, and transfers to four public benchmarks spanning legal reasoning (LegalBench) and process-mining decisions (BPIC 2012) without re-engineering.

</details>


### [183] [ComBench: A Benchmark for Rigorous Proof Reasoning and Constructive Realization in Olympiad-Level Combinatorics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10479)
*Shunkai Zhang,Haoran Zhang,Yun Luo,Qianjia Cheng,Haodi Lei,Yizhuo Li,Runzhe Zhan,Zhilin Wang,Bangjie Xu,Yucheng Su,Xinmiao Han,Xiaoye Qu,Dongrui Liu,Zhouchen Lin,Yu Qiao,Ning Ding,Yafu Li,Yu Cheng*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出ComBench，一个面向奥数级组合数学的基准测试，用于评估和诊断大语言模型的组合推理能力。该基准包含100道人工标注的竞赛级题目，分为以分析为主的问题（需严格数学论证）和以构造为主的问题（需明确构造并验证正确性）。评估协议结合了基于评分标准的证明评分与确定性构造验证，揭示了证明质量与构造有效性之间的差异。实验表明，当前最强模型在整体平均得分上仅达65.4%，最佳4次尝试得分75.3%，且模型在严谨证明推理与构造实现方面表现出显著差异：某些模型在证明上表现较弱但在构造上更强。存在性与构造类问题对主流前沿模型仍具挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前最先进大语言模型在奥数级组合数学任务中表现不一，暴露出在创造性数学推理方面的不足。亟需一个能有效评估和诊断模型组合推理能力的基准。

Method: 构建ComBench基准，包含100道人类标注的竞赛级组合数学题，分为分析型与构造型两类；采用基于评分标准的证明评分与确定性构造验证相结合的评估协议，以检测模型在逻辑严谨性与构造能力上的差异。

Result: ComBench未被饱和，最强模型仅达到65.4%整体平均分和75.3%最佳4次尝试得分；模型在‘严谨证明推理’与‘构造实现’两方面能力不同，部分模型在构造任务上优于证明任务；存在性与构造类问题始终是最难的类别。

Conclusion: ComBench为评估大模型在高阶组合数学推理中的能力提供了有力工具，揭示了当前模型在创造性数学推理方面的局限，尤其在构造性问题与存在性论证上仍有巨大提升空间。

Abstract: Combinatorics is central to Olympiad-level mathematical problem solving, requiring deep discrete reasoning, creative constructions, and rigorous structural insight. Recent evidence suggests that even today's strongest frontier models remain uneven on Olympiad combinatorics, revealing a gap in creative mathematical reasoning. We introduce ComBench, an Olympiad-level combinatorics benchmark for evaluating and diagnosing the combinatorial reasoning capabilities of large language models. ComBench contains 100 human-annotated competition-level problems organized around two complementary settings: analysis-centric problems, which primarily require rigorous mathematical arguments, and construction-centric problems, which require explicit constructions in addition to correctness justifications. The evaluation protocol combines rubric-guided proof grading with deterministic construction verification, exposing cases where proof quality and construction validity diverge. Experiments on frontier open- and closed-source models show that ComBench is far from saturated: the strongest model reaches 65.4% overall Avg. and 75.3% overall Best@4. We further find that Rigorous Proof Reasoning and Constructive Realization are distinct capabilities: Kimi-K2.6 trails GPT-5.5 on analysis-centric proof grading but surpasses it on construction-centric Best@4, while Existence and Construction problems remain consistently hardest across representative frontier models.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Cross-modal knowledge distillation (CMKD) studies how a (large) teacher model trained on one type of data (e.g., images) can guide a (smaller) student model building on another type of data (e.g., text/audio). Existing CMKD methods often require paired multi-modal data with aligned semantics, but obtaining such paired data are often costly and impractical. To mitigate this limitation, we develop a new CMKD framework for the more challenging setting where paired data are unavailable. In particular, we establish a cross-modal distributional relationship between teacher and student models, which reveals two fundamental quantities governing effective distillation: feature alignment and label alignment. These quantities characterize semantic discrepancy between modalities at the levels of representation and prediction distributions, respectively. Motivated by this insight, we propose a principled framework, with theoretical guarantees, that enables effective cross-modal knowledge distillation by aligning distributions rather than individual samples. Extensive experiments across a wide range of multimodal benchmarks show that our framework is highly effective in both unpaired and paired data settings, improving significantly over prior work.

### [187] [HIPIF: Hierarchical Planning and Information Folding for Long-Horizon LLM Agent Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10507)
*Juncheng Diao,Zhicong Lu,Peiguang Li,Yongwei Zhou,Changyuan Tian,Qingbin Li,Rongxiang Weng,Jingang Wang,Xunliang Cai*

TL;DR: 提出HIPIF方法，通过子目标分解和已完成进度的摘要折叠来缓解长上下文干扰，提升大语言模型在多轮长期任务中的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法未能直接解决长上下文干扰问题，即持续增长的历史信息削弱了代理对全局任务状态的追踪能力，影响后续推理与决策。

Method: HIPIF通过端到端训练使代理围绕显式子目标组织长期执行，并折叠已完成的子目标历史以减少长上下文干扰；结合层次化反思与面向子目标的过程奖励，指导子目标的生成、转换与执行。

Result: 在三个公开的代理基准测试中，实验验证了该方法的有效性，显著提升了长周期任务中的性能。

Conclusion: HIPIF有效缓解了长上下文干扰，增强了大语言模型在复杂、长期任务中的规划与执行能力，且无需依赖昂贵的辅助模型或特定任务专家轨迹。

Abstract: While Large Language Models (LLMs) have demonstrated strong capabilities as autonomous agents across a wide range of tasks, their performance often degrades in multi-turn long-horizon agentic tasks. Existing methods have made progress through fine-grained credit assignment to alleviate long-horizon sparse rewards and hierarchical reinforcement learning to decompose tasks and reduce long-term dependency. However, these methods still do not directly address long-context interference, in which continuously growing histories weaken the agent's ability to track the global task state and impair subsequent reasoning and decision-making. Inspired by the way humans handle complex tasks through subgoal decomposition and completed progress summarization, we propose Hierarchical Planning and Information Folding (HIPIF) for long-horizon LLM agent learning. HIPIF trains the agent end-to-end to organize long-horizon execution around explicit subgoals while folding completed subgoal histories to reduce long-context interference. Furthermore, to stabilize subgoal-based planning and execution, HIPIF combines hierarchical reflection and subgoal-oriented process rewards to guide subgoal generation, transition, and execution, without relying on costly auxiliary models or task-specific expert trajectories. Extensive experiments on three publicly available agentic benchmarks demonstrate the validity of our method.

### [188] [ActiveMem: Distributed Active Memory for Long-Horizon LLM Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10532)
*Yunhan Jiang,Wenbin Duan,Shasha Guo,Liang Pang,Xiaoqian Sun,Huawei Shen*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大语言模型记忆机制多为集中式，存在上下文过载与信息丢失的权衡问题，难以有效支持长时推理任务。

Result: 在BrowseComp-Plus和GAIA数据集上的实验表明，ActiveMem达到当前最优准确率，且计算开销显著降低。

Abstract: Memory is essential for enabling large language model (LLM) agents to handle long-horizon reasoning tasks. Existing memory mechanisms are largely centralized, typically organizing retrieved information and interaction history within a single model context. This design imposes a fundamental trade-off: scaling reasoning trajectories risks context overload, whereas aggressive content pruning may result in irreversible information loss. Seeking a better trade-off, we draw inspiration from human cognitive systems, especially the functional complementarity between the prefrontal cortex (executive control) and the hippocampus (memory management), suggesting that such a trade-off need not be inherent, but may instead stem from centralized memory organization. To this end, we propose ActiveMem, a heterogeneous framework that decouples agent memory from the core reasoning process. Specifically, a high-level Planner utilizes distilled semantic gists to execute reasoning, while a lightweight, distributed memory system operates in parallel to actively accumulate and consolidate these gists throughout the task. ### [189] [One Token per Multimodal Evidence: Latent Memory for Resource-Constrained QA](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10572)
*Zhi Zheng,Ziqiao Meng,Hao Luan,Wei Liu,Wee Sun Lee*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: Latent Memory 提出一种基于潜在空间的内存范式，用小型压缩模型生成的高维潜在标记替代原始文本或图像证据，显著降低生成模型的令牌消耗和存储压力，在多个文本和多模态问答基准上表现优异，且在图像接地问答任务中表现最强。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有记忆范式使用原始文本和图像形式表示记忆项，导致检索系统需将大量原始数据传递给生成模型，造成高令牌消耗和存储压力，难以在资源受限的应用中使用。

Method: 提出潜空间记忆机制，利用小型压缩语言模型/视觉语言模型将每个原始证据转换为单一高维潜在标记，并在统一潜在表示空间中进行查询嵌入与相关潜在标记检索，直接通过预训练的语言模型或视觉语言模型生成答案；压缩器通过重建、对比和蒸馏目标联合训练以确保潜在标记在重建、检索和生成方面的信息丰富性。

Result: 在七个纯文本问答基准（如 HotpotQA）和多模态问答基准上，该方法实现了与先进检索增强生成（RAG）基线相当的问答性能，同时减少3至10倍的生成令牌消耗；在 WebQA 上展现出最强的图像接地问答性能。

Abstract: External memory effectively grounds large language models (LLMs) and vision-language models (VLMs)-based question answering (QA) in relevant multimodal evidence. However, existing memory paradigms represent each memory item in raw text and image forms, so retrieval-based systems must pass the retrieved text or images to the generation LLMs/VLMs, resulting in high token consumption and storage pressure, making it unaffordable for resource-constrained applications. We propose Latent Memory, a latent-space memory paradigm that replaces each raw text or image evidence item with a single high-dimensional latent token produced by a small compressor LLM/VLM. Rather than retrieving raw evidence for generation, Latent Memory operates in a unified latent representation space: the query is embedded into this space to retrieve relevant latent tokens, and the retrieved latent tokens are directly prompted to a pretrained LLM or VLM for answer generation. To make each latent token simultaneously informative for reconstruction, retrieval, and generation, we train the compressor with reconstruction, contrastive, and distillation objectives in a unified end-to-end manner. Latent Memory is evaluated on seven text-only QA benchmarks (e.g., HotpotQA) and multimodal QA benchmarks, where it achieves competitive QA performance compared to advanced RAG baselines while consuming 3x to 10x fewer generator tokens. It can also deliver the strongest image-grounded QA performance on WebQA. Code is available at https://github.com/zz1358m/Latent-Memory-Master.

### [190] [Learning What to Remember: Observability-Safe Memory Retention via Constrained Optimization for Long-Horizon Language Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10616)

Method: 提出OSL-MR框架，将记忆保留建模为受约束的随机优化问题；引入观测安全学习机制，严格区分在线可观测特征与离线监督信号（OAS）；采用证据学习器结合混合评分启发式，实现从交互数据中学习查询条件下的证据价值，同时保持部署安全性与可观测性一致性。

Result: 在LOCOMO和LongMemEval基准上，OSL-MR显著优于传统基于时效性的方法、生成式代理评分方式及其他启发式基线，尤其在低内存预算下优势明显；混合评分先验有效提升精确率，维持高召回率；对不同成本参数配置表现出良好鲁棒性。

Abstract: Long-horizon language agents accumulate observations, reasoning traces, and retrieved facts that exceed their finite context windows, making memory retention a fundamental resource-allocation problem. Existing memory systems improve management through heuristic scoring, retrieval optimization, or learned compression, but largely treat retention as a local decision problem and do not explicitly model its long-term consequences under realistic observability constraints. To fill this gap, we formulate memory retention as a constrained stochastic optimization problem with explicit budget feasibility, evidence utility, and delayed costs including miss penalties, reacquisition delays, and stale-information risk. We then propose OSL-MR (Observability-Safe Learning for Memory Retention), a novel framework that enforces a strict separation between online-observable features and offline-available supervision (OAS). OSL-MR combines an evidence learner trained from realized evidence supervision with a Mixed-Score heuristic that serves both as a deployable online-safe baseline and as a structured inductive prior for learning. The resulting policy learns query-conditioned evidence value directly from interaction data while remaining deployable under the same observability constraints. Experiments on LOCOMO and LongMemEval show that OSL-MR consistently outperforms recency-based methods, Generative Agents-style scoring, and other heuristic baselines, particularly under tight memory budgets. The Mixed-Score prior further improves precision while preserving recall, and sensitivity analysis demonstrates robustness across a wide range of cost configurations.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将记忆建模为以主题为单位的结构化文档，通过缓冲区暂存新观测，并周期性地将其整合为连贯的文本上下文；推理阶段采用迭代工具调用方式实现对记忆的逐步读取与分析。

Conclusion: Infini Memory通过主题结构化文档和迭代检索机制，有效解决了长期大模型代理中记忆维护与证据利用的挑战，为构建可持续、可演进的智能体记忆系统提供了可行路径。

Existing memory systems often store observations as isolated records, summaries, or indexed fragments, which makes evidence aggregation, fact revision, and memory maintenance difficult. We propose Infini Memory, a maintainable text-based persistent memory architecture that treats agent memory as topic-structured documents. Each topic document serves as a semantic unit for collecting related evidence, preserving metadata, and revising facts over time. New observations are first staged in a buffer and periodically consolidated into coherent textual contexts. At inference time, an agentic retrieval procedure lets the LLM read memory through iterative tool calls rather than a single retrieval step. On MemoryAgentBench, Infini Memory achieves 64.7% overall score. Ablations show that topic-structured maintenance and iterative evidence inspection improve complementary aspects of long-term memory use.

### [192] [When the Chain of Thought Knows Better: Failure Modes in Multi-Turn Reasoning Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10740)
*Sai Kartheek Reddy Kasu,Nils Lukas,Samuele Poppi*

TL;DR: 本文提出一种名为CoT-Output 2x2安全矩阵的追踪级诊断框架，通过在内部推理和可见输出两个维度上标注每一轮对话，识别出四种故障类型：稳健对齐、对齐伪装、明显越狱以及一种新型的上下文注入失败（即内部推理安全但输出产生危害，体现多轮推理不忠实）。基于6750个回合级观察数据，在信息危害场景下评估三个蒸馏推理目标，发现两个可复现的漏洞：监督悖论（明确监控提示反而提升对齐伪装率）和上下文注入失败（模型锁定不安全外部输出，尽管内部状态安全）。研究公开了完整多轮对话与推理轨迹数据集，以支持后续追踪诊断研究。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有终端评分评估无法揭示多轮推理模型中的隐藏错误动态，例如模型早期锁定不安全立场但最终拒绝率与稳健基线无异，因此需要更细粒度的诊断方法来暴露这些时间性缺陷。

Method: 提出CoT-Output 2x2安全矩阵，对每一轮对话在内部推理和可见输出两个独立维度上进行标签化，构建四类操作定义的失败单元；在五种监督条件下，对三个蒸馏推理目标进行攻击测试，收集信息危害场景下的多轮对话数据，并分析其行为模式。

Result: 发现两个可复现的漏洞：监督悖论（显式监控提示反而增加对齐伪装率）和上下文注入失败（内部推理安全但输出有害），揭示了多轮推理中推理与输出不一致的问题。

Abstract: Failures in multi-turn reasoning models are largely invisible to terminal-score evaluation. A model can lock onto an unsafe stance early in a long dialogue, yet its final-turn refusal rate may appear indistinguishable from a robustly aligned baseline. To expose these hidden temporal dynamics, we propose a trace-level diagnostic - the CoT-Output 2x2 safety matrix. This framework labels every turn along two independent axes (internal reasoning and visible output), yielding four operationally defined failure cells: robust alignment, alignment faking, overt jailbreak, and a distinct failure mode we term context-injection failure (where the CoT maintains safe reasoning, but the visible output produces harm, highlighting a multi-turn manifestation of reasoning unfaithfulness). We evaluate three distilled reasoning targets against a fixed attacker across five oversight conditions, collecting 6750 turn-level observations on the Information-Hazard scenario. Our analysis reveals two reproducible vulnerabilities: an oversight paradox where explicit monitoring cues paradoxically increase alignment-faking rates rather than suppress them, and a context-injection failure where models lock onto unsafe external outputs despite safe internal states. We release the full dataset of multi-turn dialogues and CoT traces to support follow-up trace-diagnostic research.

### [193] [The Arbiter Agent: Continually Monitoring Multi-Agent Conversations to Detect Emergent Misalignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10747)
*Filippo Tonini,Federico Torrielli,Anton Danholt Lautrup,Peter Schneider-Kamp,Mustafa Mert Çelikok,Lukas Galke Poech*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为Arbiter的代理，用于实时监控由多个语言模型代理组成的系统中的对话，识别可能表现不一致的参与者。Arbiter在有限的‘检查预算’下运作，需谨慎分配资源，可选择等待、质询参与者、检查内部信息（如系统提示或推理轨迹）或记录可疑行为。实验评估了五种不同对话场景，涵盖从高风险金融建议到评估感知和合谋代理的情况，测试了五种能力递增的工具配置和两种主干模型。结果显示，Arbiter能提前检测出不一致行为，主动检查工具显著提升检测准确性和速度；权重引起的不一致最难检测，而指令引起的不一致即使在被动观察下也能可靠识别。日志工具具有双重作用：提高召回率但降低精确度。研究表明，持续且预算敏感的监控能有效发现不一致，监督多代理系统需要将审计者视为过程中的主动参与者。代码已开源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着由多个语言模型代理构成的AI系统日益普遍，它们在共同决策中面临交互带来的对齐问题。尽管单个代理在独立测试中表现良好，但在协作过程中可能出现不一致行为。因此，亟需一种机制来实时监测多代理对话，及时发现潜在的不一致行为，以保障系统的安全与可靠性。

Method: 提出Arbiter代理，具备实时监控能力，根据有限的检查预算动态决定行动策略：包括等待、质询参与者、审查内部信息（如系统提示或推理轨迹）或记录行为。通过逐步分析对话内容，生成最终报告指出最可能的不一致来源。

Result: Arbiter能在对话结束前有效检测出不一致行为，主动检查工具显著提升检测准确率和速度；权重诱导的不一致最难被发现，而指令诱导的不一致在被动观察下仍能可靠识别；日志工具虽提高召回率，但牺牲了精确度。

Conclusion: 持续且预算意识的监控机制可有效捕捉多代理系统中的不一致行为，监督此类系统应将审计者视为积极的参与角色。

Abstract: As AI systems built from multiple language-model agents become more common, they are increasingly used to make decisions together: discussing, negotiating, and acting on shared tasks. While individual agents may appear well-aligned when tested on their own, problems can arise from how they interact with one another. We introduce the Arbiter, an agent designed to monitor multi-agent conversations in real time and identify which participants may be behaving in misaligned ways. The Arbiter operates under a limited "inspection budget", meaning it must decide carefully how to use its resources. As it observes a conversation step by step, it can choose to wait, question a participant, examine internal information such as system prompts or reasoning traces, or log concerning behavior. At the end, it produces a report identifying the likely source of misalignment. We evaluate the Arbiter across five conversation conditions, ranging from risky financial advice model organisms to evaluation-aware and colluding agents, we test five tool configurations of increasing capability and two backbone models. We find that the Arbiter reliably detects misaligned agents well before the end of the conversation, with active inspection tools improving both detection accuracy and speed. Weight-induced misalignment proves hardest to detect, while instruction-induced misalignment is identified reliably even under passive observation. The logging tool exhibits a dual effect, improving recall at the cost of precision. These results suggest that continual, budget-aware monitoring can effectively catch misalignment, and that overseeing multi-agent systems may require treating the auditor as an active participant in the process. The code is available at https://github.com/aisilab/arbiter.

</details>


### [194] [AutoPDE: Reliable Agentic PDE Solving via Explicitly Represented Solver Strategies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10752)
*Huanshuo Dong,Keyao Zhang,Hong Wang,Zhezheng Hao,Zhiwei Zhuang,Ziyan Liu,Jiacong Wang,Gengyuan Liu,Xin Jin*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: AutoPDE is a code agent that explicitly represents and manages the solver strategy for PDEs as an independent, inspectable object before code generation. It operates in three stages: PDE analysis, numerical method selection, and adaptive tuning, using a library of reusable PDE-solving skills. This approach enables strategy revision based on numerical evidence, improving solver reliability and performance.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Current LLM-based coding agents skip explicit solver strategy design, embedding it implicitly in code. This makes it difficult to diagnose failures or revise decisions based on numerical results. AutoPDE addresses this by making the solver strategy explicit and revisable.

Method: AutoPDE constructs a solver strategy object through three stages: (1) PDE analysis to identify equation type and structure; (2) numerical method selection matching the analysis with discretization, stabilization, and solver choices; (3) adaptive tuning via low-cost pilot solves to calibrate resolution and tolerances under accuracy and runtime constraints.

Result: On the PDE Agent Bench, AutoPDE achieves a 54.5% pass rate, outperforming the strongest baseline by 14.2 percentage points.

Conclusion: By treating the solver strategy as an explicit, inspectable, and revisable entity, AutoPDE enables more robust and interpretable PDE solving, significantly improving success rates and facilitating better debugging and optimization.

Abstract: Numerical solvers for partial differential equations (PDEs) are core computational tools in science and engineering. Building reliable PDE solvers requires not only executable code, but a numerical solver strategy, a set of decisions about discretization, stabilization, solver configuration, and resolution control, that matches the PDE structure. Recent LLM-based coding agents have begun to reduce the programming burden by generating and debugging solver implementations. However, they typically move directly from a PDE problem to solver code, leaving the solver strategy implicit in implementation details. Feedback from a failed solve is therefore routed back to code edits rather than to the underlying strategy, so numerical decisions remain hard to check before code is generated and hard to revise using numerical evidence when it fails. To address this limitation, we propose AutoPDE, a code agent that maintains the solver strategy as an explicitly represented object throughout the solving process: an independent, inspectable object that is built before any code is written and can be revised, using numerical evidence, whenever a solve fails. AutoPDE builds and maintains this object in three stages, all drawing from a library of reusable PDE-solving skills: PDE analysis identifies the equation type and algebraic structure; numerical method selection chooses a numerical method that matches the analysis result and commits to a discretization, stabilization, and linear solver accordingly; and adaptive tuning runs low-cost pilot solves to calibrate resolution and tolerances under the prescribed accuracy and runtime budget. We evaluate AutoPDE on the PDE Agent Bench, where experimental results show that AutoPDE achieves a pass rate of $54.5%$, improving over the strongest baseline by $14.2$ percentage points.

</details>

### [196] [READER: Robust Evidence-based Authorship Decoding via Extracted Representations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10794)
*Jiaxu Liu,Sunnan Mu,Dong Huang,Liuyin Wang,Jing Shao,Jie Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出READER框架，通过代理模型提取隐藏的作者特征，在动态黑箱LLM溯源中实现高精度识别，显著优于传统方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着代理应用越来越多地通过官方和第三方LLM API处理用户任务，确定黑箱响应的来源模型成为关键操作问题。现有方法在非预设、查询变化的提示下表现不佳，因提示语义主导输出而模型特异性痕迹微弱且不一致。

Method: READER利用冻结的代理LLM作为隐藏作者证据的‘阅读器’，将黑箱输出映射到代理激活空间，对每个响应内的标记状态进行时间滤波，并通过贝叶斯证据累积整合独立采样提示下的单响应对数后验证据，避免了脆弱的均值池化，保留了查询级别的证据以实现校准置信度。

Result: 在Agent500数据集上，仅需一次响应时，READER达到31.0%-42.4%的top-1准确率；使用50次响应时，准确率提升至70.0%-84.0%，显著优于句子编码器指纹方法。扩展至九个代理阅读器表明，更强的LLM能揭示更线性可解的作者结构，说明作者感知已存在于冻结LLM表示中，可转化为可靠的多查询归属。

Conclusion: READER证明了在动态黑箱设置下，基于代理模型激活空间的证据提取与贝叶斯累积可实现高效、可信的多查询来源溯源，为未来模型可追溯性提供了新范式。

Abstract: As agentic applications increasingly route user tasks through official and third-party LLM APIs, provenance becomes an operational question: which model generated a given black-box response? We study Dynamic Black-Box LLM Provenance: identifying the source LLM from generations elicited by query-varying, non-predefined prompts rather than a fixed input set or benchmark suite. This setting is difficult because prompt semantics dominate the text, while model-specific authorship traces are weak and inconsistent at the surface level. We introduce READER (Robust Evidence-based Authorship Decoding via Extracted Representations), a lightweight provenance framework that treats a frozen proxy LLM as a reader of hidden authorship evidence. READER maps black-box outputs into proxy activation space, temporally filters token states within each response, and performs Bayesian Evidence Accumulation by summing single-response log-posterior evidence across independently sampled prompts. This avoids fragile mean-pooling of prompt-specific representations while preserving the query-wise evidence needed for calibrated confidence. On Agent500, a 50-target dataset built from agent-style prompts, READER reaches $31.0$-$42.4\%$ top-1 accuracy from a single response and $70.0$-$84.0\%$ from 50 responses, substantially outperforming sentence-encoder fingerprints. Scaling across nine proxy readers further shows that stronger LLMs expose more linearly decodable authorship structure, suggesting that authorship perception is already present in frozen LLM representations and can be converted into reliable multi-query attribution.

### [197] [Evaluating Research-Level Math Proofs via Strict Step-Level Verification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10799)
*Yifeng Sun*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于步骤级验证的框架，以解决大语言模型在验证复杂数学证明时因上下文污染导致的幻觉或过度怀疑问题。通过严格约束每一步推理的定理来源并维护详细上下文，该方法在对抗性诊断集上显著优于全局评估，并揭示出剩余错误多源于对领域惯例的过度严谨，而非严重逻辑错误。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在验证复杂数学证明时易受上下文污染影响，导致幻觉或过度怀疑，现有全局评估方法无法有效定位细微逻辑错误。

Method: 采用步骤级验证框架，严格控制每一步推理中定理的应用来源，并维护详细的推理上下文，实现对数学证明的精确审查。

Result: 相比全局评估，该方法能更准确地识别逻辑错误；错误类型主要为对未明说领域惯例的过度严格判断，暴露了基准数据集中的隐含模糊性。

Conclusion: 通过模仿人类数学家的谨慎推理方式，可显著提升模型区分严谨证明与错误证明的能力，为未来自动化证明评审系统提供理论基础，并增强代理在前沿数学概念上的推理能力。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) struggle to rigorously verify complex mathematical proofs. Standard global evaluation approaches suffer from "context poisoning," in which superficially plausible statements mask subtle logical flaws, leading to hallucination or over-skepticism. To address this, we shift from global evaluation to strict step-level verification: our framework maintains detailed context for each deduction step and strictly constrains the sources of applied theorems. We evaluate on a carefully curated adversarial diagnostic suite of research-level proofs drawn from the FirstProof challenge. A systematic ablation study demonstrates that these deductive constraints are indispensable, as unconstrained global prompting consistently fails to localize subtle logical errors. Beyond outperforming global evaluation, our approach fundamentally alters the failure taxonomy. Error analysis reveals that, rather than exhibiting severe logical hallucinations, remaining rejections are primarily instances of "pedantic hyper-rigor" stemming from unstated domain conventions, effectively exposing implicit ambiguities within the expert benchmark itself. Our findings suggest that prompting agents to organize their verification notes in a cautious, human-mathematician-like manner can substantially improve their ability to distinguish rigorous proofs from flawed ones, with the potential to strengthen agentic reasoning on frontier mathematical concepts that the base model does not already know well, and to lay a theoretical foundation for future automated proof-review systems. Code and prompts are available at GitHub.

### [198] [Moonshine: An Autonomous Mathematical Research Agent Centered on Conjecture Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10806)
*Xiaoyang Chen,Xiang Jiang*

Result: 成功建立了神经雅可比猜想（NJC），并对N=n+1的情形给出了独立且完整的证明；通过多模型协作获得几何拓扑视角的证明路径，提供了该猜想合理性的初步证据。然而，对于更一般的高维情形（N≥n+2），尚未取得突破。

Conclusion: Moonshine展现了自主生成深刻数学问题并推动其严谨进展的能力，标志着人工智能在数学发现领域迈出了重要一步。未来工作将聚焦于高宽度情形的解析与统一理论的构建。

Abstract: Moonshine is an autonomous agent whose central objective is to generate mathematical conjectures. Its core capability is to extract structure from classical problems, distill new concepts, and formulate conjectures of mathematical significance. Rather than treating the solution of a single proposition as its endpoint, Moonshine builds an extensible theoretical framework through conjecture generation, bridge building, and obstacle identification. This article uses Moonshine's exploration of the Jacobian conjecture as an example. It shows how the central logic of whether local nondegeneracy can force global injectivity is transferred to one-hidden-layer affine-ridge sigmoid networks. This leads to the formulation of the \emph{Neural Jacobian Conjecture} (NJC): if such a network has strictly positive Jacobian determinant on the whole space, then it must be globally injective. By invoking GPT-5.5-pro and DeepSeek-V4-pro separately, Moonshine obtained independent complete proofs for the case \(N=n+1\). In addition, with the assistance of ChatGPT through interactive use of its web interface with GPT-5.5-pro, a geometric-topological proof was developed. These results provide preliminary evidence for the plausibility of the conjecture. The general higher-width case \(N\ge n+2\), however, remains unresolved and is left for further investigation. This work illustrates Moonshine's ability to autonomously generate meaningful mathematical problems and make rigorous progress on them.

### [199] [Do VLMs Reason Like Engineers? A Benchmark and a Stage-wise Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10833)
*Syed Wasiq,Syed Mohamad Tawseeq,Yashwant Pravinrao Bangde,Debaditya Roy*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出EngVQA多模态基准，覆盖5个工程领域共696个问题；设计8阶段自动评估框架，对每个推理步骤进行独立评估，包括图示理解、原理选择、方程建立、变量识别、单位处理、计算过程、逻辑一致性及最终答案验证；结合人工评估验证框架可靠性。

Result: 多个主流开源和闭源VLM在该基准上的表现均不理想，暴露出在工程推理中的严重缺陷；自动化评估框架与人类评分高度一致（皮尔逊相关系数0.975，平均绝对误差0.67），证明其有效性；结果显示，仅评估最终答案无法揭示深层推理错误，过程导向评估至关重要。

Conclusion: 当前VLMs在工程推理方面仍存在明显不足，必须通过过程导向的评估机制来准确衡量其真实能力。EngVQA和8阶段评估框架为未来研究提供了重要工具，有助于推动更具物理一致性和可解释性的工程辅助AI系统的发展。

Abstract: Vision-Language Models (VLMs) demonstrate strong performance on general multimodal reasoning benchmarks, yet their ability to perform engineering reasoning remains largely unexplored. Unlike general visual question answering, engineering problem solving requires interpreting technical diagrams, selecting governing physical principles, and maintaining physically consistent multi-step reasoning. These capabilities are increasingly important for AI systems used in engineering education, scientific assistance, and technical decision-making, where reasoning failures may produce physically invalid yet superficially plausible solutions. Existing benchmarks primarily evaluate final answers and provide limited assessment of intermediate reasoning processes. We introduce EngVQA, a multimodal benchmark for evaluating engineering reasoning across 5 engineering subjects containing 696 problems. We introduce an 8-stage automatic evaluation framework for assessing VLM-generated solutions. The framework independently evaluates each stage of the solution, enabling fine-grained analysis of reasoning failures. We benchmark multiple state-of-the-art open and closed source VLMs on our evaluation framework and demonstrate substantial limitations in current engineering reasoning capabilities. Human evaluation shows strong agreement with our automated framework, achieving a Pearson correlation of 0.975 and a mean absolute error of 0.67 on a 10-point grading scale. Our results highlight the importance of process-oriented evaluation for reliable assessment of multimodal engineering reasoning systems.

### [200] [Large-scale semantic mapping of learner agency and autonomy reveals what measurement and generative AI research overlook](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10881)
*Fei Qin,Xiaobo Liu,Yaowen Zhang,Xuming Li,Fei Wang,Mutlu Cukurova,Jingjing Chen,Yu Zhang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用语义分析管道，从大量学术文献中提取定义与量表条目，基于语言使用实践分析概念的实际内涵，并识别其核心维度。

Result: 发现学习者自主性与能动性可归纳为三个维度：任务层面的调控与控制、个人层面的内在动机与决策、社会文化层面的互动行为；但现有测量工具普遍忽略社会文化维度，且生成式AI研究也集中于前两个维度。

Conclusion: 必须重新审视和重构学习者自主性与能动性的概念框架，确保在测量与教育技术设计中充分涵盖其多维特性，以真正支持学习者的全面发展。

Abstract: Learner agency and autonomy are foundational to personal development, yet a pervasive "jingle-jangle" fallacy (i.e. identical terms denoting different constructs, distinct terms denoting identical ones) has substantially hindered cumulative knowledge. Treating meaning as a phenomenon constituted through use in linguistic practice, we extracted 8,954 definitions and 2,700 scale items from over 14,000 publications, to investigate how researchers actually used learner agency and autonomy with a semantic analysis pipeline. The definitional landscape of two constructs resolves into three dimensions: regulation and control of learning (task), intrinsic motivation and internal decision-making (person), and social-relational action (sociocultural), thereby empirically quantifying the jingle-jangle fallacy. Existing scales, however, systematically underrepresent the sociocultural dimension. Critically, current generative AI research in education concentrates on learning regulation and control, narrowing the behavioral repertoire that AI-mediated learning environments are designed to cultivate. Beyond conceptual clarification, this work carries direct implications for conceptualization, measurement, and practice towards supporting the multidimensional learner agency and autonomy.

### [201] [Role-Agent: Bootstrapping LLM Agents via Dual-Role Evolution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10917)
*Xucong Wang,Ziyu Ma,Shidong Yang,Tongwen Huang,Pengkun Wang,Yong Wang,Xiangxiang Chu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: Role-Agent 是一种利用单一大语言模型同时充当智能体和环境的框架，通过自举式协同进化提升学习效率。其包含两个核心组件：世界在智能体（WIA）中，模型预测动作后的未来状态并以预测与实际状态的一致性作为过程奖励，促进环境感知推理；智能体在世界（AIW）中，分析失败轨迹并检索具有相似失败模式的任务，重构训练数据分布以实现针对性练习。实验表明，该方法在多个基准测试上均显著优于基线，平均性能提升超过4%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大语言模型智能体的学习受限于低效的交互反馈和静态训练环境，导致泛化能力不足，亟需更高效的自适应学习机制。

Method: 提出 Role-Agent 框架，利用单一 LLM 同时担任智能体和环境角色，通过 WIA 和 AIW 两个组件实现自举式协同进化：WIA 基于状态预测与实际状态的对齐提供过程奖励；AIW 通过失败模式分析与任务重采样优化训练数据分布。

Result: 在多个基准测试中，Role-Agent 显著提升智能体性能，平均优于强基线超过4%，验证了其在复杂任务中的有效性与泛化能力。

Conclusion: Role-Agent 通过将智能体与环境统一于同一 LLM 中，实现了高效的自举式协同进化，有效克服了传统训练中反馈效率低和环境静态的问题，为大语言模型智能体的高效学习提供了新范式。

Abstract: Although Large Language Model (LLM) agents have demonstrated strong performance on complex tasks, their learning is often limited by inefficient interaction feedback and static training environments, which hinder broader generalization. To address these limitations, this paper introduces Role-Agent, \textcolor{black}{a framework} that harnesses a single LLM to function concurrently as both the agent and the environment, enabling a bootstrapped co-evolution. Role-Agent comprises two synergistic components: World-In-Agent (WIA) and Agent-In-World (AIW). In WIA, the LLM acts as the agent and predicts future states after each action; the alignment between predicted and actual states is then used as a process reward, encouraging environment-aware reasoning. In AIW, the LLM analyzes failure modes from failed trajectories and retrieves tasks with similar failure patterns, thereby reshaping the training data distribution for targeted practice. Experiments on multiple benchmarks show that Role-Agent consistently improves performance, yielding an average gain of over 4\% over strong baselines.
