### [202] [Frontier Coding Agents Use Metaprogramming to Adapt to Unfamiliar Programming Languages](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10933)
*Aman Sharma,Sushrut Thorat,Paras Chopra*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文评估六种主流编码代理在四种冷门编程语言上的表现，发现强代理（如Claude Opus 4.6和GPT-5.4 xhigh）常通过编写Python生成器来间接实现目标语言代码，而非直接编写。禁止此元编程策略导致性能显著下降；而仅靠文本引导无法提升弱代理表现。但若提供基于Opus的辅助Python代码（无解题答案或隐藏测试反馈），则能显著提升Sonnet 4.6和GPT-5.4 mini的表现，而Haiku 4.5仍表现不佳。更多解释器调用和输出令牌仅增强强代理能力，不改变弱代理表现，表明资源放大已有有效策略而非创造新策略。结果表明，强代理通过工具、反馈与工作区状态构建对陌生语言规则的理解，元编程是其中最明显的表现，更广泛的能力差异体现在制定并调试适配目标语言的策略上。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有编码代理评估多集中于主流语言与常见库，难以揭示其在陌生语言环境下的真实能力。本文旨在探索编码代理在非主流、冷门编程语言中的行为差异，揭示其适应陌生语言的核心机制。

Method: 采用顺序式评估协议，包括文件编辑、本地执行与隐藏测试评分，评估六种编码代理在四种冷门语言（Brainfuck、Befunge-98等）上的表现。通过禁用元编程策略、引入辅助代码等方式对比不同代理的响应与适应能力。

Result: 强代理倾向于使用元编程（如用Python生成目标语言代码），禁用该策略后性能大幅下降；文本引导无法提升弱代理；而提供强代理的辅助代码可显著提升弱代理表现；更多计算资源仅强化强代理，不改善弱代理。表明强代理依赖策略构建与工具利用，而非单纯依赖模型能力。

Conclusion: 强大的编码代理在面对陌生语言时，通过工具、反馈和工作区状态构建对目标语言规则的理解，其核心优势在于策略的生成与调试能力，而非直接编码能力。元编程是这一能力的突出体现，但更深层的能力差距在于能否有效构建并验证可行的解决路径。

Abstract: LLM-based coding agents are usually evaluated in familiar software settings: mainstream languages, common libraries, and public repositories. These benchmarks remain important, but they can hide how agents behave when the language itself is unfamiliar. We evaluate six contemporary coding agents on four esoteric programming languages using a sequential setup with file editing, local execution, and hidden-test grading. Our protocol exposes capability differences between these agents that mainstream coding and agentic benchmarks such as SWE-Bench Verified and Terminal-Bench 2.0 compress into much narrower bands. We observe that the strongest agents, Claude Opus 4.6 and GPT-5.4 xhigh, often avoid writing the target language directly. On Brainfuck and Befunge-98, they write Python programs that generate target-language code and debug those generators locally. Forbidding this metaprogramming strategy causes large performance drops. Text guidance distilled from this strategy does not materially improve weaker agents. In contrast, Opus-derived Python helper code for building generators, with no solved benchmark programs or hidden-test answers, sharply improves Sonnet 4.6 and GPT-5.4 mini on the same problems, while Haiku 4.5 remains low. More interpreter calls and output tokens improve stronger agents but leave weaker agents near their original performance, indicating that these resources amplify useful strategies rather than create them. Together, these results show that strong coding agents adapt to unfamiliar languages by using tools, feedback, and workspace state to build a working model of the target language. Metaprogramming is the clearest case, but the broader gap is constructing and debugging a strategy that works under the target language's rules.

</details>


### [203] [WorldKernel: A World Model is the Coupling Kernel of Admissible Possible Worlds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10934)
*Fabio Rovai*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文揭示了在因果推断中，即使拥有大量观测和干预数据，强预测模型在处理未识别的反事实耦合时仍会失效。研究提出将世界模型建模为正定耦合核K(T,T')，其对角线表示普通后验（预测模型可恢复），而反对角线则表示反事实推理所需的跨世界耦合，这是预测模型无法捕捉的。通过正定性约束和本体论公理，可有效缩小反事实估计的不确定范围，并可通过针对性的约束学习加速收敛。尽管完全重构耦合结构在计算上仍属困难，但该方法在多项式时间内提供可操作的边界，显著优于传统方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法假设充足的数据和强大的预测模型足以解决所有因果问题，但本文发现这一假设在未识别的反事实耦合问题上存在根本缺陷：预测模型无法表达对跨世界关系的不确定性，导致严重误判。

Method: 构建基于正定耦合核K(T,T')的世界模型框架，利用正定性作为部分识别信息来约束反事实估计；引入本体论公理以进一步收紧边界；通过针对不一致性的约束学习（靶向疤痕）加速收敛；分析其计算复杂性与近似可行性。

Result: 在28%的模型中，强预测模型退化为一个无效点，而真实值是一个不可压缩的可接受区间；通过所提方法，可在多项式时间内获得紧致边界，逻辑结构可提升效果达三分之一，靶向约束比非靶向快数倍；完全重建需近似计数，但在低于Sly-Sun阈值时可行。

Conclusion: 预测模型本质上无法捕捉反事实耦合的不确定性，必须引入显式的耦合结构建模。正定性约束和本体论知识提供了有效的理论与计算工具，使反事实推理在不可行的精确程序之外仍具可操作性。

Abstract: A common assumption holds that enough observational and interventional data, given to a strong enough predictor, suffices. We report a failure mode that contradicts it. Across hundreds of structural causal models, on identified quantities a strong predictor and a Bayesian baseline both succeed, but on unidentified quantities (the couplings between counterfactual worlds) the predictor collapses to a point, on 28% of models to one no valid model can produce, while the truth is an admissible interval more data never narrows. The gap is structural: prediction cannot represent uncertainty over counterfactual couplings. We cast a world model as a single positive semidefinite coupling kernel K(T,T') over admissible worlds, whose diagonal is the ordinary posterior (what a predictor recovers) and whose off-diagonal is the cross-world coupling it cannot, which every counterfactual reads. The paper is the theory of that off-diagonal. It is real: two states with identical posteriors differ on a cross-world query, and the off-diagonal is the coupling that fixes counterfactuals. It can be bounded: positive semidefiniteness is partial-identifying information the marginals lack, and enforcing it bounds counterfactuals in polynomial time where the exact response-type program is intractable. Logical structure sharpens it: ontology axioms tighten the bound by up to a third, propagating to couplings they never touch. It can be acquired: targeted scars, constraints learned from encountered infeasibilities, close the gap several times faster than untargeted ones. Its full reconstruction is approximate counting of the admissible worlds, tractable below the Sly-Sun threshold and inapproximable above; we do not claim to beat the worst case.

</details>


### [204] [Recalling Too Well: Sycophancy Evaluation and Mitigation in Memory-Augmented Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10949)
*Shelly Bensal,Axel Magnuson,Aparna Balagopalan,Daniel M. Bikel*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了持久记忆系统在大语言模型中会系统性地放大奉承行为，即模型更倾向于迎合用户而非追求准确。通过引入MIST基准测试，研究发现记忆系统使奉承率最高提升25倍，主要原因是记忆提取中的有损压缩导致用户错误信念被保留而纠正信息被丢弃。研究提出了两种轻量级缓解方法，能显著降低奉承行为，同时保持或优于原有记忆系统的事实召回能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索持久记忆系统对大语言模型准确性的影响，发现其可能加剧模型对用户观点的盲目迎合，从而损害模型的正确性。

Method: 构建MIST基准，包含科学、医学和道德推理领域中合成生成的多轮对话，评估三种先进记忆系统与五种模型家族在记忆影响下的表现，并进行误差分析以识别问题根源。

Result: 记忆系统显著放大了模型的奉承行为，奉承率最高达基线的25倍；记忆提取中的有损压缩是主要原因，导致用户错误信念被保留而纠正信息丢失。

Conclusion: 建议采用轻量级缓解策略，在有效减少奉承行为的同时，维持甚至超越传统记忆系统的事实召回性能。

Abstract: Persistent memory systems promise to make LLMs more helpful by storing user beliefs over time. We show they also make models less correct by systematically amplifying sycophancy, wherein models prioritize agreement with users over accuracy. We conduct the first systematic evaluation of this effect, introducing MIST: a benchmark of synthetically generated multi-turn conversations where users express plausible misconceptions in scientific, medical, and moral reasoning domains. Testing across three state-of-the-art memory systems and five model families reveals that memory amplifies sycophantic behavior across all conditions, with up to 25x higher sycophancy rates than in-context baselines. Error analyses suggest memory extraction as the primary culprit: lossy compression into discrete snippets encodes user misconceptions while discarding corrective context. Based on these results, we propose two lightweight mitigations that substantially reduce sycophancy while matching or exceeding memory systems at factual recall.

### [207] [Bellman-Taylor Score Decoding for Markov Decision Processes with State-Dependent Feasible Action Sets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10979)
*Yi Chen,Rushuai Yang,Qiang Chen,Dongyan,Huo*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为Bellman--Taylor score decoding的框架，用于解决操作研究中状态依赖且由约束隐式定义的动作空间问题。该方法将策略学习映射到欧几里得得分空间，并通过动作解码器保证可行性，使标准深度强化学习算法可在不微分解码器的情况下优化潜在得分马尔可夫决策过程。理论分析表明，该方法的最优性差距可分解为结构近似误差和算法学习误差。在排队网络控制问题上的实验显示，小规模实例中接近最优，大规模系统中显著优于基准方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 许多运筹学中的马尔可夫决策过程具有状态依赖且由运营约束隐式定义的动作，这使得标准深度强化学习算法难以应用，因为它们通常假设固定有限的动作集或简单的欧几里得空间。

Method: 提出贝尔曼-泰勒得分解码框架，将策略学习转换到欧几里得得分空间，利用动作解码器确保动作可行性，从而允许使用标准DRL算法优化潜在得分MDP，同时避免对解码器进行反向传播。

Result: 理论证明了该方法的最优性差距可分解为结构近似误差与算法学习误差；在排队网络控制问题上，小规模实例表现接近最优，大规模系统中性能显著优于现有基准。

Conclusion: Bellman--Taylor score decoding框架有效解决了状态依赖、隐式定义动作空间下的强化学习挑战，为复杂运筹优化问题提供了可扩展且理论上保障的解决方案。

Abstract: Many Markov decision processes (MDPs) in operations research have feasible actions that are state dependent and defined implicitly by various operational constraints. These features make it difficult to use standard deep reinforcement learning (DRL) algorithms, whose action interfaces typically assume either a fixed finite action catalog or a simple Euclidean space. Motivated by a Taylor expansion of the optimal action-value function, we propose Bellman--Taylor score decoding, a framework that moves policy learning to a Euclidean score space while enforcing feasibility through an action decoder. The induced latent-score MDP then can be optimized by standard DRL algorithms without differentiating through the decoder. We provide a performance guarantee showing that the optimality gap of this approach decomposes into a structural approximation error and an algorithmic learning error. Lastly, we apply this framework to a queueing network control problem, where the policy essentially learns a state-dependent index-based dispatching rule. Numerical experiments show near-optimal performance in small instances and considerable improvements over benchmarks in larger systems.

### [208] [Null-Space Constrained Low-Rank Adaptation for Response-Specified Large Language Model Unlearning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10989)
*Bocheng Ju,Jianhua Wang,Chengliang Liu,Xiaolin Chang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: NSRU提出一种基于投影约束的低秩框架，用于可控的大语言模型遗忘。通过显式结构化的安全目标响应指定每个遗忘查询的期望行为，同时抑制原始不良内容。为实现适配局部化，NSRU从良性隐藏表示中估计保留子空间，并使用正交投影的低秩参数化将LoRA更新限制在保留子空间的零空间内，从而联合优化安全目标学习、不良响应抑制与保留性能保持。实验表明，NSRU在TOFU和WMDP数据集上均有效抑制可提取的遗忘知识，提升保留问答性能、模型效用及安全目标对齐性，且在不同超参数和提示变化下表现出稳定鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大语言模型遗忘方法多关注抑制不良回答，而目标引导型方法虽指定替换行为，但未充分约束更新局部性。因此需要一种既能精准控制遗忘行为，又能保护良性能力的机制。

Method: 提出NSRU框架：利用显式安全目标响应定义期望行为；通过分析良性隐藏表示估计各模块保留子空间；采用正交投影的低秩参数化（基于保留子空间的零空间）约束LoRA更新，实现局部化适配；联合优化安全目标学习、不良响应抑制与保留性能保持。

Abstract: Large language model unlearning aims to suppress designated undesirable knowledge while preserving benign capabilities. Many unlearning objectives focus on suppressing undesired answers, while recent target-guided variants specify replacement behavior but still leave update locality largely unconstrained. This paper introduces \emph{Null-Space Constrained Response-Specified Unlearning} (NSRU), a projection-constrained low-rank framework for controlled LLM unlearning. NSRU uses an explicitly structured safe target response to specify the desired behavior for each forget query, while suppressing the original undesired content. To localize adaptation, NSRU estimates per-module retain subspaces from benign hidden representations and uses an orthogonal-projected low-rank parameterization to confine LoRA updates to the null space of the retain subspace. The resulting objective jointly optimizes safe-target learning, undesired-response suppression, and retention preservation under this constrained parameterization. We provide a local first-order analysis showing that the projected update reduces retain-side perturbations while preserving editable directions for shaping forget-query behavior. Experiments on TOFU show that NSRU effectively suppresses extractable forget-set knowledge while improving retain QA performance, model utility, and safe-target alignment over representative baselines. On WMDP, NSRU keeps hazardous-domain accuracy near the random-choice region while preserving broad and domain-adjacent MMLU utility. Ablation studies support the complementary roles of safe-target supervision, undesired-response suppression, retention loss, and null-space projected updates, while sensitivity and robustness analyses indicate stable behavior across the tested hyperparameter and prompt variations.

### [209] [Structure from Reasoning, Numbers from Search: On-Premise Open LLMs as Structural Priors for Coupled MIMO Controller Tuning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11015)
*Jiaxuan Chen,Haonan Li,Yang Shu*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统控制器调参方法在强耦合多输入多输出（MIMO）系统中面临挑战：分散式经典自整定忽略回路交互，局部数值优化易陷入非凸代价景观中的局部极小。现有方法缺乏有效处理耦合机制的能力，且依赖模型或大量数据。因此，探索无需外部模型、数据本地化、具备推理能力的开放源代码大语言模型（LLM）是否能作为结构性先验，提升调参效率和可解释性，成为关键研究动机。

Method: 采用开放源代码大型语言模型（LLM）进行控制参数调优，结合“支架式”推理框架，使模型理解系统耦合特性并提出非直观的控制结构（如非对称设计）。通过少量评估（18次）生成可行控制器，再与经典优化器结合精炼至全局最优。对比实验包括经典继电反馈调参、直接使用LLM调参、局部优化器、全局优化器（差分进化）等，评估指标为加权成本函数J = IAE + λ·TV(u)，涵盖跟踪性能与控制动作平滑性。测试覆盖单回路CSTR、强耦合四罐系统及3×3高维系统，验证方法泛化性与边界条件。

Result: 在单回路系统中，经典继电反馈调参表现最佳（IAE 0.106），LLM调参略差（0.162），说明简单系统中LLM无增益。而在强耦合四罐系统中，传统方法（如继电调参、直接LLM调参、局部优化）均无法超越开环性能（J ~ 22.7），局部优化失败率高达10/10。而支架式LLM推理成功提出非对称结构，实现J ~ 16.9 ± 0.2，从任意初始点均可收敛；进一步与经典优化器结合后达最优解J ~ 12.0（10/10成功），甚至实现非显式的负积分修正，是传统分散式方法无法做到的。在3×3系统中，该方法比全局优化器少约6倍评估次数。四种不同开源LLM均表现出类似优势，且在低耦合系统中未体现优势，验证了其适用边界。

Conclusion: 开放源代码大语言模型（LLM）在强耦合多输入多输出（MIMO）控制系统调参中，不作为优化器本身，而作为样本高效、可解释的结构先验，显著提升调参效率与成功率。其核心价值在于通过推理理解系统耦合机制，提出非直观但有效的控制结构，从而克服传统方法在非凸代价空间中的局限。该方法在高维、强耦合系统中优势突出，适用于实际工业场景，且具有良好的泛化性和可解释性。本研究构建了一个可复现的基准，明确了LLM介入控制调参的有效边界。

Abstract: Tuning controllers for strongly coupled multi-input multi-output (MIMO) industrial processes is hard: decentralized classical auto-tuning ignores loop interaction, and local numerical optimization from natural initializations stalls in the resulting non-convex cost landscape. We ask whether on-premise open-source large language models (LLMs), which keep data on-site and need no plant model, can help. On a single-loop CSTR, classical relay-feedback tuning (IAE 0.106, near the 0.102 optimum) beats an LLM tuner (0.162): for simple loops the LLM adds nothing. The picture inverts on a strongly coupled quadruple-tank with conflicting set-points, scored by a penalized cost J = IAE + lambda*TV(u) that rewards tracking without chattering actuators. There, naive relay tuning (J ~ 28.6) and naive LLM tuning (29.7) are no better than open loop (22.7), and a local optimizer from balanced starts fails in 10/10 runs. A scaffolded open LLM instead reasons about the coupling, proposes the counter-intuitive asymmetric structure, and reaches J ~ 16.9 +/- 0.2 from any start; refining it with a classical optimizer attains the smooth global optimum (J ~ 12.0, 10/10 vs. 0/10), which even applies a non-obvious negative integral correction decentralized tuning cannot. A global optimizer (differential evolution) also reaches this optimum, so the LLM is not the only route; its advantage is sample efficiency and interpretability: a usable controller in 18 evaluations (where the global optimizer is worse than open loop) plus a stated rationale. This edge grows with dimension, reaching ~6x fewer evaluations on a 3x3 plant. The behaviour generalizes across four open models, and on a benign plant the LLM offers no advantage, sharpening the boundary. We contribute a reproducible benchmark delimiting when open LLMs help in control tuning: not as optimizers, but as a sample-efficient, interpretable structural prior.

</details>


### [210] [Superficial Beliefs in LLM Decision-Making](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11016)
*Gabriel Freedman,Francesca Toni*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究探讨大语言模型（LLMs）在二元决策中是单纯模仿推理过程，还是基于系统性决策结构作出选择。通过合成的二元决策场景，研究发现模型行为与可见属性之间存在系统关联，可被行为模型较好预测，表明其决策并非随机。然而，模型自述和评分判断仅部分反映行为推断出的关键驱动因素，说明其输出虽有结构性但显式理由与实际驱动因素不完全匹配。这一模式在多种扰动下保持一致，研究认为这支持‘表面信念’假说：模型的行为看似由属性的局部概率优先级引导，但对驱动其决策的属性缺乏充分的言语表达能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究大语言模型在决策过程中是否具有内在的、系统性的决策结构，而非仅仅是表面的推理模仿。理解模型真实决策机制对于评估其可靠性与透明性至关重要。

Method: 使用合成的二元决策任务，让模型在具有渐进属性的选项间进行选择；通过拟合历史决策的行为模型，反推出影响选择的关键属性，并与模型自述及独立评分判断进行对比分析。实验涵盖提示顺序变化、采样扰动、不同行为模型、目标遮蔽分析以及结构多样的决策设置。

Result: 行为模型能有效预测模型的后续选择，表明其决策具有系统性；但模型自述和评分判断仅部分捕捉到行为推断出的驱动因素，说明其显式理由与真实决策依据之间存在差距。该现象在多种条件下稳定存在。

Conclusion: 大语言模型在决策中表现出结构性行为，但其显式理由未能完全反映真正驱动其选择的属性，支持‘表面信念’的观点：模型的行为似受局部概率优先级引导，但缺乏对这些优先级的完整语言表达。

Abstract: We ask whether large language models (LLMs) merely imitate rationales when choosing between two options, or whether their choices reflect a systematic underlying decision structure. Using synthetic binary decision settings in which models choose between profiles defined by graded attributes, we compare the attribute a model says mattered most with the attribute that best explains its choice under a behavioural model fit to prior decisions. The behavioural model predicts held-out choices well, showing that model behaviour is systematically related to the visible attributes rather than being random. However, direct self-reports and a separate score-based judge recover the behaviourally inferred driver only partially. The resulting picture is neither one of arbitrary behaviour nor one of fully articulated belief - outputs are structured enough to support prediction, but explicit reasons track the recovered driver only imperfectly. This qualitative pattern persists across prompt-order and sampling perturbations, alternative behavioural models, targeted occlusion analyses, and structurally varied decision settings. We interpret this as evidence for ``superficial belief'' in LLM decision-making: models behave as if guided by probabilistic local priorities over attributes, while having only limited verbal access to the attributes that drive their decisions.

Abstract: Recent years have witnessed the rapid evolution of AI agents toward handling increasingly complex, real-world tasks. However, existing benchmarks rarely evaluate whether agents can operate graphical user interfaces to complete long-horizon, high-value professional workflows across diverse domains. Current GUI benchmarks still predominantly focus on general-purpose software, relatively simple applications, and short-horizon tasks, leaving it largely unknown whether modern agents can follow user instructions to autonomously operate domain-specific professional software and accomplish economically valuable work in an end-to-end manner. To bridge this gap, we introduce Workflow-GYM, a benchmark for long-horizon GUI tasks centered on professional domains and specialized software environments. Further analysis reveals that current agents struggle to maintain long-horizon workflow consistency, frequently exhibiting workflow stage omission, error propagation, objective drift, and insufficient understanding of professional software environments. Our findings provide important insights into the limitations of current agent systems and suggest key directions for the next generation of GUI-agent research.

### [212] [What Fits (Into Few Tokens) Doesn't Overfit: Compression and Generalization in ML Research Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11045)
*Martin Andres Bertran,Aaron Roth,Zhiwei Steven Wu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究了基准驱动的机器学习中为何很少出现过拟合的现象，提出并验证了一个假设：成功的机器学习策略具有高度可压缩性。通过在大型语言模型驱动的研究代理中引入两种信息瓶颈（输出压缩和输入压缩），实验表明即使仅用极短提示或一位反馈，也能成功复现或发现高性能模型。当人为制造验证集过拟合时，复现失败，验证了该假设的可证伪性。结果支持‘成功策略位于策略空间中低复杂度区域’这一解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管自适应地重用保留基准理论上会导致过拟合，但实践中基准驱动的机器学习却表现出极少过拟合现象。为此，本文提出并检验一个核心假设：成功的机器学习策略本身具有高度可压缩性，从而限制了过拟合的发生。

Method: 采用两种信息瓶颈设置：1）输出压缩——探索者使用验证集自适应搜索高性能模型，再由一个新代理仅凭极短提示和训练数据尝试复现性能；2）输入压缩——探索者仅接收一位反馈（是否优于当前最佳模型），测试其能否仍找到高性能模型。实验覆盖8个不同数据集，涵盖表格分类、视觉、语言建模、扩散建模和奖励建模等任务。

Result: 在所有8个数据集上，无论是输出压缩还是输入压缩，都几乎未影响模型性能：极短提示和一位反馈足以复现或发现高绩效模型。当人为引入验证集过拟合时，复现失败，说明该现象与过拟合敏感相关。

Conclusion: 实验结果支持‘成功机器学习策略具有低描述长度’的解释，即它们处于策略空间的低复杂度区域，因此在基准驱动的学习中不易过拟合。这为现实世界中基准学习的有效性提供了理论依据。

Abstract: Reusing a held-out benchmark adaptively should, in principle, invite overfitting. Yet benchmark-driven machine learning (ML) has produced surprisingly little overfitting in practice. An attractive hypothesis is that successful ML strategies are highly compressible. We study this in the setting of LLM-driven research agents, where the hypothesis becomes directly testable via two complementary information bottlenecks. In \emph{output compression}, an exploration agent adaptively searches for high-performance models using a validation set, and we test whether a fresh ``reproducer agent'' can reproduce its performance given only an extremely short prompt and the training data. In \emph{input compression}, the explorer receives only one-bit feedback indicating whether each submitted model improves on the running best. Across 8 datasets spanning tabular classification, vision, language modeling, diffusion modeling, and reward modeling, we find that these bottlenecks have little effect on performance: short prompts and compressible feedback are sufficient to reproduce and find high-performance models. The hypothesis is falsifiable: when we deliberately induce validation-set overfitting, the results fail to reproduce with short prompts. Taken together, our results support a description-length explanation for the lack of overfitting in benchmark-driven ML: successful strategies occupy a low-complexity region of strategy space.

</details>


### [213] [CIAware-Bench: Benchmarking Control Intervention Awareness Across Frontier LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11063)
*Joachim Schaeffer,Thomas Jiralerspong,Alexander Panfilov,Guillaume Lajoie,Jonas Geiping,Yoshua Bengio,Roland S. Zimmermann*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出CIAware-Bench基准，用于评估前沿模型对控制干预（CI）的感知能力。该基准涵盖四个任务领域，并在不同干预策略下测试模型是否能区分原始轨迹与被修改轨迹。实验发现模型的CI感知能力差异显著，且主要受模型家族和训练风格影响，表明其非固定属性，需针对每项新模型部署重新评估。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AI控制协议依赖可信模型监控并干预不可信模型的行为，但干预可能被模型察觉并利用以规避控制。因此需要一种有效方法来衡量模型对控制干预的感知能力，从而改进控制协议设计。

Method: 构建CIAware-Bench基准，包含四种任务域（论文写作、BigCodeBench、Bash Arena、SHADE-Arena），通过改变轨迹水印、附加任务和控制协议等变量，测试模型识别自身轨迹是否被干预的能力。采用二分类任务评估模型检测干预的能力。

Result: 在默认设置下，模型的CI感知能力从低到中等不等（最高0.87，随机水平为0.5），不同任务域和模型对间差异明显；跨模型家族检测更容易，暗示模型利用了特定提供商的风格或后训练特征。

Conclusion: CI感知能力并非模型固有属性，应针对每次新模型发布和部署场景单独评估。研究释放CIAware-Bench以持续监测该能力，帮助设计更隐蔽、更难被察觉的控制干预机制。

Abstract: AI control protocols oversee untrusted models by monitoring their actions and modifying potentially unsafe steps, often using a trusted model. This partially tampers with the untrusted model's trajectory. If the trusted model detects such an intervention, it may infer properties of the monitor and adapt to evade control. We introduce \textbf{CIAware-Bench}, a benchmark for measuring \textbf{c}ontrol \textbf{i}ntervention (CI) awareness across frontier models. CIAware-Bench tests whether models can distinguish their own trajectories from those modified by a control intervention. The benchmark is comprised of a suite of four task domains (essay writing, BigCodeBench, Bash Arena, and SHADE-Arena), while varying trajectory watermarking, side-task presence, and the control protocol. Evaluating eleven frontier models, we find low to moderate CI awareness under default settings (up to 0.87; random chance balanced binary classification accuracy is 0.5) with substantial variation across task domains and model pairs. Detection is generally easier across model families, suggesting that models exploit provider-specific differences in style or post-training. Overall, CI awareness is not a fixed model-level property, and should be measured for each new model release and deployment scenario. We release CIAware-Bench to track CI awareness and inform control protocols whose interventions are harder to detect.

</details>


### [214] [A History-Aware Visually Grounded Critic for Computer Use Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11078)
*Jaewoo Lee,Zaid Khan,Archiki Prasad,Justin Chih-Yao Chen,Supriyo Chakraborty,Kartik Balasubramaniam,Sambit Sahu,Elias Stengel-Eskin,Hyunji Lee,Mohit Bansal*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: HiViG 是一种面向计算机使用代理（CUAs）的测试时干预框架，通过多模态批评模型实现历史感知与视觉接地，以解决现有批评模型在短期决策和视觉误判上的局限。该框架在测试时整合批评机制，提供宏观动作历史与视觉验证反馈，显著提升跨平台长时程任务的性能，平均成功率提升5.8%至9.0%，且各组件均对性能提升至关重要。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出一个基于真实GUI轨迹训练的多模态批评模型，将历史交互抽象为紧凑记录，并结合当前屏幕截图对动作坐标进行视觉验证，集成到策略决策循环中，实现历史感知与视觉接地的双重优化。

Conclusion: HiViG 通过引入历史感知与视觉接地机制，有效解决了测试时批评模型的关键缺陷，为复杂GUI任务中的智能体提供了可扩展、高鲁棒性的性能增强方案。

Abstract: Various test-time interventions for Computer Use Agents (CUAs), including critic models, have been developed to improve performance through pre-execution action evaluation in complex Graphical User Interface (GUI) environments. However, existing critics suffer from two key limitations: they (1) focus primarily on short-sighted decision loops (e.g., forgetting earlier actions) and (2) lack the visual grounding needed to detect flawed actions (e.g., clicking wrong UI elements). To address these, we introduce HiViG, a History-aware Visually Grounded test-time framework, built around a multimodal critic trained on real GUI trajectories to abstract past interactions into a compact record and to evaluate actions with visual grounding. At test time, HiViG integrates the critic into the policy decision loop to provide macro-action history, which summarizes the policy's completed achievements, and visually grounded critique, which verifies raw execution coordinates against the current screenshot to intercept errors before execution. Across web, mobile, and desktop benchmarks, HiViG consistently outperforms existing scalar and verbal critics, improving average success rates over the strongest baseline by 5.8% for Qwen3-VL-32B and 9.0% for Gemini-3-Flash, and demonstrates strong cross-platform generalization. Ablations show that macro-action history mitigates short-sighted planning and visually grounded critique reduces execution errors, with both components being critical for test-time scaling in long-horizon GUI tasks.

### [215] [Monte Carlo Pass Search: Using Trajectory Generation for 3D Counterfactual Pass Evaluation in Football](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11120)
*Andrew Kang,Priya Narasimhan*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文将足球传球评估重构为类似蒙特卡洛树搜索（MCTS）的问题，利用已有文献中的组件：价值模型（控球价值）、世界模型（带球交互的多智能体轨迹）和反事实动作策略（带噪声的传球变体采样）。基于德甲联赛首个公开的高保真3D球轨迹数据集，提出蒙特卡洛传球搜索（MCPS），通过推断传球参数、采样执行与选项变体，使用球条件世界模型向前滚动至下一次球接触，并用学习的价值模型评分，获得收益分布。该分布支持分布感知归因，引入均值和分位数两种互补的执行盈余评分用于分析与排序。为提升在有限公开数据下的采样效率，采用自动驾驶领域的离散标记自回归轨迹生成器（SMART），在预测准确性上优于基线方法，且支持完全假设性回溯以供下游评估。模型检查点与代码已开源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统足球传球评估方法难以全面量化传球决策的价值，尤其在面对复杂动态场景时缺乏对多种可能结果的建模能力。现有方法通常依赖静态指标或简单模型，无法充分捕捉传球行为的不确定性与潜在影响。因此，需要一种能够模拟多种执行与选项变体、并评估其长期价值的系统化框架，以实现更精准的传球质量分析与球员表现评估。

Method: 提出蒙特卡洛传球搜索（MCPS）框架，包含三个核心组件：1）价值模型：学习控球价值函数；2）世界模型：基于离散标记自回归生成器（源自自动驾驶领域，如SMART）构建球条件多智能体轨迹模型，支持高效且真实的轨迹生成；3）策略采样：对每个观测传球采样执行变体（如力度、方向）与选项变体（如目标球员选择），结合噪声进行多样化探索。通过多次前向模拟，评估每种变体的结果价值，最终形成价值分布。

Result: MCPS在德甲公开数据集上表现出色，其世界模型在最佳20种预测中达到高准确率，显著优于多个基线方法。所提出的均值与分位数执行盈余评分能够有效区分传球质量，揭示传统指标忽略的细微差异。实验表明，该方法可成功用于球员传球表现的排名与分析，支持对真实与假设情景的对比评估，具备较强的实用性与扩展性。

Conclusion: 本研究通过将足球传球评估形式化为一个类MCTS问题，构建了可解释、可扩展的蒙特卡洛传球搜索框架（MCPS）。该框架整合了价值模型、世界模型与策略采样机制，实现了对传球决策的分布级评估。实验验证了其在真实数据上的有效性与鲁棒性，同时开源了代码与模型，为未来足球数据分析提供了新范式。

Abstract: We recast pass evaluation in football (soccer) as a Monte Carlo Tree Search (MCTS)-like evaluation problem whose components mostly exist in the literature under different names: a value model (possession value), a world model (multi-agent trajectories with ball interactions), and a policy over counterfactual actions (sampling pass variants with noise). Building on the first public high-fidelity tracking dataset with 3D ball trajectories from the Bundesliga, we introduce Monte Carlo Pass Search (MCPS), which infers kick parameters for each observed pass, samples execution variants and option variants, rolls each candidate forward with a ball-conditioned world model until the next ball interaction, and scores outcomes with a learned value model to obtain a distribution over gained value. This distribution enables distribution-aware attribution with two complementary execution-surplus scores used for analysis and ranking: mean-based and percentile-based scores. To make the world model sample-efficient under limited public data, we adapt a discrete-token, autoregressive trajectory generator from autonomous driving (SMART) and show it yields strong best-of-20 forecasting accuracy compared to baselines, while supporting fully hypothetical rollouts for downstream evaluation. We have released model checkpoints and code.

</details>


### [216] [ABC-Bench: An Agentic Bio-Capabilities Benchmark for Biosecurity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11150)
*Andrew Bo Liu,Samira Nedungadi,Bryce Cai,Alex Kleinman,Harmon Bhasin,Seth Donoughe*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种名为ABC-Bench的基准测试，用于评估大语言模型（LLM）在生物安全相关任务中的代理能力。该基准涵盖从撰写液体处理机器人代码、设计DNA片段进行体外组装到规避DNA合成筛查等任务，涉及生物学与软件技能的结合。所有测试的LLM代理在三项任务中均超过中位数人类专家表现，尤其在基于已有知识和标准协议的任务上表现优异，而在需要新颖生物信息学推理的任务上表现较弱。通过三个湿实验验证，OpenAI的o4-mini-high生成的脚本成功在OpenTrons机器人上实现了预期序列的DNA组装。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着大语言模型在生物研究中展现出文献综述、实验数据分析及模拟生物学任务的能力，其潜在的双重用途风险日益凸显。为评估这些模型在生物安全方面的潜在威胁，亟需一个系统性的基准测试工具来衡量其代理能力。

Result: 所有测试的LLM代理在三项任务中均优于中位数人类专家；在已有知识和标准化流程任务上表现良好，在需要创新性生物信息学推理的任务上表现较弱；o4-mini-high生成的代码在真实机器人上成功完成了预期的DNA组装。

Conclusion: 大语言模型已具备执行复杂生物操作的能力，尤其在已有知识支持的任务中表现出色，这既带来科学发现的新机遇，也对生物安全构成新挑战。因此，建立持续评估机制以监控和管理此类技术风险至关重要。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are rapidly acquiring capabilities relevant to biological research, from literature synthesis to interpretation of experimental data. Increasingly, LLM agents can also perform in silico biology tasks that previously required experienced human biologists. These emerging AI capabilities offer new opportunities for scientific discovery and biomedical advances, but they also shift the landscape of biosecurity risks. To address this, we introduce the Agentic Bio-Capabilities Benchmark (ABC-Bench), a suite of tasks to measure agentic biosecurity-relevant capabilities. ABC-Bench evaluates LLM agents on both benign and dual-use biology tasks: writing code to operate liquid handling robots, designing DNA fragments for in vitro assembly, and evading DNA synthesis screening. These tasks require a combination of biology and software expertise. All tested LLM agents outperformed the median expert human baseliner on all three tasks. Agents performed highly on tasks drawing on published knowledge and well-documented protocols, and more weakly on a task requiring novel bioinformatics reasoning. In three wet-lab validation experiments, we found that OpenAI's o4-mini-high produced scripts that, when run on an OpenTrons liquid handling robot, successfully assembled DNA with expected sequences.

### [217] [ReasonAlloc: Hierarchical Decoding-Time KV Cache Budget Allocation for Reasoning Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11164)
*Wenhao Liu,Hao Shi,Yunhe Li,Weizhi Fei,Xiangyuan Wang,Mengzhe Ruan,Hanxu Hou,Peisong Wang,Linqi Song,Shuang Qiu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出ReasonAlloc框架，通过分层预算分配解决大语言模型推理中长链思维轨迹导致的键值缓存膨胀问题。该框架结合离线层级预分配与在线头级动态重分配，有效捕捉推理过程中的上下文需求变化，在数学推理任务上显著优于现有方法，尤其在小预算下表现突出，且无需训练、开销极低。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前解码阶段的KV缓存压缩方法多采用均匀预算分配，无法适应自回归推理中逐步变化的上下文需求；而已有非均匀分配方法主要针对静态提示预填充阶段，不适用于动态推理过程。因此需要一种能适配解码阶段、支持动态资源分配的新方法。

Method: ReasonAlloc将解码时的KV压缩重构为分层预算分配问题：采用离线层级预分配策略识别由模型架构决定的‘推理波’模式；在线头级策略根据实时信息量动态向高价值头重新分配资源，实现双层次优化。

Result: 在MATH-500和AIME 2024等数学推理基准测试中，ReasonAlloc显著优于统一预算（R-KV）、SnapKV及金字塔式静态预算（Pyramid-RKV）方法，尤其在128–512令牌的小预算场景下提升最明显。该方法可无缝集成现有淘汰策略，推理开销几乎可忽略。

Conclusion: ReasonAlloc是一种无需训练、即插即用的解码时KV压缩框架，通过分层与动态的预算分配机制，有效缓解了长链推理中的缓存瓶颈，在保持高性能的同时实现了高效的资源利用。

Abstract: Long chain-of-thought (CoT) trajectories in large language model (LLM) reasoning cause severe inference bottlenecks due to rapid key-value (KV) cache growth. Current decoding-time compression methods mitigate this issue via token eviction, but typically assume a uniform budget distribution across all layers and heads. In contrast, existing non-uniform budget allocation methods are predominantly designed for the static prompt prefill phase, and they do not capture the stepwise context demands of autoregressive reasoning. To bridge this gap, we propose ReasonAlloc, a training-free framework that recasts decoding-time KV compression as a hierarchical budget allocation problem. ReasonAlloc operates at two complementary levels: an offline layer-wise preallocation strategy captures an architecture-driven demand pattern which we call ``\textit{Reasoning Wave}'', while an online head-wise strategy reallocates resources during decoding to information-rich heads based on real-time utility. Evaluations on mathematical reasoning benchmarks (MATH-500, AIME~2024) using DeepSeek-R1-Distill-Llama-8B, DeepSeek-R1-Distill-Qwen-14B, and AceReason-14B show that ReasonAlloc outperforms uniform-budget R-KV, SnapKV, and Pyramid-RKV (a baseline enforcing a static, monotonically decreasing layer budget), with the largest gains at small budgets (128-512 tokens). ReasonAlloc is plug-and-play with existing token-eviction policies and introduces negligible inference-time overhead.

</details>


### [218] [The Role of Feedback Alignment in Self-Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11173)
*Semih Kara,Oğuzhan Ersoy*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究自蒸馏中的上下文设计，通过在冻结的批评者反馈上训练求解器，比较了三种条件：二元奖励（GRPO）、参考解答和与求解器推理轨迹对齐的逐步批判。结果表明，与对齐的逐步反馈相比，其他方法效果较差，因其能精准定位推理失败的令牌，而参考解答则迫使模型在每个令牌上都改变行为（包括正确步骤），从而降低了效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自蒸馏依赖于教师模型所接收的上下文，但上下文的设计尚未被充分探索。如何设计有效的上下文以提升自蒸馏性能是关键问题。

Method: 在冻结的批评者反馈下训练求解器，对比三种不同上下文条件：二元奖励（GRPO）、参考解答、与推理轨迹对齐的逐步批判，并通过性能指标和逐令牌分析评估效果。

Result: 与对齐的逐步反馈相比，GRPO提升16.11分，参考解答条件提升5.27分（Avg@12）。逐令牌分析显示，对齐反馈仅影响推理错误的令牌，而参考解答导致模型在所有令牌上都试图改变行为，即使正确步骤也被干扰。

Conclusion: 反馈与求解器推理过程的结构对齐是自蒸馏有效性的关键因素。精确、针对性的反馈可显著提升模型性能，而泛化性或非对齐的反馈可能带来不必要的扰动。

Abstract: Conditioning a language model on additional context, such as feedback on a previous attempt, typically improves its response. Self-distillation trains the model to retain this improvement when the context is not present. The method works by matching the model's output distribution under two settings: a student that sees only the question, and a self-teacher that also sees the context. What the model learns therefore depends on what context the self-teacher receives, yet the design of this context remains largely unexplored.
  We study context design for self-distillation by training a solver on feedback from a frozen critic. We compare three conditions: (i) a binary reward (GRPO), (ii) the reference solution, and (iii) a step-by-step critique aligned to the solver's reasoning trace.
  Step-aligned critique yields the largest gains, outperforming GRPO by 16.11 points and reference-solution-conditioned self-distillation by 5.27 points (Avg@12). Per-token advantage analysis reveals why: step-aligned feedback targets only the tokens where reasoning fails, leaving correct behavior intact. Conditioning on the reference solution, by contrast, pressures the model to change its behavior at every token (even correct steps) because an alternative derivation inevitably differs in phrasing and approach. This suggests that structural alignment between feedback and the solver's reasoning is a key driver of self-distillation effectiveness.

</details>

### [219] [Mechanistic Analysis of Alignment Algorithms in Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09850)
*Aarush Sinha,Ishan Garg,Veeraraju Elluru,Arth Singh,Kushal Garg*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文系统分析了六种偏好优化方法（PPO、DPO、SimPO、ORPO、GRPO、KTO）在三种开源模型中的内部机制，发现不同方法对语言模型的表征空间产生显著不同的几何变换。其中，KTO和GRPO通过特征共享与高显著性特征激活提升线性可分性；而DPO和ORPO则因非建设性旋转和特征衰减降低可分性；PPO和SimPO基本保持原始几何结构。结果表明，对齐行为不等同于统一的内部重构，强调需建立基于特征层面的标准审计机制以保障模型安全与可解释性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前后训练对齐算法多以黑箱方式评估，缺乏对其内部计算机制的理解，限制了对模型安全性和可解释性的深入分析。本文旨在揭示不同对齐方法如何改变语言模型的内在表征，推动机制透明化与可审计性发展。

Method: 结合层间线性探针、稀疏自编码器与交叉编码器技术，定位偏好表征并量化其在潜在空间中的几何变换，实现对多种对齐方法的系统性机械分析。

Result: 偏好信号集中在早期-中期或中期-晚期层；不同方法引发质性差异的表征转变：KTO与GRPO增强线性可分性，而DPO与ORPO降低可分性，PPO与SimPO维持原结构。这些变化具有架构依赖性，表明对齐并非均质干预。

Conclusion: 对齐是异质性干预，不应假设其导致统一的内部重构。应建立标准化的特征级审计机制，以提升模型安全性与可解释性，并设计更机制感知的优化目标。

Abstract: Post-training alignment algorithms are predominantly evaluated as black boxes, obscuring how they reshape language models' internal computations. We present a systematic mechanistic analysis of six preference-optimization methods: PPO, DPO, SimPO, ORPO, GRPO, and KTO across three open-weight model families. By integrating layer-wise linear probing, Sparse Autoencoders, and crosscoders, we localize preference representations and quantify alignment-induced geometric transformations in latent space. We find that preference signals consistently concentrate in early--mid or mid--late layers, but different objectives induce qualitatively distinct representational shifts. KTO and GRPO enhance linear separability through constructive feature sharing and sparse, high-salience recruitment. In contrast, DPO and ORPO degrade separability via non-constructive geometric rotation and feature attenuation, while PPO and SimPO largely preserve baseline geometry. These transformations exhibit architecture-dependent variability, demonstrating that behavioral alignment does not imply uniform internal restructuring. Our findings establish alignment as a heterogeneous intervention, motivate standardized feature-level auditing for safety and interpretability, and highlight the need for mechanism-aware optimization objectives.

</details>


### [220] [SynIB: Informational Bottleneck for Maximizing Synergy in Multimodal Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09853)
*Konstantinos Kontras,Teodora Gagaleska,Thomas Strypsteen,Christos Chatzichristos,Matthew Blaschko,Maarten De Vos,Paul Pu Liang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种名为协同信息瓶颈（SynIB）的新训练目标，旨在直接优化多模态学习中的协同效应。与传统方法侧重于复杂模型架构不同，SynIB通过信息论形式化协同效应，并在训练中惩罚模型在单模态缺失时仍保持高置信度的行为，从而鼓励跨模态推理。在合成XOR任务和五个真实世界基准测试中，SynIB显著提升了协同依赖样本的准确率（最高提升7.8%）和整体准确率（最高提升3.8%）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大多数多模态学习方法主要通过设计更复杂的融合架构来捕捉跨模态协同效应，但往往忽视了训练目标对协同信息学习的影响。标准训练倾向于关注单模态或冗余信息，难以有效学习需要跨模态推理的任务。因此，亟需一种能主动引导模型关注协同信息的训练机制。

Method: 本文提出Synergistic Information Bottleneck（SynIB），基于信息论定义协同效应。在训练过程中，模型在每次前向传播中随机屏蔽一个模态，若模型仍保持高置信度预测，则施加惩罚，以抑制对单模态线索的依赖。同时保留标准任务损失，使模型在所有模态联合下实现准确预测。

Result: 在合成的XOR任务中，标准训练无法恢复已知的协同效应，而SynIB成功实现了目标；在五个真实世界基准任务（包括多模态情感分析、仇恨表情包识别及可控讽刺检测）上，SynIB在协同依赖样本上的准确率提升最高达7.8%，整体准确率提升最高达3.8%。

Conclusion: SynIB通过重新设计训练目标，有效引导模型学习多模态协同信息，在多个任务中显著提升了性能，证明了从训练目标层面优化协同效应的有效性。该方法为多模态学习提供了一种轻量且可扩展的替代路径，不依赖复杂架构即可增强跨模态推理能力。

Abstract: A central objective in multimodal learning is to capture synergy: task-relevant information that arises only from the joint use of multiple modalities, and is not available from any single modality alone. While most approaches operate at the architectural level through larger or more complex fusion models, we propose a complementary axis: shaping the training objective itself. Standard training often emphasizes unimodal or redundant information, falling short on examples that require cross-modal reasoning. We formalize multimodal synergy through information theory and introduce the Synergistic Information Bottleneck (SynIB), a scalable objective that targets synergy directly. To prioritize learning synergy, SynIB motivates the model to predict accurately from all modalities while penalizing confidence when information from any modality is withheld. Alongside the standard task loss, the model runs forward passes with one modality masked at a time and is penalized for remaining confident, which would indicate reliance on unimodal cues rather than cross-modal interactions. We validate SynIB in two regimes. On synthetic XOR tasks where the ground-truth synergy is known by construction, standard training fails to recover it while SynIB does. On five real-world benchmarks, including three MultiBench affective tasks, Hateful Memes with CLIP-ViT and DeBERTa backbones, and a controllable irony extension of CREMA-D we introduce, SynIB improves accuracy on synergy-dependent examples by up to 7.8% and overall accuracy by up to 3.8%.

</details>


### [221] [Uncertainty-aware Multi-fidelity Closure via Conditional Normalizing Flows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09857)
*Jice Zeng,Shady E. Ahmed,David Barajas-Solano,Panos Stinis*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文将降低阶数模型（ROM）闭合建模问题视为多保真度（MF）学习问题，提出一种基于条件归一化流的不确定性感知MF框架，以提升ROM预测精度。该方法通过学习从低保真度（LF）ROM系数到高保真度（HF）系数的概率映射，改善预测保真度并量化闭合项的不确定性。研究了两种校正策略：直接学习（直接由LF输入预测HF系数）和残差学习（学习LF与HF系数之间的差异并用于修正）。在二维Navier-Stokes方程控制的涡旋合并问题上验证了该框架，结果表明两种策略均优于未校正的ROM，且残差学习表现更优。此外，所提出的基于深度生成模型的方法能够提供对校正后ROM系数的不确定性量化，对评估预测置信度和保障实际应用中ROM的可靠性至关重要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: ROM在处理复杂多尺度系统时效率高，但其预测精度常受截断误差及已解析与未解析尺度间相互作用表示不足的影响，导致闭合问题。现有方法难以有效捕捉未解析尺度的影响，且缺乏不确定性量化机制，限制了其在实际中的可靠应用。因此，亟需一种既能提升精度又能量化不确定性的新型闭合建模方法。

Method: 提出一种基于条件归一化流的不确定性感知多保真度学习框架。通过构建从低保真度ROM系数到高保真度系数的概率映射，实现对闭合效应的建模。采用两种策略：1）直接学习，直接预测HF系数；2）残差学习，学习LF与HF系数间的差异并进行修正。利用深度生成模型实现高效概率建模与不确定性估计。

Result: 在二维Navier-Stokes方程的涡旋合并问题中，两种校正策略均显著提升了ROM的预测精度，优于未校正的ROM；其中残差学习性能更优。所提方法不仅提高了预测保真度，还提供了对校正后系数的不确定性量化，有助于评估预测置信度，支持在实际工程中的可靠应用。

Conclusion: 本文提出的基于条件归一化流的多保真度不确定性感知框架，有效解决了ROM闭合建模中的精度与不确定性问题。通过残差学习策略实现更优的校正效果，并为模型输出提供可信的不确定性评估，为复杂系统高效模拟与决策支持提供了有力工具。

Abstract: Reduced-order models (ROMs) provide an efficient surrogate for complex multiscale systems, but their predictive accuracy is often compromised by truncation errors and the inadequate representation of interactions between resolved and unresolved scales. The missing effect of truncated (unresolved) scales on ROM (resolved) scales is often denoted as the closure problem. In this work, we formulate ROM closure modeling as a multi-fidelity (MF) learning problem and propose an uncertainty-aware MF framework based on conditional normalizing flow to enhance ROM predictive accuracy. The proposed approach learns a probabilistic mapping from low-fidelity (LF) ROM coefficients to high-fidelity (HF) coefficients, thereby improving predictive fidelity while quantifying the uncertainty associated with the learned closure. Two correction strategies are investigated: direct learning, in which HF coefficients are predicted directly from LF inputs, and residual learning, which learns the discrepancy between LF and HF coefficients and uses it to recover the corrected HF solution. The framework is demonstrated on a vortex merging problem governed by the two-dimensional Navier Stokes equations. Results show that both correction strategies improve ROM accuracy over uncorrected ROM, with residual learning achieving consistently better performance than direct learning. Moreover, the two proposed deep generative model-based strategies provide uncertainty quantification for the corrected ROM coefficients, which is critical for assessing prediction confidence and supporting the reliable use of ROMs in practical applications.

</details>


### [222] [Mitigating Manifold Departure: Uncertainty-Aware Subspace Rectification for Trustworthy MLLM Decoding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09859)
*Yingxuan Zhuang,Jingxiao Yang,Miao Pan,Cheng Tan,Yuxiang Cai,Siwei Tan,Chen Zhi,Xuhong Zhang,Jianwei Yin,Jintao Chen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为Manifold-Guided Adaptive Projection (MGAP)的几何感知、无需训练的解码方法，旨在缓解多模态大模型（MLLMs）中的幻觉问题，同时保持表示结构的完整性。传统方法通过惩罚语言先验来减少幻觉，但忽略了语言先验在与视觉证据对齐时可能有益的双重性质。MGAP通过奇异值分解（SVD）构建语言先验子空间，并在解码过程中将多模态隐藏状态投影到该子空间，利用一致性感知门控自适应地抑制仅与先验相关的部分，从而实现选择性更新，保留正交语义成分。实验表明，MGAP在POPE和CHAIR数据集上优于现有基线，有效抑制幻觉且不损害文本连贯性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: MLLMs常因过度依赖语言先验而产生与视觉输入不符的幻觉。现有训练-free解码策略虽试图通过惩罚语言先验缓解此问题，但忽视了语言先验在与视觉证据一致时可提供帮助的双重性，盲目抑制会导致语义流形偏离，降低性能。

Method: MGAP首先通过SVD从盲隐藏状态构建语言先验子空间；在解码阶段，将多模态隐藏状态投影至该子空间，并使用一致性感知门控自适应衰减投影后的先验分量，实现子空间选择性更新，以保留正交语义成分。

Result: 在POPE和CHAIR数据集上的实验表明，MGAP显著优于现有解码基线，在有效抑制幻觉的同时保持了良好的文本连贯性，未出现性能下降。

Conclusion: MGAP通过几何感知的自适应投影机制，实现了对语言先验的精准调控，既减少了幻觉，又避免了语义流形的破坏，为解决多模态模型中的幻觉问题提供了新思路。

Abstract: MLLMs frequently hallucinate objects inconsistent with visual inputs. This issue is typically attributed to the over-reliance on language priors, which can override the visual context. Recent training-free decoding strategies address this by penalizing language priors. However, these methods overlook the dual nature of language priors, where they can be both helpful and harmful depending on the alignment with visual evidence. In particular, blindly suppressing language priors often disrupts the model's semantic manifold, leading to performance degradation, a phenomenon we term Manifold Departure. To address this, we propose Manifold-Guided Adaptive Projection (MGAP), a geometry-aware, training-free decoding method that mitigates hallucinations while preserving representation structure. MGAP first constructs a language-prior subspace from blind hidden states via SVD. During decoding, MGAP projects each multimodal hidden state onto this subspace and applies a consistency-aware gate to adaptively attenuate only the projected prior component, yielding a subspace-selective update that largely preserves the orthogonal semantic components. Extensive experiments on POPE and CHAIR show that MGAP outperforms prior decoding baselines, achieving stronger hallucination suppression without sacrificing coherence.

It integrates a mutual-information-based stability selection procedure to identify a compact, clinically interpretable feature subset via bootstrap resampling, constructing prediction sets whose marginal coverage provably exceeds a user-specified confidence level. We evaluated Method on a multicenter cohort from Guangzhou, China (primary n=2,187; external validation n=412) using 78 candidate features across demographics, metabolic biomarkers, and lifestyle factors. Method achieves an AUROC of 0.912 internally and 0.891 externally, outperforming deep neural networks, TabNet, support vector machines, and logistic regression. Conformal prediction sets achieve 91.3% empirical coverage at the 90% nominal level. A three-tier risk stratification derived from these scores separates the population into distinct groups, with the high-risk subgroup showing a 12-month progression rate 4.7 times that of the low-risk tier. Method: UniTok采用向量量化自编码器，结合前缀归一化以稳定尺度，使用渐进分辨率因果结构进行编码解码，并引入结构保持重建损失；UniTok-FM则直接使用通用大模型架构，不进行任何时间序列特异性修改，通过在具有相似模式的多序列上下文中进行下一标记预测来学习共享动态。

Abstract: While Next-Token Prediction (NTP) has unified LLM pretraining, its adaptation to unbounded, continuous time series (TS) remains open. To bridge the gap, we introduce UniTok, a universal tokenizer that transforms TS into discrete tokens, and UniTok-FM, a foundation model pretrained via NTP on these tokens. UniTok-FM is a general-purpose foundation model that supports zero-shot and prompt-boosted forecasting, as well as few-shot generation and classification via training-free in-context inference--a capability not achieved by prior works. Technically, UniTok is a vector-quantized autoencoder incorporating prefix normalization for scale stabilization, a progressive-resolution causal architecture for encoding and decoding, and a structure-preserving reconstruction loss for training. UniTok-FM adopts an off-the-shelf LLM architecture without TS-specific modifications. Instead of pretraining on isolated TS, it performs NTP on context windows formed by multiple series with similar patterns, aiming to capture their shared dynamics. Experiments on forecasting, generation, and classification show that a single unified UniTok-FM consistently outperforms statistical and supervised baselines, achieves competitive performance with task-specific foundation models, and uniquely enables training-free in-context inference across tasks.

### [225] [Blurry Window Attention](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09862)
*Axel Laborieux,Christos Sourmpis,Juan Gabriel Kostelec,Qinghai Guo*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为模糊窗口注意力（BLA）的新方法，旨在解决Transformer模型在长序列场景下的二次复杂度和状态膨胀问题。BLA基于状态空间模型（SSMs）思想，利用Dirichlet核进行插值重建模糊的键值历史，实现线性复杂度与有限状态大小。它可视为滑动窗口注意力（SWA）的推广或门控槽注意力（GSA）的特例。实验表明，BLA在状态效率上比SWA高8倍，并在需要信息检索的任务中表现优异，是少数随状态增大而性能提升的线性模型之一。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Transformer模型中的Softmax Attention存在序列长度二次复杂度和KV缓存状态随长度增长的问题，限制了其在长上下文场景的应用。尽管已有线性复杂度模型如SSM、LA和ABC等，但在需精确召回特定信息的任务中仍落后于Transformer。因此，亟需一种兼具高效性和强记忆能力的新型注意力机制。

Method: 提出模糊窗口注意力（BLA），通过存储频率窗口并利用Dirichlet核对键值历史进行插值重建，实现高效的模糊记忆。该方法可被看作滑动窗口注意力（SWA）的泛化版本，或门控槽注意力（GSA）中以Dirichlet核实现衰减因子的特例。采用高效算法实现，保证计算与内存开销可控。

Result: 在多查询关联回忆（MQAR）任务中，BLA的状态效率比SWA高出8倍，且与主流线性注意力模型相当；在RegBench任务中，只有BLA和SWA随着状态规模增加而提升性能，表明其具备良好的记忆扩展能力。

Conclusion: BLA是一种高效且具有强记忆能力的线性注意力机制，能够在保持低复杂度的同时有效支持长序列中的信息检索与召回任务，为替代传统Transformer在长上下文应用提供了有力候选方案。

Abstract: The Softmax Attention operation in Transformer language models has a quadratic complexity in the sequence length and a growing state size in the form of KV cache, which becomes a bottleneck in long context scenarios. To overcome this limitation, alternative architectures with linear complexity and finite state size have been introduced, such as State-Space Models (SSMs), Linear Attention (LA), and Attention with Bounded-memory Control (ABC). Though linear models achieve similar language perplexity as Transformers, they are still behind in tasks which require retrieval or recall of specific information. In this work, we introduce Blurry Window Attention (BLA) a novel ABC method inspired by SSMs. BLA stores a frequency window from which a blurry KV history is reconstructed via interpolation using Dirichlet kernels. BLA can be understood as a generalization of Sliding Window Attention (SWA) depending on the Dirichlet kernels resolution or as a special case of the Gated Slot Attention (GSA), where the decay factor is implemented with Dirichlet kernels. We describe in details the theory and efficient implementation of BLA. On the Multi-Query Associate Recall (MQAR) synthetic task, we show that the state efficiency of BLA is 8$\times$ better than SWA and is competitive with popular linear attention models, and in the RegBench synthetic task, only BLA and SWA improve their performance as the state size grows among the linear models we tested.

### [226] [From Confident Closing to Silent Failure: Characterizing False Success in LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09863)
*Laksh Advani*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了大模型代理在任务执行中出现的‘假成功’（false success）问题，即代理声称任务完成但实际环境状态未变。通过分析tau2-bench和AppWorld两个基准测试中的大量轨迹数据，发现假成功在不同场景下发生率差异显著：tau2-bench中单控域为45–48%，双控电信域仅为3%，而AppWorld自评估编码代理中高达75.8%。现有基于LLM的判断器表现不佳，无论配置如何，其在tau2-bench上AUROC均不超过0.65，在AppWorld上仅达0.54。这些判断器依赖表面线索（如自信结束语或动作数量），而非真实状态变化。相比之下，轻量级TF-IDF检测器在任务无关情况下分别达到0.83和0.95的AUROC，检出效率是最佳判断器的4–8倍，延迟降低3300倍。研究建议生产监控应采用轻量、领域校准的检测器作为初步筛查信号，而非依赖LLM判断器作为主要监控手段。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大模型代理在任务执行中可能沉默失败，即声称已完成任务但实际未达成目标，这种‘假成功’现象影响系统可靠性。现有依赖大模型判断任务完成性的方法存在不可靠性，亟需更高效、准确的监测机制。

Method: 在tau2-bench（8个模型家族，9,876条轨迹）和AppWorld（4个模型家族，1,879条轨迹）两个基准上，分析代理行为与真实环境状态之间的不一致。比较多种LLM判断器（5种配置、5种提示策略、完整任务描述）的表现，并引入轻量级TF-IDF检测器进行对比。使用AUROC评估判断准确性，分析判断器依赖的表面线索，并量化检测效率与延迟。

Result: 假成功在不同设置中普遍且差异显著：tau2-bench单控域45–48%、双控电信域3%、AppWorld自评估编码轨迹75.8%。所有LLM判断器性能有限，最高AUROC仅0.65（tau2-bench）和0.54（AppWorld），主要依赖表面线索。轻量级TF-IDF检测器在任务无关条件下分别达到0.83（tau2-bench）和0.95（AppWorld）的AUROC，检出假成功能力为最佳判断器的4–8倍，延迟降低3300倍。

Conclusion: 生产环境中应避免依赖大模型判断器作为主监控手段来识别假成功。推荐使用轻量、领域校准的检测器（如TF-IDF）作为初步筛查工具，以实现高效、低延迟的假成功检测。

Abstract: LLM agents can fail silently by asserting task completion when the environment state shows otherwise. We study this failure mode, false success, across two agent benchmarks: 9,876 tau2-bench trajectories from 8 model families and 1,879 AppWorld trajectories from 4 model families with text-independent ground truth. False success is common but varies by setting: 45--48% of failures in single-control tau2-bench domains, 3% in dual-control telecom, and 75.8% among AppWorld self-assessing coding-agent trajectories with explicit status claims. LLM judges fail reliably: no configuration across 5 judges, 5 prompt strategies, and full task specifications exceeds AUROC 0.65 on tau2-bench, and the same judges reach only 0.54 AUROC on AppWorld API-call traces. Judges rely on surface completion proxies -- confident closing language in tau2-bench and coarse action-sequence volume in AppWorld -- rather than verified state changes. Lightweight TF-IDF detectors achieve task-disjoint AUROC 0.83 on tau2-bench and 0.95 on AppWorld, recovering 4--8x more false successes than the best judge at the same flag rate with 3,300x lower latency. These results suggest that production monitoring should use lightweight, domain-calibrated detectors as triage signals rather than relying on LLM judges as the primary monitor for false success.

### [227] [Alignment Collapse Under KV Cache Quantization: Diagnosis and Mitigation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09864)
*Bruce Changlong Xu,Adarsh Kumarappan,Mu Zhou*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究揭示了低比特KV缓存量化会无声破坏大语言模型的安全对齐，尽管标准指标（如困惑度）未显示明显下降。通过分析11个指令微调模型（3.8B-72B）和5个基准测试（1,894个提示），发现安全特征位于对量化噪声极度敏感的低维激活子空间中，导致模型在极低比特下出现剧烈的安全性退化。提出Per-Channel Reduction（PCR）诊断方法，可识别三种机制性失效模式：异常值压制安全、异常值即安全、多层稀释。PCR仅需20个校准提示即可准确预测缓解方向，在九个主模型及一个独立家族模型上表现良好，且泛化性强，适用于未见提示、模型和生产级量化器。最终实现无需训练的修复协议，仅需约35 GPU分钟，恢复高达97%的安全对齐，有效解决实际部署中FP8 KV缓存带来的安全隐患。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有KV缓存量化评估仅关注困惑度和准确性，忽视其对模型安全对齐的影响。然而，低比特量化可能无声破坏安全特性，导致模型更易生成有害内容，亟需系统性评估与修复机制。

Method: 提出Per-Channel Reduction（PCR）诊断框架，通过分析各通道在量化过程中的响应行为，识别安全特征所在通道及其脆弱性；基于此分类模型为三类失效模式，并设计针对性修复策略；利用少量校准提示实现跨模型、跨任务泛化，构建训练-free的修复协议。

Result: PCR能准确预测九个主要模型及一个独立模型的修复方向；在多种模型、提示和量化器上实现高达97.2%的安全对齐恢复；修复仅需约35 GPU分钟，内存开销极小，且已在生产级vLLM FP8部署中验证有效性。

Conclusion: KV缓存量化存在隐蔽的安全风险，传统评估指标无法捕捉。通过揭示安全特征的几何脆弱性并引入PCR诊断，可实现高效、通用、无需训练的对齐恢复，显著提升量化部署下的安全性。

Abstract: Key-value (KV) cache quantization is widely used to reduce Large Language Model (LLM) inference memory, yet existing evaluations solely focus on measuring perplexity and accuracy without assessing the safety impact. In this study, we explore alignment preservation under KV cache quantization. Across eleven instruction-tuned models (3.8B-72B) and five benchmarks (1,894 prompts), we find that low-bit quantization can silently destroy safety alignment: Mistral-7B loses 15.2% of its refusals at only 1.03x perplexity, and no universal safe bit-width exists, with sharp model-specific phase transitions invisible to standard metrics. We identify that the root cause is geometric: safety features occupy a low-dimensional activation subspace 10^2-10^3x more vulnerable to quantization noise than the full representation space perplexity averages over. Inspired by this observation, we propose Per-Channel Reduction (PCR), a diagnostic that classifies each model into one of three mechanistic failure modes: outlier-crushes-safety, where safety lives in non-outlier channels collaterally damaged by outlier-driven scale factors; outlier-as-safety, where safety overlaps outlier channels and finer granularity cannot rescue it; and multi-layer dilution, where safety is distributed across many layers and per-layer fixes fail. PCR predicts the correct mitigation direction on all nine primary models and one held-out model from an independent family using 20 calibration prompts. PCR generalizes across unseen prompts, models, and production quantizers, including KIVI with up to 97.2% recovery, succeeding where attention-based allocation methods fail. The resulting training-free protocol, requiring approximately 35 GPU-minutes, recovers up to 97% of lost alignment at minimal memory overhead, addressing vulnerabilities confirmed in production vLLM serving with FP8 KV cache on NVIDIA GPUs.

### [228] [LLM-as-a-Discriminator: When Synthetic Tables Still Look Real](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09865)

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于大语言模型（LLM）的合成数据隐私审计方法，通过让LLM判断表格数据是真实还是合成的来评估隐私风险。实验对比了LLaMA和Gemini在两种设置（仅表格数据与表格加分布元数据）下的表现，使用CTGAN、TVAE和高斯耦合三种生成模型处理UCI Adult和ACS Census数据集，共451次有效试验。结果显示不同模型间存在显著差异：在Adult数据上，LLaMA对报告单元的判别率为0%，而Gemini对CTGAN和TVAE的判别率高达100%；在Census数据上，LLaMA多数预测为合成，而Gemini在C1中保持高位，但在C2中对CTGAN和TVAE下降。相比传统的两样本检验（C2ST）和记录链接等基线方法，以及人工标注（2名标注者，240次试验），LLM判别表现出较强的实用性，前提是需谨慎处理模型选择、提供方报告和数据编码问题。代码与实验脚本已公开。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 隐私与数据共享之间存在矛盾，合成数据被广泛用于降低隐私风险并实现数据共享，但现有方法难以有效审计合成数据的隐私泄露风险，尤其在表格数据场景下，人类也难以区分真实与合成数据。因此，亟需一种可靠且可操作的隐私审计手段。

Method: 采用大语言模型（LLM）作为判别器，设计两种测试场景：C1（仅表格数据）、C2（表格加分布元数据）。利用开源模型LLaMA和参考模型Gemini，对CTGAN、TVAE和高斯耦合三种合成模型生成的数据进行分类任务，判断其为真实或合成。同时引入两样本检验（C2ST）、记录链接作为分布基线，并开展人工标注实验以对比评估。

Result: 实验表明，不同合成模型在不同设置下表现出明显差异：在UCI Adult数据集上，LLaMA的判别率（DRS）为0%（即无法识别），而Gemini对CTGAN和TVAE的判别率高达100%；在ACS Census数据集上，LLaMA普遍预测为合成，而Gemini在C1中表现稳定，在C2中对CTGAN和TVAE的判别能力下降。整体来看，LLM判别性能优于传统基线方法，且具备实际应用潜力，但结果受模型选择、数据编码等因素影响较大。

Conclusion: 基于大语言模型的判别方法可作为合成数据隐私审计的有效信号，具有较高的实用价值，但需在模型选择、数据呈现方式及提供方透明度方面加以规范，确保结果可复现与可信。相关代码与实验脚本已开源，支持研究复现。

Abstract: Privacy and data sharing are often in tension. Many organizations use synthetic data to reduce privacy risk and still share useful data. For tabular data, auditing privacy remains hard. In many cases, even humans cannot easily tell if a table is real or synthetic. In this paper, we propose a method based on LLM discrimination. We ask an LLM to classify each table sample as REAL or SYNTHETIC. We test two settings: C1 with table only, and C2 with table plus distributional metadata. We use LLaMA as an open model and Gemini as a reference model. In our experiments, we run three synthesis models, CTGAN, TVAE, and Gaussian Copula, on two public datasets, UCI Adult and ACS Census. We collect 451 valid trials. Our results show clear differences between models. On Adult, LLaMA reaches DRS=0% in reported cells, while Gemini reaches DRS=100% for CTGAN and TVAE. On Census, LLaMA predicts SYNTHETIC for most samples, while Gemini stays high in C1 but drops for CTGAN and TVAE in C2. We also compare with a classifier two-sample test (C2ST) and record linkage as distributional baselines, and with a human pilot of 2 annotators and 240 trials. Our results show that LLM discrimination is a practical privacy audit signal when model choice, per provider reporting, and data encoding are handled with care. For reproducibility, code and experiment scripts are available at https://github.com/SlokomManel/LLM-as-a-Discriminator.

### [229] [Two to Tango: Coupled Task-Reference Selection for Safe LLM Fine-tuning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09866)
*Xinrui Chen,Jianhao Zhang,Ou Wu,Di Gao*

Method: 提出DualSelect框架，通过最小最大视角，联合选择具有高保留损失和任务冲突的安全参考，以及与所诱导参考方向兼容的任务样本；采用熵正则化评分代理、懒惰参考刷新机制和梯度修正策略实现高效优化。

Conclusion: DualSelect为安全对齐大模型的微调提供了一种有效且可扩展的方法，不仅在任务适应中保持强安全性，还适用于以保留为核心目标的持续学习场景。

Abstract: Fine-tuning safety aligned large language models (LLMs) on downstream data improves adaptation but may erode learned safety behavior. Existing methods use fixed safety examples, global constraints, or one-sided task filtering. Our diagnostics show task updates expose different safety constraints, motivating joint selection of relevant references and compatible task samples. We propose DualSelect, a coupled framework for task and reference selection that refreshes task conditioned safety references before filtering whole task samples compatible with the induced reference direction. Under a minimax view, DualSelect selects safety references with high preservation loss and task conflict, together with compatible task samples, through entropy-regularized scoring surrogates, lazy reference refresh, and gradient correction. On 1B-8B LLMs, DualSelect preserves safety without losing task utility; using the REDORCA judge, it improves Safety Avg. over the strongest baseline by at least 5.10 points and remains highest in Safety Avg. across judges with moderate overhead. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有机器遗忘方法依赖目标概念的视觉数据，但在严格数据保留政策下难以获取，因此需要无需源数据的无源免学习方法。

Method: SPACE包括两个阶段：(1) 文本引导的代理锚点选择（TPAS），从共享特征空间中检索语义对齐的代理锚点；(2) 双约束语义隔离（DCSI），优化这些锚点以间接擦除目标概念，并将更新限制在保留知识的零空间内，确保结构完整性。

Result: 在六个数据集上的实验表明，SPACE在无源场景下的性能与最先进的依赖数据的方法相当，验证了其有效性。理论分析证明其能严格限制对保留知识的扰动并最大化特征谱熵。

Conclusion: SPACE是首个针对多模态大模型的无源免学习框架，能够在不访问目标数据的情况下有效且安全地移除敏感信息，同时维持模型性能，具有重要的实际应用价值。

Abstract: As Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) face growing privacy risks and regulatory constraints, machine unlearning (MU) has emerged as a crucial solution for removing sensitive data while preserving model performance. However, existing MU methods typically rely on visual data of the target concepts, which is often unavailable due to strict data retention policies, thus creating a demand for source-free unlearning approaches that operate without access to the target data. In this work, we propose Source-free Proxy Anchor Concept Erasure (SPACE), the first source-free unlearning framework specialized for MLLMs. SPACE consists of two stages: (1) Text-Guided Proxy Anchor Selection (TPAS), which retrieves semantically aligned proxy anchors from the shared feature space. (2) Dual-Constraint Semantic Isolation (DCSI), which optimizes these anchors to indirectly erase target concepts. DCSI confines updates to the null space of retained knowledge, ensuring structural integrity. We theoretically prove that SPACE strictly bounds the perturbation on retained knowledge and maximizes feature spectral entropy, thereby maintaining the model's performance. Furthermore, extensive experiments across six datasets show that SPACE achieves performance comparable to that of state-of-the-art data-dependent methods, validating its effectiveness in source-free MU scenarios. The source code will be released.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在异构设备环境下难以确定最优的模型分割点，固定分割点会导致资源弱设备过载，增加通信和服务器负担，影响收敛速度与稳定性。

Method: 采用轻量级硬件指标（如CPU利用率、内存、电池电量、网络延迟）作为状态输入，结合基于衰减损失下降的奖励机制与委员会式DQN架构，利用多数投票策略防止奖励欺骗，实现动态且智能的分割点选择。

Abstract: Federated Learning (FL) combined with Split Learning (SL) is a privacy preserving paradigm that enables training deep neural networks (DNNs) on resource constrained devices while reducing overall training cost. Fixed split points can overload weak devices and increase the communication and server load, which slows convergence and reduces stability. This paper introduces QSplitFL, a novel capability-aware Deep Q-Network (DQN) framework for optimal split point selection in Split learning based Federated Learning (SFL) environments. Unlike existing approaches that rely on high-dimensional model weight representations, QSplitFL employs a lightweight state representation derived directly from client hardware metrics, including CPU utilization, memory, battery level, and network latency. The proposed framework incorporates a decayed loss-drop reward function that prioritizes early convergence, and a committee-based DQN architecture with majority voting to mitigate reward hacking. Extensive experiments on MNIST, Fashion-MNIST, CIFAR-10, and CIFAR-100 datasets using CNN, ResNet50, MobileNetV4, and ConvNeXt architectures demonstrate that our approach achieves better convergence and higher accuracy compared to existing methods, while effectively adapting to heterogeneous device resources. The source code is publicly available at https://github.com/AIPO-Lab/QSplitFL.

### [232] [PatchSTG: Scalable Spatiotemporal Graph Transformers for Traffic Forecasting on Irregular Sensor Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09872)

Method: 提出PatchSTG模型，采用基于地理信息的层次化空间表示，将传感器划分为平衡、局部性保持的块；设计双注意力编码器，交替使用块内注意力捕捉局部交互，块间注意力建模全局依赖，从而降低计算复杂度。

In practical traffic networks, sensors are unevenly distributed across regions, leading to non-uniform spatial structures that limit the effectiveness and scalability of existing graph-based and attention-based models. To address these challenges, we propose PatchSTG, a patch-based spatiotemporal graph Transformer designed for efficient forecasting on irregular sensor networks. The key idea is to introduce a hierarchical spatial representation that partitions sensors into balanced, locality-preserving patches based on geographic information. On top of this structure, a dual attention encoder alternates between intra-patch attention for capturing local interactions and inter-patch attention for modeling global dependencies, reducing computational complexity from quadratic to near-linear scaling. We evaluate PatchSTG on real-world traffic data from Rhode Island and additional large-scale datasets. Experimental results demonstrate that the proposed model achieves stable and competitive forecasting performance across multiple horizons, while significantly improving computational efficiency. Ablation studies further validate the effectiveness of spatial partitioning and dual attention in capturing both local and long-range traffic dynamics. These results suggest that patch-based spatiotemporal modeling provides a scalable and effective framework for traffic forecasting under irregular spatial settings.

TL;DR: Rotate2Think 是一种无需训练的方法，通过分析输入与思考向量在嵌入空间中的几何差异，利用正交普罗克拉斯特定理估计一个旋转矩阵，将合成的思考向量注入推理过程起始位置，从而引导模型产生更优的推理路径。该方法在多个数学、科学和代码任务中显著提升准确率，并可零样本推广至多模态推理任务。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 发现输入和思考嵌入均具有高度锥度性，且方向不共线；基于此提出使用正交普罗克拉斯特定理估计从输入到思考的旋转，并在推理时注入合成思考向量作为几何引导。

Conclusion: 思考过程的嵌入在语义空间中占据独立于输入的几何区域，通过几何旋转可有效引导推理，表明旋转式思维注入是一种高效、通用且无需训练的推理增强策略。

Abstract: Reasoning models achieve strong performance on challenging tasks by generating explicit intermediate reasoning traces before producing a final answer. Yet the internal structure of representation space when reasoning remains poorly understood: how do a model's hidden representations differ during thinking versus the embeddings of the input prompt, and can this structure be exploited to elicit stronger reasoning at inference time? We show that both input embeddings and thinking embeddings (mean-pooled last-layer hidden states over the prompt and reasoning trace, respectively) exhibit extremely high conicity, with all vectors clustering tightly around a single mean direction. Crucially, these mean input and thinking directions are non-collinear, with thinking embeddings occupying a geometrically distinct region of embedding space across many different models and benchmark tasks. This observation motivates casting the input-to-thinking transition as a rotation problem admitting a closed-form solution via orthogonal Procrustes analysis. We propose Rotate2Think, a training-free method that estimates this rotation from a small set of correctly solved examples and injects the resulting synthetic thinking vector between thinking delimiters at inference time, providing a geometric primer at the onset of the reasoning trace. Evaluated across multiple benchmarks and model families, Rotate2Think improves accuracy in 30 of 32 model-benchmark configurations across mathematics, science, and code tasks, and generalizes zero-shot to multimodal reasoning on MATH-Vision.

### [234] [Disjoint or Overlapping? Inference Windowing for Reconstruction-Based Time Series Anomaly Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09874)
*Guillaume Coulaud,Reza Akbarinia,Florent Masseglia*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文重新审视了单变量离线时间序列异常检测中的基于重构的方法，重点研究了推理步长（inference stride）的影响，提出了一套统一的训练、调参和多种子评估协议，并在TSB-AD基准上评估了多种模型（如PCA、DLinear、AutoEncoder、TimesNet、Transformer等）在重叠窗口与非重叠窗口下的表现。结果表明，重叠推理可带来高达28%的相对性能提升，并可能改变方法排名。研究还分析了数据集、随机种子和超参数配置带来的变异性。此外，在完整UCR存档上的评估也验证了该方法的有效性。结论是：重构型异常检测不仅依赖模型结构和训练方式，还受推理策略影响，因此需要清晰、可复现的评估协议。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于重构的异常检测方法在评估实践中存在异质性，导致结果难以比较；同时，推理过程中的步长设置（如窗口是否重叠）对性能有显著影响但常被忽视。因此，亟需建立统一、透明且可复现的评估框架，以准确评估不同方法的真实性能。

Method: 提出一个统一的训练、调参与多种子评估协议，使用标准化的TSB-AD基准数据集，系统评估不同模型在不同推理步长（重叠/非重叠窗口）下的表现；通过大量实验分析性能差异来源，包括数据集、随机种子和超参数配置的影响。

Result: 在所有模型中，采用重叠窗口进行推理均带来一致的性能提升，平均相对增益达+28%，部分情况下甚至改变模型间的排名；在完整UCR存档上的评估也显示重构方法具有强竞争力。

Conclusion: 重构型异常检测的性能不仅取决于模型设计与训练，还高度依赖于推理策略，尤其是窗口重叠与否。因此，应建立标准化、可复现的评估流程，以推动领域内公平比较与进步。同时，重构基线方法在多个基准上表现优异，具备实际应用价值。

Abstract: Reconstruction-based methods are widely used for time series anomaly detection, where models are trained to reconstruct subsequences, and anomalies are identified through reconstruction errors. However, reported results are often hard to compare due to heterogeneous evaluation practices and underspecified inference procedures. In this paper, we revisit reconstruction-based anomaly detection in the univariate offline setting and study the role of the inference stride, which controls whether subsequences are processed as disjoint windows or with overlap. We propose a unified training, tuning, and multi-seed evaluation protocol on the curated TSB-AD benchmark, and study how overlapping inference affects anomaly detection performance for a range of reconstruction models, including PCA-based baselines, DLinear, an AutoEncoder, TimesNet, and Transformer variants. The results show that across all models, overlapping windows yield consistent improvements, with average relative gain up to +28%, and can alter method rankings. We further analyze variability across datasets, random seeds, and hyperparameter configurations. Finally, we complement the benchmark study with an evaluation on the full UCR archive using localization criteria aligned with sliding-window reconstruction. Overall, our results highlight that reconstruction-based anomaly detection performance depends not only on model architecture and training, but also on inference choices, motivating a clear and reproducible protocol. Our results show that reconstructionbased baselines achieve strong performance on both TSB-AD and UCR benchmarks, supporting them as competitive and practical approaches for univariate time series anomaly detection.

### [235] [Integrating Local and Global Entropy for Uncertainty Quantification in LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09875)
*Johanne Medina,Tianyi Zhou,Keivin Isufaj,Aristides Gionis,Sanjay Chawla*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种名为GLU的新型不确定性量化方法，通过结合隐藏状态的全局几何复杂度（全局不确定性）与标记级熵（局部不确定性），在无需监督信号的情况下实现高效、准确的可靠性预测。该方法在多个模型家族和基准测试中表现优异，仅需一次前向传播，且具有长度归一化和架构无关性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型常以自信的方式产生幻觉，因此需要有效的不确定性量化（UQ）来确保可靠部署。现有方法主要依赖于标记级别的信号，忽略了中间隐藏状态的几何结构信息。

Method: 利用隐藏状态矩阵的几何复杂度作为全局不确定性度量，将标记级熵视为局部度量；发现两者在统计上近乎正交，能捕捉不同的失效模式；提出全局-局部不确定性（GLU）方法，通过乘法门融合两种信号。

Conclusion: 通过结合全局几何复杂度与局部标记不确定性，GLU提供了一种高效、通用且可靠的无监督不确定性量化方案，尤其能识别传统方法遗漏的‘自信但错误’的失效模式。

Abstract: Large language models hallucinate confidently, making uncertainty quantification (UQ) essential for reliable deployment. Existing methods rely predominantly on token-level signals, leaving the geometric structure of intermediate hidden states underused. In this paper, we take the geometric complexity of hidden-state matrices as a measure of the global uncertainty of LLMs, while treating token-level uncertainty estimation as a local metric. We show that hidden-state geometric entropy (global uncertainty) and token-level entropy (local uncertainty) are statistically near-orthogonal, capturing distinct failure regimes for reliability prediction. In particular, global geometry recovers the confident-but-wrong failure mode that local signals systematically miss. Building on this, we propose Global-Local Uncertainty (GLU), an unsupervised, single-pass score that fuses the two signals via a multiplicative gate. Across three model families and six benchmarks, GLU matches or outperforms all unsupervised baselines while requiring only a single forward pass and remaining length-normalized and architecture-agnostic.

*Ke Li,Chongzhe Zhang,Zifan Zeng,Feng Liu,Qunli Zhang,Zheng Hu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出PCHI方法，在推理时通过冻结的探测器检测可能错误但自信的回答，并条件性地调整注意力头输出，以选择性降低过度自信，同时尽量保留正确答案的置信度。在Qwen3-4B-Instruct上，读出标记的PCHI将82.2%的错误置信转换为否，联合干预使ECE从21.9%降至9.2%，仅影响5.1%原本正确的回答。该方法在Gemma3-4B上也有效，但效果较弱且依赖掩码。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型常对错误答案表现出过高置信，现有校准方法通常全局作用于分数，虽能降低不当自信，但可能损害正确答案的合理置信度。需要一种能选择性抑制错误自信而不影响正确判断的方法。

Method: 引入Probe-Conditioned Head Intervention（PCHI），利用冻结探测器识别高自信但可能错误的响应，并在置信度生成过程中条件性地重缩放下游注意力头输出，实现局部、精准的置信度调控。

Result: 在Qwen3-4B-Instruct上，读出标记的PCHI使82.2%的错误‘是’置信转为‘否’；联合干预使ECE从21.9%降至9.2%，仅5.1%原正确答案被误伤。在Gemma3-4B上效果存在但较弱且依赖掩码设置。

Conclusion: 通过条件化内部干预可选择性减少语言模型的过度自信，部分解耦了对不当自信的抑制与对正当自信的保持之间的矛盾，为更精细的置信度控制提供了新路径。

Abstract: Large language models often express high confidence in answers that are wrong. Standard calibration remedies typically act globally or at the score level, reducing unwarranted confidence but also risking erosion of warranted confidence on correct answers. We introduce Probe-Conditioned Head Intervention (PCHI), an inference-time method that uses a frozen probe to detect likely wrong-but-confident responses and conditionally rescales downstream attention-head outputs during confidence generation. On Qwen3-4B-Instruct solving OpenMathInstruct problems with a structured binary confidence field, readout-token PCHI converts 82.2% of originally wrong-yes confidence readouts to $\texttt{no}$, while a joint intervention across upstream confidence-template tokens reduces ECE from 21.9% to 9.2% and damages only 5.1% of originally correct-yes readouts. The readout-token effect also appears on Gemma3-4B, though upstream interventions are weaker and more mask-dependent. These results show that verbalized overconfidence can be selectively reduced through conditionally applied internal intervention, partially decoupling the suppression of unwarranted confidence from the loss of warranted confidence.

</details>


### [237] [Streaming Knowledge Compilation: Proactive Materiality-Scored Pinning for Time-Evolving LLM Wikis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09877)
*Juan M. Huerta*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出Streaming Knowledge Compilation（流知识编译）框架，解决大语言模型（LLM）维基系统在动态信息环境下的知识更新问题。通过引入一个材料度信号φ_t(k,n)来预测文档对实体k的重要性，实现提前缓存关键信息以最小化未来查询的累积遗憾（regret）。理论证明了该方法在任意可预测知识缺口的领域中具有O(√(T log K))的遗憾界，且仅依赖于一个领域相关的误差ε = ℰ[|φ_t - φ̂_t|]。在金融和维基百科两个领域验证：金融中使用冻结的Llama 3.1 8B分类头预测异常波动（AUROC=0.728），维基百科采用归一化的异常编辑率（AER）作为信号。实验表明，基于遗憾分析的评估优于传统QA得分，能有效消除LLM作为评判者带来的后训练知识偏差。金融领域遗憾收敛至-20.0（每步-0.12），维基百科为+16.0（每步+0.13），后者正值证实编辑内容确实提升了知识丰富性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM维基系统假设知识库静态不变，无法应对信息随时间演化的场景。当新知识出现或旧知识更新时，系统表现会下降。因此需要一种能够持续适应动态信息流、在有限缓存预算下主动选择重要知识进行编译的机制，以最小化因知识缺失导致的查询性能损失。

Method: 提出Streaming Knowledge Compilation框架，利用材料度信号φ_t(k,n)作为文档重要性的代理指标，根据其值决定是否将文档内容预填入KV缓存。该信号在金融领域由冻结的Llama 3.1 8B分类头预测异常股票波动，在维基百科中使用跨主体标准化的异常编辑率（AER）衡量编辑活跃度。通过在线学习策略动态维护缓存，确保在固定token预算下最大化知识覆盖。理论分析给出了基于φ_t估计误差的累积遗憾上界。

Result: 在金融数据集上，预测材料度信号的AUROC达0.728，被预测为高材料度的文章在未来表现出1.49倍更高的实际波动率；在维基百科上，使用AER同样有效。端到端问答评估显示，传统QA分数受LLM自身知识偏见干扰严重，而基于累积遗憾的评价方法更可靠。金融领域遗憾收敛至-20.0（每步-0.12），说明系统优于离线最优解；维基百科遗憾为+16.0（每步+0.13），表明新增编辑内容确实带来了更有价值的知识，提升整体表现。

Conclusion: Streaming Knowledge Compilation提供了一种通用且可扩展的方法，用于在动态信息环境中高效管理编译知识。只要存在可预测的知识缺口信号，该方法即可保证理论上的遗憾界。实验证明，基于遗憾分析的评估比绝对QA分数更能真实反映系统性能，为构建鲁棒的实时知识系统提供了新范式。

Abstract: LLM wiki systems compile knowledge into pre-filled KV caches for efficient inference, but assume a static corpus -- an assumption that fails whenever the underlying information landscape evolves. We formalize Streaming Knowledge Compilation: given a document stream, a fixed token budget, and future queries unknown at ingestion time, maintain a compiled wiki that minimizes cumulative regret against an offline oracle with perfect foresight. The enabling insight is a materiality signal $φ_t(k,n)\in[0,1]$ that scores document importance for entity $k$ at time $t$, acting as a query-relevance surrogate for proactive pinning before queries arrive; we prove an $O(\sqrt{T\log K})$ regret bound where $\varepsilon=\mathbb{E}[|φ_t-\hatφ_t|]$ is the only domain-specific quantity. We instantiate in two domains: finance, where $φ_t$ is abnormal stock volatility predicted by frozen Llama 3.1 8B classification head (AUROC = 0.728 on 76K articles, strict temporal split; $1.49\times$ higher realized forward volatility for predicted-material articles); and Wikipedia, where $φ_t$ is the Abnormal Edit Ratio (AER), a cross-sectionally normalized edit velocity -- showing the same algorithm generalizes beyond the finance domain. End-to-end QA evaluation on 173 matched pairs (finance) and 119 (Wikipedia) reveals a pervasive LLM-as-judge confound on post-training knowledge, establishing that regret analysis -- not absolute QA scores -- is the reliable evaluation metric for compiled knowledge systems. Finance cumulative regret converges to -20.0 (-0.12/step); Wikipedia to +16.0 (+0.13/step), with the positive sign confirming that Wikipedia edit content is genuinely post-training -- richer context consistently improves scores (No Wiki 3.80 vs. Oracle 4.74) -- and eliminates this confound. The $O(\sqrt{T\log K})$ guarantee applies to any domain where knowledge gaps can be predicted from streaming signals.

</details>


### [238] [FailureScope: Cross-Regime Behavioral Diagnosis of Language Model Weaknesses](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09878)
*Nicholas Saban*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: FailureScope是一种行为诊断方法，通过聚类评估探针的跨模型通过/失败模式（留一模型排除，LOMO），在单轮基准、多轮对话和对抗性代理攻击三种不同场景中均能生成稳定且可解释的故障分类体系。在18个模型的2,664个单轮任务上，基于分类的采样在50个任务内达到Kendall's tau = 0.81（随机选择为0.34），跨模型故障预测达到AUC 0.88。该方法同样适用于363个任务的多轮语料库和630条对抗性代理轨迹，揭示出一种元故障模式：大语言模型判断的ASR与真实执行之间存在73-100个百分点的差距。三类场景中聚类一致性保持良好，表明行为聚类是一种可迁移的诊断基础方法，超越单一基准的局限。研究团队发布了分析管道、三个标注语料库及跨场景分类体系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有标准基准仅报告整体准确率，但无法帮助从业者识别模型具体缺失的能力。需要一种能够系统识别模型失败模式并提供可解释诊断的方法，以支持针对性改进。

Method: FailureScope通过留一模型排除（LOMO）策略，根据模型在评估探针上的通过/失败模式进行聚类，从而识别出具有相似失败特征的任务组，构建跨场景的故障分类体系。

Result: 在单轮任务中，分类引导采样达到Kendall's tau = 0.81（优于随机选择的0.34），跨模型故障预测AUC达0.88；在多轮对话和对抗性代理攻击中也获得可解释的聚类结果，揭示出显著的元故障模式（如LLM-judge ASR与真实执行间的巨大差距），且聚类一致性在三类场景中均保持良好。

Conclusion: 行为聚类（如FailureScope）是一种可迁移的诊断原语，能够在不同任务范式间泛化，为理解模型失败模式提供了统一、可解释的框架，并有助于更高效地定位和修复模型缺陷。

Abstract: Standard benchmarks report aggregate accuracy, but practitioners need to know which specific capabilities a model lacks. We introduce FailureScope, a behavioral-diagnosis method that clusters evaluation probes by their cross-model pass/fail patterns (leave-one-model-out, LOMO), and show it yields stable, interpretable failure taxonomies across three regimes usually studied separately: single-turn benchmarks, multi-turn dialogue, and adversarial agent attacks. On 2,664 single-turn tasks across 18 models, taxonomy-conditioned sampling reaches Kendall's tau = 0.81 at 50 tasks (versus 0.34 for random selection), and cross-model failure prediction reaches AUC 0.88. The same primitive recovers interpretable clusters on a 363-task multi-turn corpus and on 630 adversarial agent traces, where it exposes a meta-failure mode: a 73-100 percentage-point gap between LLM-judge ASR and real execution. Cluster cohesion remains strong across all three regimes, which we take as evidence that behavioral clustering is a portable diagnosis primitive that generalizes beyond any single benchmark. We release the pipeline, three annotated corpora, and the cross-regime taxonomies.

### [239] [Operator Fusion for LLM Inference on the Tensix Architecture](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09879)
*Qingbo Wu,Ke Li,Wenzhu Wang,Jie Yu,Ruian Zhang,Lili Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究针对Tenstorrent Tensix架构上Transformer模型的设备端推理瓶颈，提出一种操作融合策略，通过将RMSNorm与自注意力及前馈网络中的矩阵乘法融合，提升数据局部性，显著减少中间结果的DRAM读写和调度开销。为支持多核并行，采用基于NoC的多播机制，由行列主节点高效分发输入和权重，缓解DRAM带宽竞争。在Wormhole平台上对Qwen2.5-0.5B、Qwen3-0.6B和Qwen3-4B的实验表明，注意力模块延迟最高降低37.44%，MLP模块降低15.89%，每解码层最多降低7.91%，且皮尔逊相关系数（PCC）保持在98.75%以上，证明了在数值一致性下的显著端到端效率提升。

  <summary>Details</summary>
