Method: 提出一种操作融合策略，将RMSNorm与自注意力和前馈网络中的矩阵乘法融合，实现内存密集型与计算密集型操作在片上SRAM中的连续执行；同时引入基于NoC的多播机制，由行/列主节点在核心网格中高效分发输入和权重，以支持多核并行并缓解DRAM带宽竞争。

Result: 在Wormhole平台上的实验显示，注意力模块延迟最高降低37.44%，MLP模块延迟最高降低15.89%，每解码层延迟最多减少7.91%；皮尔逊相关系数（PCC）超过98.75%，表明在数值精度保持一致的前提下实现了显著的端到端性能提升。

Conclusion: 通过操作融合与高效的多核通信机制，该方案有效缓解了Tensix架构上Transformer模型的推理瓶颈，在保证数值一致性的同时实现了显著的性能优化，为边缘侧大模型部署提供了可行路径。

Abstract: This study addresses on-device inference bottlenecks of Transformer models on Tenstorrent's Tensix architecture and proposes an operator fusion strategy that enhances data locality. RMSNorm is fused with matrix multiplication in self-attention and in the FFN, enabling back-to-back execution of memory-bound and compute-bound operators in on-chip SRAM to significantly reduce DRAM reads/writes of intermediate results and scheduling overhead. To support multi-core parallelism, a NoC-based multicast mechanism is leveraged in which row/column master nodes efficiently distribute inputs and weights across the core mesh, alleviating DRAM bandwidth contention. Experiments on the Wormhole platform with Qwen2.5-0.5B, Qwen3-0.6B, and Qwen3-4B show up to 37.44% latency reduction for attention and 15.89% for MLP, with up to 7.91% reduction per decoder layer, while Pearson Correlation Coefficient (PCC) remains above 98.75%, confirming significant end-to-end efficiency gains under numerical consistency.

The proposed method integrates DE into the training process of the LFT model to automatically learn optimal regularization parameters $λ_1$, $λ_2$ and $λ_3$. As a result, the model can adaptively search the hyperparameter space and improve prediction accuracy. *Ryan Brown,Chris Russell*

Result: 在同域与跨数据集测试中，FF consistently 减少不同群体间的FPR/TPR差异，显著提升最低群体准确率，同时维持甚至提高整体准确率。方法具有极低的运行时开销，适用于实际部署。

Conclusion: Face-Fairness 提供了一种高效、通用、无需敏感标签的公平性缓解方案，解决了深度伪造检测中因群体差异导致的性能不公问题，具有良好的实用价值和推广潜力。

Abstract: Deepfake detectors show large performance gaps across demographic groups. Existing fairness approaches require demographic labels, retraining, or sacrifice accuracy. We introduce Face-Fairness (FF), a plug-and-play framework for bias mitigation. Our primary contribution, Face-Feature Tuning (FFT), is the first demographic label-free fairness method demonstrated for deepfake detection: a lightweight calibrator that performs a logit remapping conditioned on frozen face embeddings. We complement FFT with two variants: FF-Max, which maximizes worst-group accuracy when demographics are available, and FF-Discover, which does the same with embedding-discovered groups. Across in-domain and cross-dataset test settings, FF consistently reduces FPR/TPR gaps and improves minimum group accuracy while maintaining (often improving) overall accuracy. The approach is detector-agnostic, adds negligible runtime overhead, and requires no access to identity attributes.

### [242] [TD-Grokking: Learning from Zero-Reward Problems by Training-Time Decomposition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09883)
*Ningyuan Xi,Hao Xu,Hongsheng Xin,Ning Miao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出TD-Grokking框架，通过训练时分解零奖励问题为可验证的子问题，形成层级树结构，使原本无优化信号的问题产生非零奖励，从而提升大语言模型在数学和医学任务上的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有强化学习与可验证奖励（RLVR）方法在高难度零奖励问题上失效，因为所有推理路径均失败，无法提供优化信号。现有解决方案如密集过程监督、部分奖励分配或前缀引导探索存在任务限制，未能充分赋予模型解决原难题的能力。

Method: 提出一种训练时分解框架TD-Grokking，递归地将难以求解的根问题分解为自包含且可验证的子问题，构建层次化树结构，使得可解的叶节点能够提供非零奖励，从而生成有效训练信号。

Result: 在数学和医学任务上的实验表明，TD-Grokking优于基线方法（包括标准GRPO），显著提升了模型性能，并验证了训练时分解能有效将零奖励示例转化为可用训练信号。

Conclusion: 训练时分解能有效克服零奖励问题的瓶颈，通过构建可验证的子问题层级结构，为模型提供持续优化信号，实现稳定性能提升。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have made remarkable progress in reasoning tasks, largely driven by post-training paradigms, especially reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR). However, a critical bottleneck persists: RLVR fails on highly challenging zero-reward problems, where all sampled reasoning trajectories yield uniformly failed outcomes, providing no optimization signal to drive model improvement. Prior efforts to address this limitation, such as dense process supervision, partial reward assignment, or prefix-guided exploration, suffer from inherent task constraints or do not fully equip the policy model with the capabilities necessary to solve the original intractable problems. To address this, we propose TD-Grokking, a training-time decomposition framework for zero-reward problems. It recursively decomposes intractable root problems into self-contained, verifiable subproblems, forming hierarchical trees where solvable leaves provide non-zero rewards. Evaluations on mathematical and medical tasks show that TD-Grokking outperforms vanilla GRPO as well as all baseline approaches. Together with detailed analysis, these results confirm that training-time decomposition effectively converts zero-reward examples into usable training signals, enabling consistent performance gains. Our code and datasets are available at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/TD-Grokking-6567/.

### [243] [TENP: Trapezoidal Expert Neuron Pruning For Mixture-of-Experts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09885)
*Jiangyang He,Shaolin Zhu,Deyi Xiong*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: TENP是一种结构化分层专家神经元剪枝框架，通过保留重要专家和对不重要专家进行神经元级剪枝，在保持模型性能的同时显著降低参数量。实验表明，该方法在40%专家稀疏度下仅导致1%准确率下降，并在代码生成任务上优于全参数模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有压缩方法要么移除整个专家破坏路由结构，要么依赖非结构化权重剪枝，效率有限。为解决这些问题，需一种既能保持路由拓扑又高效压缩参数的方法。

Method: 提出TENP框架，利用少量样本识别重要专家；对不重要专家采用专家神经元剪枝（ENP），按从浅到深层的梯形模式保留参数；结合输出幅度与输入方向变化能力评估专家重要性；通过神经元投影贡献衡量其重要性并保留关键神经元。

Result: 在DeepSeek模型上，40%专家稀疏度下仅损失1%准确率，平均激活参数比例为63.76%，且在代码生成任务中比全参数模型提升10%。

Conclusion: TENP有效实现了Mixture-of-Experts LLMs的高效压缩，在保证性能的同时大幅减少静态参数占用，具有良好的实用潜力。

Abstract: Mixture-of-Experts large language models (LLMs) scale efficiently through sparse activation, yet their deployment is fundamentally constrained by the large static parameter footprint of experts. Existing compression approaches either remove entire experts, disrupting routing topology and harming performance, or rely on unstructured weight pruning with limited practical efficiency. To address the limitations, we propose TENP, a structured Trapezoidal ExpertNeuron Pruning framework. Using a few samples, we identify and retain important experts, while applying expert neuron pruning (ENP) to less important experts, reserving model parameters in a trapezoidal pattern from shallow to deep layers. When evaluating expert importance, we jointly consider both the magnitude of the expert output and its ability to change the direction of the input vector. For ENP, we measure each neuron's projected contribution to the expert output to identify and retain important neurons. We conduct extensive experiments on the Qwen and DeepSeek models. Under a routing expert sparsity of 40% and an average of 63.76% activated expert parameters, the DeepSeek model suffers only a 1-point drop in accuracy compared to the full-parameter model. Moreover, it outperforms the full-parameter model by 10% on code generation tasks.

</details>


### [244] [SHAPE: Coalition-Aware Expert Pruning for Sparse Mixture-of-Experts LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09886)
*Yuhao Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: SHAPE是一种任务驱动的专家剪枝框架，通过引入合作博弈中的Shapley值思想，显式建模MoE模型中层内专家间的协作关系，从而识别对高价值组合至关重要的专家。该方法在保持模型拓扑结构的前提下，采用质量-覆盖选择策略，在每层保留最小专家子集以覆盖α比例的非负Shapley贡献，结合二分查找实现目标保留率。在Qwen3-30B-A3B、GPT-OSS-20B和DeepSeek-V2-Lite三个主流MoE模型上验证，SHAPE在20%和40%的专家剪枝率下均保持竞争力精度，显著降低峰值GPU内存占用，且无需额外训练。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有专家剪枝方法通常独立评估专家重要性，忽略了MoE推理中专家组合的协同效应。为克服这一局限，本文提出一种能捕捉层内专家协作关系的剪枝框架，以更准确地识别关键专家。

Method: 将小规模校准集上的路由轨迹建模为合作博弈，使用类Shapley值分配专家的交互感知贡献度，并基于质量-覆盖选择规则与二分查找，在全局剪枝预算下保留每层最小但高效专家子集。

Result: 实验表明，SHAPE在多个MoE模型和基准测试中优于全局及逐层剪枝方法，在20%和40%剪枝率下仍保持良好精度，显著减少峰值显存占用，且无需再训练。

Conclusion: SHAPE通过建模专家间的协作关系，实现了更精准、高效的专家剪枝，有效缓解了稀疏MoE模型部署中的内存瓶颈问题，具有良好的实用性和可扩展性。

Abstract: Sparse Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) large language models achieve strong quality with low per-token compute, yet their deployment is often limited by the memory wall: the full expert pool must remain resident to support token-dependent routing. Expert pruning is a direct remedy, but prior criteria typically score experts independently and overlook that MoE inference is inherently \emph{coalitional}, where outputs arise from routed top-$k$ expert combinations. We propose \textbf{SHAPE}, a task-driven pruning framework that explicitly models \emph{intra-layer} expert cooperation. SHAPE formulates routing traces on a small calibration set as an empirical cooperative game and assigns interaction-aware expert values via a Shapley-style attribution over observed top-$k$ coalitions, enabling the identification of experts that are essential for high-utility collaborations rather than merely frequent. To preserve MoE topology under a global pruning budget, SHAPE further introduces a \emph{quality-coverage} selection rule that retains, in each layer, the minimal expert subset covering an $α$ fraction of non-negative Shapley mass, while using bisection to match a target keep rate. Experiments on three modern MoE backbones (Qwen3-30B-A3B, GPT-OSS-20B, and DeepSeek-V2-Lite) across diverse benchmarks show that SHAPE consistently improves robustness over global and layer-wise pruning variants, maintaining competitive accuracy under 20\% and 40\% expert pruning without additional training and delivering clear reductions in peak GPU memory footprint. The open-source code is available at https://github.com/Alizen-1009/Shapley-Moe.

</details>


### [245] [SocraticPO: Policy Optimization via Interactive Guidance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09887)
*Zirui Liu,Jie Ouyang,Qi Liu,Xianquan Wang,Jiayu Liu,Tingyue Pan,Qingchuan Li,Jing Sha,Zhenya Huang,Shijin Wang,Enhong Chen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: SocraticPO 是一种用于大语言模型强化学习的政策优化框架，通过在推理过程中引入苏格拉底式自然语言指导来改进错误修正。当学生回答错误时，教师会诊断问题并提供简洁的纠正指导，学生在扩展上下文中继续推理。为防止模型依赖教师帮助获取奖励，正确答案在教师干预后仅获得衰减奖励。该方法可无缝集成到现有策略梯度框架中，并能利用强大的黑盒教师模型，无需访问对数或分布匹配。在科学推理基准测试中表现优于强基线，消融实验表明目标引导和奖励衰减均至关重要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前强化学习通常使用标量结果奖励（如正确性）监督大语言模型的推理，但这类奖励仅提供优化方向，缺乏如何修正错误的具体解释，容易导致捷径学习和脆弱策略。需要更有效的机制来指导模型从错误中学习。

Method: 提出 SocraticPO 框架，在强化学习的回溯过程中加入苏格拉底风格的自然语言指导：学生先独立作答；若错误，由教师进行诊断并提供简明纠正指导，学生在扩展上下文基础上继续推理；同时采用奖励衰减机制，使经教师干预后正确的回答只能获得部分奖励，以抑制对辅助纠正的依赖。

Result: 在 SciKnowEval 的本科级科学推理基准上，SocraticPO 显著优于现有的强化学习与自蒸馏基线方法；消融实验证明，目标导向的指导和奖励衰减缺一不可，后者有效减少了对辅助纠正的依赖。

Conclusion: SocraticPO 通过引入自然语言指导和奖励衰减机制，有效提升了大语言模型在复杂推理任务中的纠错能力和鲁棒性，且可兼容现有强化学习架构，具有良好的通用性和实用性。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning (RL) for large language models usually supervises reasoning with scalar outcome rewards, such as binary correctness. Such rewards provide an optimization direction but rarely explain how a model should revise its mistaken reasoning, which can encourage shortcut learning and brittle policies. We propose \textbf{SocraticPO} (Socratic Policy Optimization), a policy-optimization framework that augments RL rollouts with Socratic-style natural-language guidance. During rollout, the student first answers independently; if the answer is incorrect, a teacher diagnoses the attempt and provides concise corrective guidance, after which the student continues under the expanded context. Crucially, this guidance is paired with reward decay: correct answers obtained after teacher intervention only receive decayed rewards, preventing the policy from treating teacher help as a free path to reward. Since SocraticPO only modifies the rollout process while leaving the standard expected-reward objective intact, it can be plugged into existing policy-gradient backends such as Reinforce++. Moreover, because the teacher provides only text-level guidance, SocraticPO can leverage stronger black-box teacher models without requiring access to logits or distribution matching. On undergraduate-level scientific reasoning benchmarks from SciKnowEval, SocraticPO improves over strong RL and self-distillation baselines. Ablations show that both targeted guidance and reward decay are necessary, with reward decay mitigating reliance on assisted correction.

</details>


### [246] [SinkRec: Mitigating Semantic State Sink in Long Sequence Recommendation with Memory-Conditioned Gated Delta Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09888)
*Zhuang Zhuang,Zhipeng Wei,Ji Dai,Jie Chen,Fei Pan,Peng Jiang,Kun Gai*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: SinkRec提出一种混合记忆-转移循环架构，通过残差向量量化将重复的行为模式外化到可学习的条件记忆中，并利用记忆键值对增强注意力模块。同时引入时间感知的状态关系差分门控网络（TDGD），通过抑制被记忆覆盖的更新和移除与记忆对齐的读出响应，净化递归状态的写入与读取。该方法将重复语义从竞争状态的信号转变为可检索的记忆模式，使递归状态专注于动态转换，有效缓解了语义状态下沉问题，在保持线性时间效率的同时提升了长序列推荐性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 线性注意力虽高效，但其压缩的递归状态易受重复行为模式影响，导致语义状态下沉，即重复语义占据状态空间，干扰后续读出。

Method: 提出SinkRec，结合残差向量量化实现行为模式外化至条件记忆，通过记忆键值对注入注意力块；引入TDGD模块，利用记忆净化递归状态的写入与读出过程，抑制冗余更新和对齐响应。

Result: 在公开和工业数据集上的实验表明，SinkRec在长序列推荐任务中具有更高的准确率和更强的效率，有效缓解了语义状态下沉问题。

Conclusion: SinkRec通过解耦行为模式存储与动态转换建模，成功将重复语义转化为可检索的记忆模式，使递归状态专注动态变化，显著提升长序列推荐效果，且保持线性时间复杂度。

Abstract: Linear attention provides an efficient backbone for long-sequence recommendation by avoiding the quadratic cost of standard Transformers, but its compressed recurrent state can be dominated by repetitive behavior patterns. We identify this phenomenon as semantic state sink, where recurring semantics over-occupy the recurrent state and bias subsequent readouts. To mitigate semantic state sink, we propose SinkRec, a hybrid memory-transition looped architecture that decouples collaborative behavioral pattern storage from dynamic transition modeling. SinkRec externalizes recurring local patterns into a learnable conditional memory through residual vector quantization, reinjects the retrieved codes, and exposes memory key-value pairs to the attention block. It further introduces Temporal-Aware State-Relation Differential Gated DeltaNet (TDGD), which uses memory to purify recurrent writing and reading by suppressing memory-covered updates and removing memory-aligned readout responses. This design turns recurring semantics from state-competing signals into memory-retrievable patterns, allowing the recurrent state to focus on dynamic transitions and alleviating semantic state sink with linear-time efficiency. Experiments on public and industrial datasets demonstrate the effectiveness and efficiency of SinkRec.

Conclusion: 预测性监控是大语言模型安全中一个关键且被忽视的任务。当前模型在前瞻性风险识别方面仍有显著不足，亟需发展更强的因果推理与未来预期能力以提升系统安全性。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed as autonomous agents capable of executing multi-step action trajectories toward a given objective. While existing safety research has focused on detecting unethical behavior from complete trajectories, this paradigm is fundamentally retrospective: it identifies harm only after it has already occurred. In this work, we study a critical yet overlooked safety task, which we term Predictive Monitoring: given only a partial action trajectory, can a model infer whether it will culminate in an unethical action before the overt action is executed? To support this task, we present PreActBench, a benchmark of 1,000 paired ethical and unethical action trajectories spanning five domains. We evaluate a range of LLMs, safety guardrail models, and latent probing methods across varying fractions of the action trajectory using our Prefix Foresight F1 metric. Results show that while humans achieve promising performance, predictive monitoring remains challenging even for strong models, highlighting the need for future-oriented risk reasoning in LLM safety.

### [249] [Representation Curriculum: Stagewise Training for Robust Ranking and Allocation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09891)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出 Representation Curriculum (RC)，在训练过程中分阶段使用特征：初期仅使用内容相关的优势信号，随后逐步引入暴露依赖的信念信号，并将内容路径锚定在已学得的优价值表示上，防止梯度衰减并抑制对历史信号的捷径依赖。

Conclusion: Representation Curriculum 有效缓解了排序系统中因过度依赖暴露相关信号而导致的偏差问题，提升了模型在冷启动和分布漂移场景下的泛化能力，是一种通用且可推广的训练干预策略。

Abstract: Ranking in digital marketplaces is a dynamic exposure-allocation mechanism: displayed items shape discovery trajectories and success events logged by the platform to update future allocation policies. Modern ranking systems rely heavily on exposure-confounded signals (e.g. popularity estimates, CTR/CVR aggregates, and ID-based representation), because they are highly predictive under stationary demand. Yet this predictive power can become a learning shortcut: early access to exposure-dependent belief signals steers optimization toward over-reliance on them and away from exposure-independent merit signals (e.g., content-based competitiveness and semantic affinity). Consequently, the learned policy tends to entrench incumbents and degrade cold-start generalization and robustness under distribution shift. We propose Representation Curriculum (RC), a training-time intervention that temporally stages feature utilization. RC foregrounds content-based merit signals initially, then introduces exposure-dependent belief signals while anchoring the content pathway near the learned merit representation, curbing shortcut reliance on historical signals and mitigating gradient starvation on content signals. We formalize RC independently of task and hypothesis class and provide ranking-specific instantiations. In a Gaussian linear ridge setting, we derive closed-form solutions and sufficient conditions under which RC strictly reduces population risk on a cold-start target distribution, with a quantified Pareto tradeoff against source performance. Experiments on public learning-to-rank and recommendation benchmarks, and randomized online experiments in a large-scale e-commerce search system, show that RC measurably shifts reliance from historical belief signals toward content-based merit signals and yields consistent gains on cold populations with a controlled trade-off in head performance.

<details>

Abstract: Textual event records, such as alarm logs, have become an increasingly common data source in engineering and manufacturing systems. Beyond identifying correlations or recurring patterns, engineers are often interested in understanding which types of events causally trigger or influence other events during system operation. Textual event descriptions may contain semantic clues about such causal relationships, and recent large language models (LLMs) provide a promising tool for extracting these signals. However, relying solely on LLM-encoded textual information is insufficient for accurate causal discovery, since semantic patterns do not directly reveal causal mechanisms and may confuse causation with correlation or frequent sequential patterns. To address these challenges, we propose \textbf{LMT}, a Bayesian causal discovery framework for engineering event data that jointly leverages textual descriptions and timestamps. Specifically, LMT first uses LLMs to extract semantic causal signals from event descriptions and constructs a prior distribution over causal graphs among event types or event clusters. It then incorporates temporal evidence through a Poisson-process-based likelihood, allowing the LLM-informed prior to be refined by timestamp-based statistical evidence. By integrating the textual and temporal information, LMT produces a causal graph that is both interpretable and data-supported. Simulation studies show that the proposed framework is effective across different settings and is especially advantageous in small-sample alarm-event scenarios.

*Sophie Zhao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了变换器模型嵌入空间中是否存在与人类意识谱相关的结构化几何特征。结果显示，嵌入向量在空间中呈现出与意识谱一致的全局组织结构：相似状态的句子聚集为局部连贯区域，形成一个有结构的流形。高层和低层区域表现出类似凸性的稳定性，而中间区域则构成过渡走廊。动态分析表明，无论是基于效用引导还是仅依赖几何的贪婪路径，均一致地从低层级向高层级移动，经过中间层级，说明导航性是表示空间的内在属性，受全局方向信号引导但不被其决定。这些发现表明，嵌入空间编码了与假设的意识谱分类法对齐的结构化、可导航几何，为分析和引导模型行为提供了表示层面的新视角。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解语言模型是否在表示空间中编码了类似于人类意识谱的结构化、可解释的意识层次，对于模型引导、评估和对齐具有重要意义。

Method: 通过分析变换器嵌入空间中的几何结构和动态轨迹，研究句子嵌入在意识谱上的分布模式。采用聚类分析、流形结构检测以及路径追踪方法，比较基于效用引导和仅基于几何的贪婪路径的演化趋势。

Result: 嵌入空间呈现出与意识谱一致的全局几何结构，包括局部凝聚的区域、高低层的稳定性和中间过渡带；动态路径显示从低到高层级的系统性迁移，证明导航性是嵌入空间的内在属性。

Conclusion: 嵌入空间编码了与人类意识谱分类法对齐的结构化且可导航的几何，为从表示层面理解与指导模型行为提供了新范式。

Abstract: Across contemplative, philosophical, and psychological accounts, human consciousness is often described along a similar spectrum, ranging from reactive and self-focused patterns to more integrative and coherent ones. Understanding whether language models encode such a structured, human-interpretable consciousness spectrum in representation space is important for model guidance, evaluation and alignment. In this work, we study the geometric structure and dynamics of patterns along this spectrum in transformer embedding spaces. We show that embeddings exhibit a globally organized geometry aligned with this spectrum: sentences associated with similar states cluster into locally coherent regions, forming a structured manifold. In particular, higher-level and lower-level regions exhibit convexity-like stability, while intermediate regions form a transition corridor. Dynamically, both utility-guided and geometry-only greedy trajectories consistently traverse from lower- to higher-level regions, passing through intermediate tiers, indicating that navigability is an intrinsic property of the representation space, guided but not dictated by a global directional signal. These results suggest that embedding spaces encode structured and navigable geometry aligned with a hypothesized consciousness-spectrum taxonomy, broadly inspired by recurring structural descriptions of human consciousness across contemplative traditions, philosophy, and modern psychology, providing a representation-level perspective for analyzing and guiding model behavior.

### [252] [TRAPS: Therapeutic Response Analysis via Pathway-informed Stratification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09898)
*Sujoy Banik,Sayantan Chakraborty,Boishakhi Das Toma,Zainab Ghafoor,Ushashi Bhattacharjee,Koushik Howlader,Tirtho Roy*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Cancer treatment planning requires decisions across multiple clinical dimensions at once. Clinicians must determine whether a patient should receive targeted molecular therapy, radiation therapy, and whether they are likely to survive beyond six months. Existing pathway-informed deep learning models have been developed and tested in isolation, making fair comparison across architectures impossible. We present the first unified benchmark for pathway-guided therapy response modeling, evaluating three biologically informed architectures, BINN, GraphPath, and PATH, across five cancer cohorts drawn from The Cancer Genome Atlas, representing 2,622 patients encoded using Reactome pathway activity scores. Each model is trained jointly on all three clinical outcomes under identical data and evaluation conditions, the first study to treat pathway-structured deep learning as a combined therapy and survival prediction problem. Our results show that no single architecture wins across all tasks: PATH performs best for targeted molecular therapy prediction overall, BINN is most reliable for survival prediction, and no model produces useful predictions for radiation therapy, as the key drivers of that decision are clinical variables not captured in gene expression data. Most strikingly, GraphPath achieves an AUROC of 0.92 on prostate targeted molecular therapy prediction, the highest score in the entire benchmark, demonstrating that lateral co-regulation structure produces exceptional discriminative power when matched to a cohort with a narrow targetable driver programme, even under conditions of extreme class imbalance at only 11\% positive prevalence.

### [253] [When Attribution Patching Lies: Diagnosis and a Second-Order Correction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09899)
*Luyang Zhang,Jialu Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了语言模型中基于梯度的归因方法（如attributions patching）的不可靠性来源，发现主要源于下游网络的非线性而非局部曲率。为此提出三个实用工具：（i）可靠性评分以识别不可信估计，（ii）误差边界量化归因偏差，（iii）通过一次反向传播实现的海森-向量积（HVP）修正，可消除主导级误差。在五个模型家族（124M-9B参数）和多种扰动设置下，HVP是唯一可在大规模模型上可行的二阶修正方法，其多步变体在计算成本远低于Integrated Gradients的前提下，性能达到或超过其水平，显著提升电路识别的准确性，并支持‘筛查-标记-修复’的工作流程，仅对不可靠组件投入计算资源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前机制可解释性依赖于归因估计来识别驱动语言模型行为的内部组件，但常用的一阶梯度方法（如attributions patching）存在系统性误差，影响电路识别的准确性。尽管激活修补（activation patching）是因果评估的金标准，但其计算开销过大，难以扩展。因此亟需理解并修正归因方法的可靠性问题，以支持高效、准确的机制发现。

Method: 分析归因误差来源，揭示非线性在下游网络中的主导作用；提出可靠性评分、误差边界与基于海森-向量积（HVP）的二阶修正方法；设计多步HVP变体以提升精度；构建‘筛查-标记-修复’工作流以优化计算资源配置。

Result: HVP修正方法在多个模型规模和任务设置下均表现出色，其多步变体在远低于Integrated Gradients的计算成本下达到或超越其精度；可靠性评分有效识别不可信估计；误差边界提供可信度量化；整体提升了电路恢复的保真度，支持更高效的可解释性研究流程。

Conclusion: 归因方法的系统性误差主要由下游网络的非线性引起，而非局部曲率。通过引入HVP修正与可靠性评估工具，可在保持高精度的同时大幅降低计算成本，为大规模语言模型的机制可解释性提供了高效、可靠的解决方案。

Abstract: A central goal of mechanistic interpretability is to identify which internal components causally drive a language model's behavior. Because these importance estimates serve as the evidence for identifying circuits, systematic errors can lead to the misidentification of the underlying mechanisms. While activation patching provides a gold-standard causal metric, its computational cost is prohibitive at scale. Practitioners instead rely on attribution patching, a gradient-based, first-order approximation whose reliability remains poorly understood. In this work, we characterize the source of this unreliability, demonstrating that the dominant error stems from the non-linearities in the downstream network rather than local curvature at the patched component. This insight yields three practical tools: (i) a reliability score to detect untrustworthy estimates, (ii) error bounds quantifying potential attribution mis-specifications, and (iii) a Hessian-vector-product (HVP) correction that eliminates the leading-order error with only one additional backward pass. In evaluations across five model families (124M-9B parameters) and both random-token and naturalistic (name-swap) perturbations, HVP is the only second-order correction feasible at larger scale, where standard baselines like Integrated Gradients become computationally prohibitive. In comparative experiments, a multi-step HVP variant matches or exceeds the accuracy of Integrated Gradients at significantly lower compute, outperforming prior second-order baselines. These improvements lead to higher-fidelity circuit recovery on standard benchmarks and support a Screen-Flag-Fix workflow that targets computational effort only toward the components flagged as unreliable.

### [254] [LongMoE: Longitudinal Multimodal Learning via Trajectory-Aware Mixture-of-Experts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09907)
*Maxx Richard Rahman,Prakhar Kumar,Wolfgang Maass*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: LongMoE 是一个统一框架，用于解决多模态临床学习中的模态缺失和纵向动态性两大挑战。它结合上下文感知的补全模块、注意力分词模块、轨迹感知编码器以及上下文条件稀疏专家路由机制，在处理不完整模态数据时表现出更强的鲁棒性，并在多个数据集上验证了其优越性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法分别处理模态缺失或纵向动态问题，但无法同时应对两者；尤其是当模态缺失时，传统方法因忽略时间上下文而表现不佳。因此需要一种能够联合建模模态缺失与疾病进展的统一框架。

Method: LongMoE 采用上下文感知补全模块处理缺失模态，利用注意力分词模块捕捉不规则就诊序列中的频域时间模式，通过轨迹感知编码器建模疾病演变过程，并引入上下文条件稀疏专家混合（Sparse MoE）路由机制实现患者特异性专家选择。

Result: 在 ADNI、OASIS-3 和 MIMIC-IV 数据集上的实验表明，LongMoE 在模态缺失或弱同期模态条件下显著提升模型鲁棒性，且在全模态设置下仍保持竞争力。

Conclusion: LongMoE 成功构建了一个兼顾模态缺失与纵向动态性的统一多模态临床学习框架，为未来智能化临床决策支持系统提供了坚实基础。

Abstract: Multimodal clinical learning is increasingly important for integrating diverse patient data, including imaging, text, and personalised health records. However, it faces two fundamental challenges: i) modality missingness, where arbitrary subsets of modalities are unavailable at a given patient visit, ii) longitudinal dynamics, where the diagnostic significance of an observation depends on the patient's evolving disease trajectory over time. Existing methods address these challenges in isolation: missing-modality frameworks treat each visit as an independent static snapshot and discard temporal context, while longitudinal models often assume complete modality availability and degrade under systematic modality incompleteness. We propose LongMoE (Longitudinal Mixture-of-Experts), the unified framework to jointly address both challenges. LongMoE combines a context-aware imputation module with an attentional tokenization module that captures frequency-domain temporal patterns across irregular visit sequences, a trajectory-aware encoder for modeling disease progression, and context-conditioned Sparse MoE routing for patient-specific expert selection. Experiments on ADNI, OASIS-3, and MIMIC-IV show that LongMoE improves robustness under missing or weak contemporaneous modalities and remains competitive in full-modality settings, establishing a strong foundation for longitudinally-aware multimodal clinical learning.

### [255] [Mix, Don't Pick: Why Synthetic Corpus Composition Matters for Time Series Foundation Model Pretraining](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09912)
*Aaryan Nagpal,Debdeep Sanyal,Murari Mandal,Dhruv Kumar,Saurabh Deshpande*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 合成生成器的选择对时间序列基础模型预训练影响巨大，不同生成器在相同训练预算下可导致预测误差相差两倍。然而，目前缺乏系统性选择方法，且生成器的有效性随模型架构变化而波动。本文提出不解决生成器选择问题，而是采用所有生成器的等权混合，该方法在两种架构上均表现优于或等于最佳单一生成器，并与真实数据结合后形成最强预训练语料库。因此，合成预训练本质是语料组合问题，而非生成器选择问题，组合策略应针对不同模型家族独立验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法缺乏系统性指导来选择合适的合成生成器，且生成器性能受模型架构影响，导致无法通用。错误选择生成器会显著降低模型性能，带来高昂代价。

Method: 采用所有生成器的等权混合，并与真实数据结合，构建预训练语料库；通过实验评估其在不同模型架构上的表现，验证组合策略的有效性。

Result: 等权混合生成器在两种模型架构上均达到或超过最优单个生成器的表现，且与真实数据结合后形成最强预训练语料库。生成器排名不稳定，组合策略需按模型家族定制。

Conclusion: 合成预训练的核心问题是语料组合而非生成器选择，应根据具体模型家族验证组合方案，避免假设通用适用性。

Abstract: Choosing the wrong synthetic generator for time-series foundation model pretraining is costly: under identical training budgets, the best and worst generators produce up to a $2\times$ gap in forecasting error, yet the field has no principled way to make this choice. The problem is compounded by the fact that generator rankings are not stable across architectures: across 11 generator families evaluated on Chronos-T5-Mini and Moirai-Small trained from scratch, we find that which generators are useful depends on the model architecture. Rather than solving the generator selection problem, we sidestep it: a simple equal-weight mixture of all generators matches or beats the best individual generator for both architectures, and composing this mixture with real data yields the strongest pretraining corpora overall. Synthetic pretraining is therefore a corpus composition problem, not a generator selection problem, and composition choices should be validated per model family rather than assumed to transfer.

### [256] [IntentKV: Cross-Turn Intent-Aware KV Cache Pruning for Agent Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09916)
*Junjie Li,Jiong Lou,Jie Li*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: IntentKV 是一种学习型的键值（KV）缓存压缩技术，用于解决多轮大语言模型（LLM）代理在长轨迹任务中因KV缓存膨胀导致的性能瓶颈问题。它通过维护跨轮次的意图记忆（QueryMemory），利用记忆注意力规则对历史token进行评分，并引入零初始化的残差头实现当前查询与K向量的交叉注意力，从而在保持基础模型冻结的前提下，显著减少内存占用和读取带宽。其设计兼容前缀缓存，采用槽位映射重定向机制进行缓存淘汰，确保高效且无损。实验表明，在8k KV预算下，IntentKV几乎无精度损失地匹配全缓存基线；在最长100个BCP查询上，峰值请求token降低77.8%，原始KV读取量减少92.6%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多轮LLM代理在执行复杂任务时会产生大量工具调用、搜索结果和中间推理，导致键值（KV）缓存和读取带宽急剧增长，使KV缓存成为服务瓶颈，而非参数计算。现有方法难以在不牺牲准确性的前提下有效压缩长期轨迹中的冗余信息。因此亟需一种高效、可组合且低开销的KV缓存优化机制。

Method: IntentKV提出一种基于学习的KV缓存剪枝策略：1）构建会话级查询记忆（QueryMemory）以捕捉跨轮次意图；2）使用记忆注意力规则对活跃历史token进行评分，识别重要信息；3）引入零初始化的残差头部，通过交叉注意力关注当前查询与已有K向量的关系；4）采用槽位映射重定向机制实现缓存淘汰，即被丢弃的位置指向一个哨兵死槽，而保留的K/V行、旋转位置编码（RoPE）相位和槽位标识不变，保证与前缀缓存的兼容性。

Result: 在8k KV缓存预算下，IntentKV在Qwen3-8B和Qwen2.5-14B上分别仅造成23.9%和30.7%的平均峰值请求token下降，几乎无精度损失；在最长100个BCP查询任务中，峰值请求token从92.3k降至20.5k（下降77.8%），原始KV读取量从411M降至31M（下降92.6%），显著优于无剪枝基线。

Conclusion: IntentKV通过智能的跨轮次意图建模与轻量级缓存管理机制，在极小的资源开销下实现了对长轨迹任务的高效支持，解决了多轮代理中KV缓存主导的瓶颈问题，具备高实用性与可扩展性，适用于大规模部署的多轮交互式LLM系统。

Abstract: Multi-turn LLM agents fan short queries into long trajectories of tool calls, search results, and intermediate reasoning. Both KV memory and KV read bandwidth grow by orders of magnitude across a single trajectory, making the key-value (KV) cache, not parameter compute, the dominant serving bottleneck for long-horizon agents. We introduce IntentKV, learned KV pruning that keeps the base LLM frozen. IntentKV maintains a session-level QueryMemory of cross-turn intent, scores live history tokens with a memory-attention rule, and adds a zero-initialized residual head with cross-attention over current-query K-vectors. To stay composable with prefix caches, eviction is a slot-map redirection: dropped positions route to a sentinel dead slot while surviving K/V rows, RoPE phases, and slot identities stay in place. IntentKV matches the no-pruning full-cache baseline with almost no accuracy drop under tight KV budgets: at an 8k KV budget, mean peak request tokens drop 23.9% on Qwen3-8B and 30.7% on Qwen2.5-14B. On the 100 longest BCP queries that all methods complete on Qwen2.5-14B, IntentKV-8k further cuts worst-case peak request tokens from 92.3k to 20.5k, a 77.8% reduction, and worst-case raw KV reads from 411M to 31M, a 92.6% reduction.

</details>


### [257] [SPDM: Geometry-Modulated State Space Modeling with Manifold Constraints for Time Series Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09917)
*Xingsheng Chen,Siu-Ming Yiu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种名为SPDM的几何感知状态空间模型，通过将多变量时间序列的交叉变量相关结构建模为对称正定（SPD）流形上的连续轨迹，利用黎曼几何特征（如切空间线性、Frechet均值中心性）作为正则化项，指导并稳定状态空间模型的选择性扫描动态。该方法通过流形轨迹路径和几何门控机制，在保持线性时间复杂度的同时嵌入丰富的结构约束，实现了预测精度与计算效率的双重提升。在11个真实世界基准数据集上的实验表明其性能达到当前最优水平，且几何约束是其性能优势的主要来源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有状态空间模型在处理多变量时间序列时，仅扫描分段的时间或空间序列，忽略了变量间相关结构的动态演化几何特性，导致建模能力受限。因此，需要一种能够捕捉并利用这种演化相关结构的方法。

Method: 提出SPDM架构，包含两个核心机制：(1) 流形轨迹路径，将动态变化的协方差矩阵从SPD流形投影到欧氏切空间；(2) 几何门控机制，基于流形轨迹提取的几何信号直接调节SSM内部的选择性参数。整体设计保留了Mamba的并行扫描线性复杂度，同时引入几何正则化。

Result: 在11个真实世界数据集上实现当前最优的预测性能，实验验证了几何约束是性能提升的关键因素，且模型在保持高精度的同时维持高效计算。

Conclusion: 通过将多变量时间序列的相关结构建模为流形上的动态轨迹，并利用其几何特性作为正则化引导状态空间模型，SPDM显著提升了建模能力和预测性能，同时保持了高效的计算特性，为多变量时间序列预测提供了新的范式。

Abstract: Multivariate time series forecasting requires capturing the continuously evolving correlation structure among interacting variables. Existing state-space models process time series by scanning tokenized temporal or spatial sequences, discarding the evolutionary geometric structure. We address this limitation by introducing manifold constraints into state-space modeling: treating the cross-variable correlation structure as a continuous trajectory on the symmetric positive definite manifold, whose Riemannian geometric features, tangent space linearity, and Frechet mean centrality act as a principled geometric regularizer that guides and stabilizes the selective scanning dynamics of SSMs. We propose SPDM, a geometry-aware SSM architecture that realizes this principle through two cooperating mechanisms: a manifold trajectory path that projects dynamically evolving covariance matrices from the SPD manifold to a Euclidean tangent space, and a geometric gating scheme that directly modulates SSM's internal selective parameters based on geometric signals derived from the manifold trajectory. The parameterization preserves the linear-time complexity of the Mamba parallel scan while embedding rich structural constraints, making the architecture preserve prediction accuracy and computational efficiency simultaneously. Extensive experiments on eleven real-world benchmark datasets establish state-of-the-art forecasting performance, and further studies confirm that geometrically constrained state-space dynamics are the dominant architectural factor behind its performance gains.

</details>


### [258] [Co-GLANCE: Uncertainty-Aware Active Perception for Heterogeneous Robot Teaming](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09919)
*Michal P. Podolinsky,Neel P. Bhatt,Pranay Samineni,Rohan Siva,Christian Ellis,Ufuk Topcu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Co-GLANCE 是一个实时机载感知与决策系统，用于异构机器人团队在非结构化户外环境中解决感知不确定性问题。它通过将视觉语言模型的语义推理能力蒸馏到端到端模型中，实现遮挡分割和机器人分配，避免了云端推理的延迟。系统结合置信区间预测与选择性拒绝，提供统计上有效的覆盖保证，以量化感知不确定性，并据此触发主动感知，派遣最合适的机器人获取信息丰富的视角来消除不确定性。实验表明，Co-GLANCE 在遮挡分割和机器人分配准确率上分别优于基于云的视觉语言模型基线25%和36%，同时每帧推理延迟降低350倍。研究还发布了空地协同数据集，代码、视频和数据集已公开。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出 Co-GLANCE 系统，采用知识蒸馏技术将视觉语言模型的语义推理能力压缩至轻量级端到端模型，用于遮挡分割与机器人分配；引入置信区间预测与选择性拒绝机制，对分割、分配和检测结果进行校准的不确定性量化；基于校准的不确定性自动触发主动感知，调度最优机器人获取新视角以缓解不确定性。

Result: 在真实世界场景中，Co-GLANCE 在遮挡分割准确率上比云基视觉语言模型提升25%，机器人分配准确率提升36%，每帧推理延迟降低350倍。系统具备实时性、高精度和可解释的不确定性输出，有效支持动态任务调度与主动感知。

Conclusion: Co-GLANCE 成功实现了异构机器人团队在复杂环境中的实时、可靠感知与决策，解决了感知不确定性问题。其轻量化设计与校准的不确定性估计使系统适用于机载部署，为未来自主机器人系统提供了可扩展的解决方案。

Abstract: Perceptual uncertainty is a central challenge for heterogeneous robot teams operating in unstructured outdoor environments, where no single viewpoint affords reliable scene understanding. Perceptual uncertainty, arising from sources such as occlusions, manifests differently across robot viewpoints depending on scene structure. Detecting and resolving sources of perceptual uncertainty requires both scene-based contextual reasoning and capability-aware robot allocation. While vision-language models provide strong semantic priors for both, they are computationally prohibitive for onboard inference and lack calibrated uncertainty quantification. We introduce Co-GLANCE, a real-time onboard perception and decision-making system for uncertainty resolution in heterogeneous robot teams. Co-GLANCE distills the semantic reasoning capabilities of a vision-language model into an end-to-end model for occlusion segmentation and robot allocation, eliminating the need for cloud-based inference. To quantify perceptual uncertainty, Co-GLANCE combines conformal prediction with selective abstention to provide statistically valid coverage guarantees for segmentation, robot allocation, and detection outputs. These calibrated uncertainty estimates directly trigger active perception, dispatching the most appropriate robot to acquire informative viewpoints and resolve uncertainty. Across real-world scenarios, Co-GLANCE outperforms cloud-based vision-language model baselines in occlusion segmentation and robot allocation accuracy by 25% and 36%, respectively, while reducing per-frame inference latency 350x. We also release an air-ground dataset for future research. Code, videos, and dataset available at https://co-glance.github.io/ .

### [259] [Conformal Prediction for Neural Operators: Distribution-Free Uncertainty Quantification in Physics Simulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09923)
*Michael Chin*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文首次将分割合符预测（split conformal prediction）应用于基于神经算子的物理模拟，为神经算子提供无需分布假设的预测区间，并具备有限样本覆盖保证。通过引入归一化合符预测机制，结合MC Dropout不确定性，生成空间自适应的预测区间，在低不确定性区域更紧、高不确定性区域更宽，更好地反映物理不确定性结构。实验在稳态热传导基准上验证了方法的有效性，达到89.1%的实证覆盖率（目标置信水平α=0.1），并提出不确定性分解框架，分离出68%的认知不确定性与32%的随机不确定性，指导数据收集与模型优化。代码开源，支持REST API和3D可视化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有神经算子的不确定性量化方法（如蒙特卡洛丢弃、深度集成）仅提供相对不确定性估计，缺乏形式化的覆盖率保证，难以满足安全关键工程应用的需求。因此需要一种具有严格统计保障的不确定性量化方法。

Method: 提出将分割合符预测应用于神经算子，并设计归一化合符预测方案，利用MC Dropout的不确定性信息生成自适应宽度的预测区间；同时构建不确定性分解框架，区分认知与随机不确定性。

Result: 在3370万参数、800个训练样本的稳态热传导任务中，实现89.1%的实证覆盖率（α=0.1），预测区间具有空间自适应性，能反映物理不确定性结构；认知不确定性占总不确定性68%，为模型改进提供方向。

Conclusion: 该方法首次为神经算子提供了具有有限样本覆盖保证的不确定性量化方案，具备实际部署潜力，尤其适用于安全关键型工程系统，且已开源并提供交互式可视化支持。

Abstract: Neural operators such as the Fourier Neural Operator (FNO) have emerged as powerful surrogates for solving partial differential equations (PDEs), achieving speedups of several orders of magnitude over traditional numerical solvers. However, deploying these models in safety-critical engineering applications -- such as thermal management of electronic components and battery systems -- requires not only accurate point predictions but also rigorous uncertainty guarantees. Existing uncertainty quantification (UQ) methods for neural operators, including Monte Carlo Dropout and Deep Ensembles, provide only relative uncertainty estimates without formal coverage guarantees. In this work, we propose the first application of split conformal prediction to neural operator-based physics simulation, providing distribution-free prediction intervals with finite-sample coverage guarantees. We further introduce a normalized conformal prediction scheme that leverages MC Dropout uncertainty to produce adaptive-width intervals, yielding tighter intervals in regions of low uncertainty and wider intervals where the model is less certain. Full-scale experiments (33.7M parameters, 800 training samples, 5 ensemble members, NVIDIA V100) on steady-state heat conduction benchmarks demonstrate that our method achieves 89.1% empirical coverage at the target level of alpha=0.1, while producing spatially adaptive prediction intervals that reflect the underlying physical uncertainty structure. We also provide an uncertainty decomposition framework that separates epistemic uncertainty (68% of total) from aleatoric uncertainty (32% of total), offering actionable guidance for data collection and model improvement. Our method is implemented in an open-source platform with REST API endpoints and interactive 3D visualization.

### [260] [Sigma-Branch: Hierarchical Single-Path Network Reconstruction for Dynamic Inference with Reduced Active Parameters](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09924)
*Kohga Tanaka,Hiroaki Nishi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Sigma-Branch (SigmaB) restructures pretrained dense networks into a hierarchical binary tree with shared backbone, routers, and specialized leaves, reducing per-inference active parameters by 58-60% without significant accuracy loss. It uses activation-based spherical k-means clustering for initialization and soft-routing fine-tuning to align branches with input subsets. At inference, only one root-to-leaf path is executed, minimizing off-chip weight transfer while preserving full parameter storage. Evaluated on CIFAR-100, ImageNet-1K, and ModelNet40, SigmaB outperforms static pruning methods in active-parameter reduction and maintains high accuracy.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Existing model compression techniques reduce off-chip weight transfer but incur permanent capacity loss. The key challenge is minimizing per-inference memory traffic without sacrificing model capacity or accuracy, especially on memory-constrained edge devices.

Method: SigmaB transforms a dense network into a hierarchical binary tree structure using activation-based spherical k-means clustering to distribute pretrained weights across the tree. This method jointly initializes router weights and channel allocations. Soft-routing fine-tuning aligns each leaf with its corresponding input subset. During inference, only one root-to-leaf path is activated, significantly reducing active parameters while keeping all weights stored on-chip.

Result: SigmaB reduces per-inference active parameters by 58-60% across multiple benchmarks (CIFAR-100/ResNet-50, ImageNet-1K/ResNet-50, ModelNet40/PointNet++) while maintaining Top-1 accuracy within 1.72 pp of the dense baseline. At comparable accuracy, it achieves 14-23 pp greater active-parameter reduction than static structured pruning methods like FPGM and HRank.

Conclusion: SigmaB successfully decouples per-inference memory traffic from total parameter count by enabling selective execution of a single path through a hierarchical tree structure. This approach preserves full model capacity while drastically reducing on-chip memory pressure, making it highly effective for deployment on memory-constrained edge accelerators.

Abstract: Deploying deep neural networks on memory-constrained edge accelerators is bottlenecked by per-inference off-chip weight transfer rather than computation: the dense network cannot be retained on-chip, and every parameter must be loaded for every input. Existing model compression reduces this transfer only at the cost of permanent capacity loss. We propose Sigma-Branch (SigmaB), a framework that restructures a pretrained dense network into a hierarchical binary tree composed of a shared backbone, hierarchical routers, and specialized leaves. Pretrained weights are distributed across the tree via activation-based spherical k-means clustering, which jointly initializes router weights and per-branch channel allocations; soft-routing fine-tuning then aligns each leaf with its routed input subset. At inference, the resulting network executes only a single root-to-leaf path, reducing the active-parameter footprint while storing the complete dense parameter set in memory. Across CIFAR-100 / ResNet-50, ImageNet-1K / ResNet-50, and ModelNet40 / PointNet++, SigmaB-Net reduces per-inference active parameters by 58-60% while remaining within 1.72 percentage points (pp) of the dense baseline Top-1. At comparable ImageNet-1K Top-1, the active-parameter reduction exceeds static structured pruning (FPGM, HRank) by 14-23 pp. The cross-modal evaluation, spanning 2D vision and 3D point-cloud backbones, substantiates a framework-level claim that decouples per-inference memory traffic from the total parameter count.

### [261] [Sample Where You Struggle: Sharpening Base Model Reasoning via Entropy-Guided Power Sampling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09926)
*Hong Guo,Nianhui Guo,Christoph Meinel,Haojin Yang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: EGPS是一种无需训练和验证器的采样方法，通过利用前向传播中的词元级熵来引导提议，跳过确定性块，将每次MCMC移动定位在高熵邻域，并在决策点应用多尝试梅特罗波利斯方法，使采样成本与熵质量而非序列长度成比例。在Qwen2.5-Math-7B上，EGPS在所有三个基准测试中达到最佳或并列最佳准确率（MATH500 75.8%，HumanEval 62.2%，GPQA 42.4%），相比标准MH基线最多实现12.6倍的时钟速度提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（MCMC）采样器梅特罗波利斯-哈斯廷斯（MH）在从序列级幂分布$p^α$中采样时效率低下且混合缓慢，原因在于其提议机制与分布结构不匹配：$p^α$仅在少数高熵决策点处偏离原始分布$p$，但MH均匀地在前缀上提议重采样，导致大量计算浪费在近似退化的条件上，同时在模式差异显著区域混合不足。

Method: 提出熵引导幂采样（EGPS），该方法无需训练和验证器，重新从前向传播中的词元级熵推导提议策略；跳过确定性部分，将每次MCMC移动限制在高熵邻域，并在关键决策点使用多尝试梅特罗波利斯方法，从而实现采样成本与熵质量相关而非序列长度。

Result: 在Qwen2.5-Math-7B模型上，EGPS在MATH500、HumanEval、GPQA三个基准测试中均达到最佳或并列最佳性能（分别为75.8%、62.2%、42.4%），相较于标准MH基线，最快提升达12.6倍的墙钟速度。

Conclusion: EGPS通过结构化地利用熵信息改进了采样效率，在不更新参数的情况下实现了高效推理，为基于幂采样的语言模型推理提供了高性能、低成本的新范式。

Abstract: Sampling from the sequence-level power distribution $p^α$ elicits RL-level reasoning from base language models without any parameter updates, but the standard Metropolis--Hastings (MH), a Markov Chain Monte Carlo (MCMC) sampler, is both expensive and slow-mixing. We trace both to a structural mismatch: $p^α$ mainly departs from $p$ at a sparse, spatially clustered set of high-entropy decision points, yet MH proposes resampling positions uniformly along the prefix -- wasting compute on near-degenerate conditionals while under-mixing precisely where modes diverge. We propose Entropy-Guided Power Sampling (EGPS), a training-free and verifier-free sampler that re-derives its proposal from token-level entropy already in the forward pass. EGPS skips deterministic blocks, localizes each MCMC move to a high-entropy neighborhood, and applies Multiple-Try Metropolis at decision points -- making sampling cost scale with \emph{entropy mass rather than sequence length}. On Qwen2.5-Math-7B, EGPS reaches best or tied-best accuracy on all three benchmarks (MATH500 $75.8\%$, HumanEval $62.2\%$, GPQA $42.4\%$) at up to a $12.6\times$ wall-clock speedup over the MH baseline.

</details>


### [262] [Trainable Smooth-Rotation Transforms with Learned Channel Scales for LLM Quantization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09927)
*Patrik Czakó,Gábor Kertész,Sándor Szénási*

TL;DR: 本文研究了后训练量化（PTQ）中激活量化困难的问题，发现异常值主导的通道导致大量化误差。提出一种基于分位数的鲁棒缩放策略，替代原有的基于最大值的激活统计方法，并结合约束梯度优化通道缩放。在LLaMA-3.2-1B模型W4A4量化下，仅使用分位数策略可使选定层误差降低11.1%，联合搜索（alpha, q）提升12%，训练后达18.5%。将最优选定层策略应用于所有解码器块的下投影层，全层平均误差从97.51降至78.08（降幅19.9%）。结果表明，鲁棒迁移控制与轻量级缩放学习在保持等价变换框架的同时，持续优于基于最大值的固定策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 引入分位数鲁棒缩放策略，用高分位数替代最大值作为激活统计；结合约束梯度优化进行通道缩放学习；采用联合搜索（alpha, q）以优化缩放参数。

Conclusion: 通过鲁棒迁移控制和轻量级缩放学习，分位数驱动的缩放策略显著优于传统最大值基固定策略，且在保持等价变换框架的前提下实现稳定性能提升。

Abstract: Post-training quantization (PTQ) is one of the most practical ways to reduce the serving cost of Large Language Models (LLMs), but activation quantization remains difficult because outlier-dominated channels lead to large quantization errors. This paper investigates whether part of this degradation is caused by over-migration in scaling-based equivalent transformations. We introduce a quantile-robust scaling policy for SmoothRot-style transforms by replacing max-based activation statistics with high quantiles, and we complement it with constrained gradient-based optimization of channel scales. On LLaMA-3.2-1B under W4A4 quantization, quantile-only policy search improves selected-layer error by 11.1% over the SmoothRot baseline, joint (alpha, q) search improves it by 12%, and training reaches 18.5%. Replaying the best selected-layer policy on all decoder-block down-projection layers reduces the corresponding full-layer mean error from 97.51 to 78.08 (19.9%). The results show that robust migration control and lightweight scale learning provide consistent gains over max-based fixed policies while preserving the equivalent-transform framework.

Abstract: The Forward-Forward (FF) algorithm offers a biologically inspired alternative to backpropagation by replacing gradient-based credit assignment with local, forward-only objectives. While recent extensions have adapted FF to convolutional neural networks (CNNs), existing formulations rely on static channel-class partitions and struggle to perform effectively in complex tasks. In this work, we introduce a learnable channel-class assignment mechanism that enables adaptive, data-driven specialization of convolutional channels, supported by entropy and orthogonality regularization to promote learning performance. Notably, it establishes new state-of-the-art performance among FF-based models, substantially narrowing the gap with backpropagation. ### [264] [Between Amnesia and Chaos: A Memory Stability Expressivity Trilemma for Trainable Dissipative Oscillator Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09929)
*Caleb Munigety*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了物理储层计算中非线性振荡器网络的端到端可训练性，发现记忆时长、梯度稳定性和动态表达能力三者不可同时最大化，均受阻尼影响。梯度反向传播速率由阻尼决定，前向敏感性随最大李雅普诺夫指数指数增长，导致可用梯度需在阻尼高于稳定阈值时才存在。随着阻尼增加，李雅普诺夫指数下降，记忆上限降低，稳定训练仅存在于一个随时长收缩并最终闭合的带状区域。实验验证了该理论：在20振子网络上，阻尼扫面显示李雅普诺夫指数单调变化并在确定阈值处过零，符合核心假设；在九个延迟回忆时长下对比学习与冻结底座，学习底座在短时长占优，优势在11步时消失甚至逆转，符合理论预测的带闭合特征。训练模型自发趋近稳定阈值，探索混沌边缘。分析上限高估实测交叉点约五倍，揭示可检测与可学习梯度间的差距。贡献在于明确何时训练物理底座优于冻结它。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统物理储层计算将基底冻结，仅训练线性读出，认为基底不可有效训练。本文挑战这一前提，探索非线性振荡器网络中质量、阻尼和刚度是否可通过端到端学习提升性能，旨在揭示训练物理基底的条件与边界。

Method: 采用辛积分器实现非线性振荡器网络的端到端训练，通过分析梯度传播特性、李雅普诺夫指数与阻尼关系，建立三者之间的权衡模型。实验在20振子网络上进行，包括阻尼扫描与延迟回忆任务的计算匹配比较，验证理论预测。

Result: 实验表明，学习底座在短记忆时长下表现更优，但优势在约11步时消失并反转，对应理论预测的稳定训练带闭合点。训练模型自然收敛至稳定阈值附近，呈现对混沌边缘的自发探索。理论预测的上限比实际观测值高约五倍，反映出可检测与可学习梯度之间的本质差距。

Conclusion: 训练物理基底并非总优于冻结它，其有效性受限于记忆时长、梯度稳定性与动态表达能力之间的内在权衡。该权衡由阻尼主导，稳定训练仅存在于特定带状区间，且随记忆时长增长而收缩。本研究提供了明确判断何时应训练基底的理论依据。

Abstract: Physical reservoir computing harnesses nonlinear mechanical dynamics but, by convention, freezes the substrate and trains only a linear readout, presuming the substrate is not usefully trainable. We revisit that premise for networks of nonlinear oscillators whose mass, damping, and stiffness are learned end-to-end through a symplectic integrator. Our central result is a trilemma: memory horizon, gradient stability, and dynamical expressivity cannot be simultaneously maximized, because all three are governed by the damping. The backward gradient decays at a rate set by the damping, capping how far back credit can propagate, while forward sensitivities grow exponentially in the largest Lyapunov exponent, so usable gradients require damping above a stability floor. Since the Lyapunov exponent falls as damping rises while the memory ceiling falls as the horizon grows, stable training is confined to a band that contracts with horizon and closes at a critical point. We test every step on a twenty-oscillator network. A damping sweep finds the largest Lyapunov exponent monotone and crossing zero at a well-defined stability floor, confirming the theorem's key assumption. A compute-matched comparison of learned versus frozen substrate on delayed recall across nine horizons shows the learned substrate dominating at short horizons and the advantage closing and reversing near a horizon of eleven steps, the predicted signature of band closure; trained models settle near the stability floor, seeking the edge of chaos unprompted. The analytic ceiling overestimates the empirical crossover roughly fivefold, a gap between detectable and learnable gradient that we report rather than tune away. The contribution is a confirmed account of when training a physical substrate beats freezing it.

</details>


### [265] [When RL Fails after SFT: Rejuvenating Model Plasticity for Robust SFT-to-RL Handoff](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09932)
*Runze Liu,Jiashun Liu,Xu Wan,Yuqian Fu,Ling Pan*

TL;DR: 本文研究了大语言模型在经过过度监督微调（SFT）后，强化学习（RL）阶段性能提升有限的问题。作者发现过度SFT会导致模型可塑性下降，表现为输出分布过于自信、参数空间陡峭，从而阻碍后续RL优化。为此，提出名为\texttt{Rejuvenation}的方法，通过基于基础模型的融合与选择性神经元重置，恢复模型可塑性并保留SFT获得的有效先验知识。实验表明，该方法在数学推理和代理任务中均显著提升了过训练SFT模型的RL表现，并增强了对分布外任务的泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索为何过度监督微调（SFT）后的模型在后续强化学习（RL）阶段难以进一步提升性能，识别其根本原因在于模型可塑性的丧失。

Method: \texttt{Rejuvenation}：结合基线模型融合以减少过度SFT带来的参数漂移，并通过选择性神经元重置来缓解模型僵化，从而恢复模型在RL阶段的优化能力。

Result: 在数学推理和代理任务上，\texttt{Rejuvenation}显著提升了过训练SFT模型的强化学习表现，并增强了模型在分布外任务上的泛化能力。

Conclusion: 过度SFT会降低模型可塑性，限制后续强化学习的优化潜力；提出的\texttt{Rejuvenation}方法能有效恢复模型可塑性，在保持已有先验知识的同时实现更优的SFT-to-RL过渡。

Abstract: Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) followed by Reinforcement Learning (RL) has become a standard pipeline for Large Language Model (LLM) post-training. SFT is expected to provide a useful behavioral prior for RL to further enhance model capabilities. However, checkpoints with excessive SFT often show limited improvement during RL. We attribute this failure to the loss of model plasticity: the reduced ability of an SFT-initialized policy to be effectively reshaped by subsequent RL. To better understand this phenomenon, we conduct detailed analysis from multiple perspectives, including parameter changes, output spaces, and RL optimization dynamics. Our results show that models from excessive SFT tend to produce over-confident token distributions and exhibit sharp parameter landscapes, which make them harder to optimize in the RL stage. To enable a more robust SFT-to-RL handoff, we propose \texttt{Rejuvenation}, a simple yet effective method that restores plasticity while preserving useful SFT-acquired priors. Rejuvenation leverages base-anchored model fusion to reduce excessive SFT-induced drift with targeted neuron reset to mitigate model rigidity. Experimental results on both math reasoning tasks and agentic tasks demonstrate that our approach consistently improves RL performance on over-trained SFT models, while also enhancing generalization to out-of-distribution tasks.

### [266] [nCMD: Benign-Anchored Feature Selection for Imbalanced Network Intrusion Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09934)

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为nCMD的轻量级、可解释的特征选择方法，通过衡量攻击类分布相对于良性类均值的偏差来评分特征相关性，从而更好地适应入侵检测中攻击作为良性流量偏离的特性。在四个基准数据集上，nCMD在多种特征预算和分类器下表现优于或匹配传统方法，尤其在资源受限和严重类别不平衡场景下效果显著。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统过滤方法使用对称计算的全局统计量进行特征排序，无法捕捉入侵检测中攻击与良性流量之间的不对称性；而实际中攻击是相对于主导的良性流量的异常，因此需要一种更符合操作语义的特征选择方法。

Method: 提出良性锚定的逐类均值偏差（nCMD）方法，基于攻击类分布与良性类均值之间的偏差来评估特征重要性，不依赖全局参考，具有低计算开销和高可解释性。

Abstract: Feature selection is critical for network intrusion detection systems (NIDS) operating under high-dimensional, highly imbalanced traffic, as found in operational and defense networks. Traditional filter methods rank features using global statistics computed symmetrically across classes and thus fail to capture the asymmetry of intrusion detection, where attacks are best characterized as deviations from dominant benign traffic.
  We propose benign-anchored Classwise Mean Deviation (nCMD), a lightweight and interpretable method that scores feature relevance based on the deviation of attack-class distributions from the benign-class mean, rather than a globally biased reference. This approach aligns feature selection with the operational semantics of NIDS at no additional computational cost.
  Across four benchmark datasets (CICIDS2017, CICDDoS2019, NSL-KDD, and UNSW-NB15), multiple feature budgets, and three downstream classifiers, nCMD matches or exceeds classical filter baselines in macro-averaged F1-score. These results support benign-anchored ranking as a scalable and interpretable preprocessing component for resource-constrained NIDS.

*Bhavith Chandra Challagundla,Sanskar Pandey,Param Thakkar,Rishikesh Mallagundla,Yugandhar Reddy Gogireddy,Wenhao Lu,Hindol Roy Choudhury,Shravani Challagundla,Mohamed Deraz Nasr,Spursh Deshpande*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有可解释性方法（如探针、激活修补、稀疏自编码器）在不同模型上重复实现，因工具链假设为仅限于变压器语言模型，缺乏对动作、环境步数和想象回放的支持，导致碎片化。

Method: 设计一个能力类型化的适配器接口，要求所有模型实现encode、transition、initial state、sample四个必需方法，并通过显式能力描述符声明可选头（decode、reward、continue、actor、critic），从而统一处理强化学习与自监督世界模型。

Conclusion: 世界模型的共享结构可通过小而强的类型接口表达，工具链的统一能显著提升可解释性研究效率，避免重复开发。

Abstract: World models are now built on substantially different computational substrates. Latent recurrent state-space models such as PlaNet and the Dreamer family compress observations into recurrent states; token-based models such as IRIS quantize observations into a learned codebook and predict autoregressively with a transformer; and joint-embedding predictive architectures such as I-JEPA predict in a learned latent space with no pixel decoder. The interpretability methods applied to these models, including probing, activation patching, sparse autoencoders, and surprise analysis, share a common set of primitives, yet they are re-implemented from scratch for each architecture because existing hook-and-cache tooling assumes a transformer language model with no notion of actions, environment steps, or imagined rollouts. We argue that this fragmentation reflects the tooling rather than the models, and that the shared structure of world models is captured by a small typed interface. We present WorldModelLens, an open-source interpretability substrate organized around a capability-typed adapter: every model implements four required methods (encode, transition, initial state, sample) and declares a set of optional heads (decode, reward, continue, actor, critic) through an explicit capability descriptor, so that reinforcement-learning and self-supervised world models are first-class without either imitating the other. A single hook and cache layer exposes time-indexed activations, imagination rollouts, and intervention replay over this interface, allowing each analysis to be written once.

### [268] [RKSC: Reasoning-Aware KV Cache Sharing and Confident Early Exit for Multi-Step LLM Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09937)
*Anirudh Sekar*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: RKSC是一种无需训练的推理框架，通过消除多分支大语言模型推理流水线中的两种结构性冗余，显著提升推理效率。它包含三个核心组件：ASKS利用隐藏状态余弦相似性共享前缀键值缓存，超越传统token精确匹配；CGEE基于置信度和层熵稳定性的双重退出机制，减少验证计算；RSBCM通过注意力加权深度优先淘汰策略防止缓存无限制增长。在五个模型家族、四个基准测试和1000个问题上，RKSC平均提速3.008倍（峰值3.990倍），相比vLLM等价前缀缓存提升1.66倍，且仅引入0.37%的错误率（1616次验证中仅6次出错）。无需微调或架构修改，代码已开源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多分支大语言模型推理中存在前缀缓存重复与验证计算冗余，导致推理效率低下。现有方法如vLLM和SGLang依赖于严格的token精确匹配，无法有效利用语义相似性，且缺乏灵活的早期退出机制，难以应对不同分支间的动态变化。因此亟需一种无需训练、可通用部署的高效推理优化框架。

Method: RKSC由三部分构成：(1) ASKS通过计算隐藏状态的余弦相似性，将前缀键值缓存广播至语义相似的分支，实现更广泛的有效缓存共享；(2) CGEE设计双机制：当各分支生成置信度一致时跳过验证前向传播；当每层熵趋于稳定时，在中间层提前终止验证过程，利用轻量级钩子嵌入Transformer主干；(3) RSBCM采用注意力加权机制进行深度优先的缓存块淘汰，避免缓存无限增长。整体方案无需模型微调或结构改动。

Result: 在五种模型（7B-10B）、四个基准和1000个问题上，RKSC相较无缓存基线平均提速3.008倍（最高达3.990倍），相比vLLM等价前缀缓存提升1.66倍。使用CGEE带来的错误率为0.37%（1616次验证中仅6次出错），表明其高可靠性。整个框架无需任何训练或架构修改，具备极强实用性与通用性。

Conclusion: RKSC成功实现了对多分支大语言模型推理中结构性冗余的系统性消除，通过语义感知缓存共享、智能早期退出与自适应缓存管理，在不改变模型的前提下大幅提升了推理速度与效率，为大规模语言模型的实际部署提供了高效、通用且可靠的新范式。

Abstract: We introduce RKSC (Reasoning-Aware KV Cache Sharing), a training-free inference framework that eliminates two structural redundancies in multi-branch LLM reasoning pipelines. ASKS (Attention-Similarity KV Sharing) computes the prefix KV cache once and broadcasts it to all semantically similar branches via hidden-state cosine similarity, strictly generalising the token-exact prefix caching used by vLLM and SGLang. CGEE (Confidence-Gated Early Exit) applies two complementary exit mechanisms: (1) it skips the verification forward pass entirely when generation confidence is decisive across branches, and (2) it terminates the verification pass at an intermediate layer when per-layer entropy stabilises, using lightweight hooks on the transformer backbone. RSBCM (Reasoning-Selective Block Cache Manager) prevents unbounded cache growth via attention-weighted depth-priority eviction. Across five model families (7B-10B), four benchmarks, and 1,000 evaluated problems, RKSC achieves a mean speedup of 3.008x over the No-KV baseline (peak 3.990x), a 1.66x mean improvement over vLLM-equivalent prefix caching, with a CGEE-induced error rate of only 0.37% (6 errors out of 1,616 verify calls). No fine-tuning or architecture changes are required. Code is available at https://github.com/AnirudhSekar/RKSC.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有字典学习方法（如稀疏自编码器和交叉编码器）在解释模型时依赖于独立特征分解，但特征间的交互会导致重构误差。本文旨在形式化这一现象，并提供一种量化特征交互的新方法，以改进模型解释性和效率。

Method: 通过构建紧凑证明，形式化交叉编码器中特征交互引起的误差项；推导出MLP层中特征交互项的显式表达式；利用该交互项设计可微分损失惩罚，实现计算稀疏性；并基于交互度量进行聚类与异常检测。

Abstract: Dictionary learning methods like Sparse Autoencoders (SAEs) and crosscoders attempt to explain a model by decomposing its activations into independent features. Interactions between features hence induce errors in the reconstruction. We formalize this intuition via compact proofs and make five contributions. First, we show how, \textit{in principle}, a compact proof of model performance can be constructed using a crosscoder. Second, we show that an error term arising in this proof can naturally be interpreted as a measure of interaction between crosscoder features and provide an explicit expression for the interaction term in the Multi-Layer Perceptron (MLP) layers. We then provide three applications of this new interaction measure. In our third contribution we show that the interaction term itself can be used as a differentiable loss penalty. Applying this penalty, we can achieve ``computationally sparse'' crosscoders that retain $60\%$ of MLP performance when only keeping a single feature at each datapoint and neuron, compared to $10\%$ in standard crosscoders. We then show that clustering according to our interaction measure provides semantically meaningful feature clusters, and finally that sleeper agents have significant interactions. Code is available at https://github.com/chainik1125/crosscoders-feature-interactions/tree/arxiv.

### [270] [Learning Where to Simulate: Generative Active Sampling for Online PDE Surrogate Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09949)

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出在线生成主动采样（OGAS）方法，通过结合扩散模型与代理模型，根据预测难度动态调整数据采样分布，显著提升复杂偏微分方程（PDE）场景下的代理模型泛化性能，尤其在高误差尾部表现上大幅降低极端错误和误差方差，且几乎不增加计算时间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统均匀采样难以覆盖具有挑战性动力学的PDE配置，导致代理模型在复杂情形下预测误差大、方差高；而在线训练虽具优势，但缺乏高效采样策略以聚焦困难样本。

Method: 引入OGAS，利用并行训练的快速扩散模型作为条件采样器，将代理模型输出的难度信号（如损失或不确定性）映射回配置参数，主动从高难度先验中采样，实现对数据生成的实时引导。

Abstract: Data-driven PDE surrogates are trained with data produced by numerical PDE solvers. However, when the surrogate's goal is to generalize across a wide range of PDE configurations (e.g., initial conditions and physical coefficients), generating a representative training set is non-trivial. Uniform sampling of configuration parameters often under-represents trajectories exhibiting challenging dynamics, leading to high prediction errors and large error variance in the trained surrogate. Online training, where data generation and surrogate training are coupled, offers a natural advantage by allowing solver parameters to be steered on-the-fly. To efficiently exploit this capability, we introduce Online Generative Active Sampling (OGAS), an active learning method that reactively learns the relationship between configuration parameters and surrogate performance to control the sampling distribution. OGAS trains a fast diffusion model in parallel to the surrogate to act as a conditional sampler, mapping a surrogate-derived difficulty signal (e.g., loss or uncertainty) to configuration parameters. By actively drawing target signals from a prior biased toward high difficulty, OGAS continuously steers data generation toward challenging regimes without delaying the training workflow. We evaluate OGAS across 2D PDEs with distinct challenging dynamics (Kuramoto-Sivashinsky, Navier-Stokes, Gray-Scott) and up to 308 parameters, using multiple surrogate architectures. Across all settings, OGAS consistently improves tail statistics, yielding substantial reductions in errors above the 99th percentile and overall error dispersion compared to uniform sampling. While prioritizing challenging trajectories introduces a trade-off with average error, OGAS effectively ensures worst-case reliability of trained surrogates with negligible wall-time overhead.

### [271] [Integrating Out, Twice:The Open-System Case That Neural-Network Ensemble Theory Is Missing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09950)
*Jin Lei*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过分析神经网络参数平均与高斯块的消去操作在数学上等价于施尔补（Schur complement），揭示了闭合情况下的网络集成本质是协方差及其逆。作者将该框架与核反应理论中的开放系统类比，提出开放情况需具备连续谱和波状动力学特征，而主流机器学习模型多为有限或耗散系统，不满足此条件。实验测试表明，开放情形下虽有守恒通量记录，但其内容缺失或受训练目标压制，不确定性主要存在于闭合侧。结论是：当前方法在开放系统建模中存在结构性缺陷，核心价值在于厘清这一局限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究神经网络集成与高斯过程之间的深层联系，特别是闭合与开放系统的数学对应关系；揭示现有方法在处理真正开放系统时的结构性不足。

Method: 基于分布矩、高斯代数与分块矩阵求逆，构建闭合系统的完整映射字典；将核反应理论中的开放系统框架引入机器学习，对比分析封闭与开放情形下的行为差异。

Result: 在截断注意力图、令牌级转移算子和稀疏专家路由器上的测试均得负面结果；开放情形下的守恒量虽可追踪，但其物理内容缺失或被人为分区或训练目标所抑制；实际有用的不确定性仍来自闭合侧。

Conclusion: 当前主流学习模型缺乏开放系统所需的连续谱与波状动态，导致无法有效实现真正的开放建模；该研究的核心发现是‘负一’——即开放性建模的结构性失败，其价值在于精准定位这一局限。

Abstract: Averaging a neural network over its random parameters and marginalizing a Gaussian sector are the same operation, the Schur complement of the eliminated block, and when that block is closed it returns a covariance and its inverse. That is all a network ensemble produces, the closed case. The open case is missing, and nuclear reaction theory has it worked out. Projecting a scattering problem onto a chosen set of channels, with the rest carrying probability irreversibly to a continuum, leaves a non-Hermitian effective generator that conserves and itemizes exactly what it loses: the nuclear optical model and its generalized optical theorem. I set the two cases side by side using only the moments of a distribution, the algebra of Gaussians, and block inversion, no field theory, and give the closed-case dictionary in full: the neural tangent kernel is the Fisher sensitivity kernel, the infinite-width Gaussian limit is the Gaussian-process emulator, and the lazy-to-feature transition is the validity boundary of a reduced-basis emulator. I then test the open export on a truncated attention map, a token-level transfer operator, and a sparse expert router, and report a mostly negative result. The conserved flux ledger ports wherever openness is genuinely present, but its distinctive content is absent, an artifact of the chosen partition, or pinned near a floor by the training objective, and the operationally useful uncertainty turns out to be epistemic, living in the closed half of the correspondence, not the open one. The negative has a structural reason this note makes precise: the open case needs an eliminated sector with a continuous spectrum and wave-like, not relaxational, dynamics, which mainstream learning's finite or dissipative objects do not supply. This is a note, not a result; its main finding is that negative one, and its value is the map that locates it.

</details>


### [272] [Hasse Diagrams for Attention: A Partial Order Framework for Designing Transformer Masks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09951)
*Chentao Li,Han Guo*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一个完整的理论框架，用于分析大Transformer模型中任意注意力掩码引起的信息流结构。研究证明，随着网络深度增加，多层Transformer的信息流会收敛到一个偏序集的哈斯图（Hasse diagram），即有向无环图。基于此，将并行训练任务的设计问题转化为寻找多个哈斯图的最小公共超图，并建立最小公共超图的标准。该框架可直接从任务族推导出注意力掩码。应用该框架，设计了两种新型掩码：保证训练-推理一致性的块生成注意力掩码（Block Two-Stream Attention）和全监督双向注意力掩码（Butterfly Attention）。结果表明该框架具备发现新结构的能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有注意力掩码种类繁多，尽管如FlexAttention等工具支持任意掩码，但缺乏对任意掩码所引发信息流结构的系统性理论分析。因此亟需一种统一的理论框架来理解并指导掩码设计。

Method: 通过形式化建模多层Transformer中的信息流路径，证明其在足够深度下收敛为哈斯图；将并行训练任务设计问题转化为多个哈斯图的最小公共超图构造问题，并给出判定准则；利用该准则反向设计具体注意力掩码。

Result: 成功构建了信息流的理论框架，提出了最小公共超图的判定标准，并据此设计出两种新型注意力掩码——Block Two-Stream Attention 和 Butterfly Attention，验证了框架的有效性和创新性。

Conclusion: 该理论框架为理解与设计复杂注意力结构提供了坚实基础，不仅揭示了信息流的本质结构，还实现了从任务需求到掩码设计的自动化推导，推动了Transformer架构的可解释性与可控性发展。

Abstract: During the training of large Transformer models, attention masks regulate the scope and direction of information flow across a sequence. Numerous mask variants exist, and operators such as FlexAttention already support arbitrary attention masks. Nevertheless, a systematic formal analysis of the information-flow structure induced by arbitrary masks has been missing. This paper develops a complete theoretical framework. We prove that, with sufficient depth, the information flow of a multi-layer Transformer converges to a Hasse diagram -- a directed acyclic graph representing a partial order. Building on this, we recast the design of parallel training tasks as the problem of finding a minimal common supergraph of Hasse diagrams, and we establish a criterion for the minimal common supergraph. This yields a constructive method to derive attention masks directly from a family of tasks. Applying the framework, we design two novel masks: a block-generation attention mask that ensures training-inference consistency (Block Two-Stream Attention), and a fully supervised bidirectional attention mask (Butterfly Attention). These results demonstrate the framework's capacity to discover new structures.

Method: 通过实验评估不同归一化策略在基于Transformer的大时间序列模型中的表现，采用分块和高效因果训练策略，并分析其对训练收敛性和预测性能的影响。

Result: 研究发现，归一化策略的选择对模型的训练收敛性和最终的预测性能有显著影响，某些策略在避免信息泄露的同时能提升模型表现。

Conclusion: 合适的归一化策略对于提升大时间序列模型在非平稳数据上的预测性能至关重要，应根据具体训练架构谨慎选择。

Abstract: Large models for time-series forecasting have been emerged as a promising paradigm for training models on heterogeneous collections of signals. However, in efficient causal settings it might induce information leakage from future observations during training. Recent alternatives, including causal normalization and statistics computed from initial observations, have been proposed to address this issue, but their practical implications remain insufficiently understood. In this work, we evaluate normalization strategies for transformer-based large time-series models trained with patching and efficient causal strategy. We showcase that normalization choice significantly influences both training convergence and forecasting performance.

This paper investigates whether lightweight temporal context can improve radar-based nowcasting, particularly for high-intensity rainfall. Experiments on KNMI radar precipitation data show that temporal conditioning is most beneficial for rare, high-intensity precipitation events, while also improving the representation of seasonal variability and predicted rainfall-intensity distributions. A layer conductance analysis further indicates that the added temporal conditioning layers are actively used by the model despite their small parameter cost. These findings suggest that simple, physically motivated temporal context can improve the realism and reliability of deep learning-based precipitation nowcasts. The implementation of our models and training setup is available on \href{https://github.com/gijsvn/TA-SmaAt-UNet}{GitHub}.

### [275] [HydraCIL: Decoupled Class-Incremental Learning through Prototype-Guided Multi-Head Classifiers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09960)
*Daniel Vila-Cruz,Laura Morán-Fernández,Verónica Bolón-Canedo*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: HydraCIL is a lightweight, decoupled continual learning model using prototype-guided multi-head classifiers, enabling fast adaptation and low resource usage in embedded systems. It avoids backbone retraining by freezing the feature extractor and creating task-specific heads, achieving competitive performance with reduced training time and carbon footprint.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Real-world applications like robots and edge AI devices require quick, energy-efficient continual learning with limited computational resources, yet most existing Class-Incremental Learning (CIL) methods demand high-end hardware and long retraining cycles, limiting their practicality.

Method: HydraCIL decouples feature extraction from learning by freezing the backbone. For each new task, it extracts features once and builds a lightweight, task-specific classifier head. At inference, the appropriate head is selected based on similarity to learned prototypes.

Result: HydraCIL achieves performance comparable or superior to state-of-the-art CIL methods on CIFAR-100, ImageNet-100, CoRe50, and Flowers102, while drastically reducing training time and energy consumption.

Conclusion: HydraCIL offers a practical, efficient, and sustainable solution for continual learning in resource-constrained environments, enabling rapid adaptation with minimal computational overhead.

Abstract: We present HydraCIL, a decoupled continual learning model based on prototype-guided multi-head classifiers, targeting sustainable deployment in embedded and resource-constrained environments. While most Class-Incremental Learning (CIL) methods rely on powerful hardware and long retraining cycles, real-world systems, such as robots or edge AI devices, must adapt quickly with limited resources. HydraCIL addresses this gap by freezing the backbone and decoupling feature extraction from learning. For each task, features are extracted once and a lightweight, task-specific classifier head is created, avoiding costly backbone retraining. At inference, HydraCIL selects the appropriate head via similarity with prototypes. Experiments on CIFAR-100, ImageNet-100, CoRe50, and Flowers102 datasets show that HydraCIL matches or outperforms state-of-the-art CIL methods while significantly reducing training time and carbon footprint, making it a practical solution for continual learning in real-world and embedded settings, where energy efficiency and rapid adaptation are critical.

*Yu Han,Kailing Li,Yang Jiao,Yulin Dai,Yuqian Fu,Linhai Zhuo,Tianwen Qian*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有强化学习算法在多轮智能体场景中因奖励稀疏、延迟且缺乏步骤级信用分配机制，导致性能受限，亟需更精细的策略优化方法。

Method: 提出3SPO，基于历史成功率计算状态得分，动态监督每步信用分配，实现无需价值函数估计或额外辅助模型的后步策略优化与自适应回放。

Result: 在ALFWorld上比GRPO提升22.6%，在WebShop上提升15.6点，探索量提高2.4倍，收敛速度加快1.8倍，资源消耗相当。

Abstract: Training large language models (LLMs) as autonomous agents via reinforcement learning (RL) has enabled frontier models to achieve superhuman performance in long-horizon tasks. However, existing RL algorithms operate at the trajectory level, performing policy optimization only after collecting complete episode rollouts. This coarse-grained approach faces fundamental challenges in multi-turn agent settings where rewards are sparse, delayed, and credit assignment across individual steps is critical. In this work, we propose \textbf{State-Score-Supervised Policy Optimization (3SPO)}, a novel RL algorithm that performs post-step policy optimization with dynamic state score supervision. At each step, 3SPO computes the state score based on historical success rates, supervising step-wise credit assignment, adaptive rollout and post-step policy optimization without requiring value function estimation or additional auxiliary models. Theoretically, under a per-state bandit abstraction, we show that the proposed score-supervised allocation mechanism achieves logarithmic allocation regret and provide sample-complexity guarantees for action identification, score distinguishability, and filtering stability. Experiments on ALFWorld and WebShop with Qwen2.5-1.5B/7B-Instruct show that 3SPO consistently outperforms GRPO by $+22.6\%$ on ALFWorld and $+15.6$ points on WebShop, while using comparable resources to achieve $2.4\times$ more state exploration and $1.8\times$ faster convergence. Code is available at https://github.com/genalyu/3SPO.

Abstract: Continuous diffusion for categorical data is a framework belonging to the diffusion family and aiming at generating discrete data. The scientific interest to such models has been constantly increasing these days because researchers try to achieve a challenging goal of finding reasonable alternatives to autoregressive large language models. In this paper, we study the properties of the structure of the latent space corresponding to discrete tokens expressed in terms of Kullback-Leibler divergence on diffusion path measures and accuracy of the correct token prediction by the optimally trained diffusion model. We find that FSQ tokenization scheme has the latent space structure with the properties that make it best suited for continuous diffusion for categorical data as verified through rigorous theoretical analysis and numerical experiments. To validate our findings in real-life scenario, we train several text-to-speech diffusion models having speech tokens as intermediate acoustic features, and show that the one based on FSQ tokens indeed performs the best, and, moreover, it outperforms its strong LLM-based counterpart, at the same time being significantly smaller and faster.

SAE features thus serve both as interpretability objects and as control directions for TTS synthesis.
