### [365] [Encoding the Euler Characteristic Transform](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10824)
*Nello Blaser,Odin Hoff Gardaa,Lars M. Salbu,Elena Xinyi Wang,Bastian Rieck*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种连续编码的欧拉特征变换（ECT）方法，通过记录每个顶点在不同方向上的净欧拉特征变化，生成方向相关的令牌序列，并使用小型Transformer将其映射为特征向量。该方法将流程分为两个阶段：每个方向内的ECC编码器和跨方向的ECT表示层。在六个分类基准上，连续编码在五个数据集上提升了准确率，且性能提升主要归因于编码方式而非模型容量。表示架构的影响小于编码方式，而其优势依赖于编码形式：连续编码下前馈网络表现最佳，但在离散化下不如卷积架构稳健。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统ECT编码依赖于对ECC的离散化，存在信息损失和不灵活的问题。为提升形状描述的表达能力与灵活性，需要一种更精细、连续的编码方式，以更好地融入神经网络并保留几何结构的内在对称性。

Method: 提出一种连续编码策略，基于每个方向上各顶点对欧拉特征变化的贡献，构建方向相关的令牌序列；采用小型Transformer处理序列并生成固定长度的特征向量；设计两阶段框架：方向内编码（ECC encoder）与方向间聚合（ECT representation）；对比多种架构（前馈、卷积、复数域等）评估其性能差异。

Result: 在六个不同类型的基准数据集（点云、图、立方体复形、网格）上，连续编码在五项任务中显著提升分类准确率；控制实验表明性能提升主要源于编码方式本身，而非额外的Transformer容量；前馈网络在连续编码下表现最优，但离散化时稳定性较差；卷积与复数模型在离散化下更具鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 连续编码显著优于传统离散化编码，是提升ECT性能的关键因素；表示架构的选择应与编码方式相匹配，连续编码更适用于结构无关的前馈模型，而离散化更适合具有等变性的复杂架构。

Abstract: The Euler Characteristic Curve (ECC) records the Euler characteristic of a linearly embedded cell complex as a function of filtration height in a given direction, and the Euler Characteristic Transform (ECT) is the injective shape descriptor obtained by collecting ECCs over many directions. How the ECT is encoded for a neural network is itself an inductive bias, conventionally fixed by discretizing each ECC. We introduce a continuous encoding: for each direction and each vertex it records the net Euler-characteristic change attributed to that vertex, producing a per-direction token sequence that a small transformer maps to a feature vector. We separate the resulting pipeline into two stages on orthogonal axes: an ECC encoder that acts within each direction, mapping its curve to a fixed-length vector, and an ECT representation that acts across directions, aggregating the per-direction vectors into one. We study six ECT representation architectures spanning a range of inductive biases, from a structure-agnostic feedforward baseline to convolutional and complex-valued models that preserve equivariance under planar rotations. Across six classification benchmarks covering point clouds, graphs, cubical complexes, and meshes, the continuous encoding improves accuracy on five of six datasets, and control experiments attribute the gain to the tokenization itself rather than to the added transformer capacity. The representation architecture matters less than the encoding, and the payoff from its inductive biases depends on the encoding: a feedforward network performs best under continuous encoding but is less robust under discretization than convolutional architectures.

</details>


### [366] [MODIP: Efficient Model-Based Optimization for Diffusion Policies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10825)
*Zakariae El Asri,Philippe Gratias-Quiquandon,Nicolas Thome,Olivier Sigaud*

TL;DR: MODIP 是一种用于扩散策略（DP）从离线到在线微调的框架，通过世界模型（WM）引导策略适应，利用模型预测控制（MPC）生成高质量轨迹作为监督目标进行微调。该方法采用终端状态价值替代依赖策略的状态-动作值以提升效率，并使用独立于策略的TD目标训练评价网络，从而减少推理和训练时间。在D4RL（MuJoCo, Kitchen）和RoboMimic任务上，MODIP显著优于行为克隆（BC），并达到或超越现有基于强化学习的扩散策略微调方法及强大的基于模型基线如TD-MPC2。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: MODIP 利用世界模型生成高质轨迹，通过模型预测控制（MPC）规划并以终端状态价值降低计算开销；同时采用政策无关的TD目标训练评论家，提升训练效率。

Abstract: Diffusion policies (DPs) have emerged as expressive policy representations for robot learning, often used with imitation learning methods such as behavioral cloning (BC). However, while their success has largely been confined to BC, direct reinforcement learning (RL) fine-tuning remains challenging because actions are generated through a multi-step denoising process. In this work, we propose MODIP, a framework for the offline-to-online fine-tuning of DPs. Rather than directly applying RL to the DPs, MODIP leverages a world model (WM) to guide policy adaptation and keeps the simplicity and stability of BC. We utilize model predictive control (MPC) to generate high-quality trajectories within the WM, and use them as supervised targets for fine-tuning the DP. To make MPC planning efficient, MODIP uses a terminal state value instead of a policy-dependent state-action value, reducing inference time. Additionally, MODIP trains critics with policy-independent TD targets, reducing training time. Experiments on D4RL (MuJoCo, Kitchen) and RoboMimic tasks show that MODIP improves diffusion policies beyond BC, and is competitive with or outperforms diffusion policy RL fine-tuning methods and strong model-based baselines such as TD-MPC2.

### [367] [Geometrically Averaged Hard Target Updates for Linear Q-Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10835)
*Donghwan Lee*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出并分析了一种称为$\lambda$-target update的新型目标更新机制，通过几何加权平均$m$-周期目标更新映射，实现了从单周期更新到投影Q值迭代的平滑过渡。该方法在基于线性函数逼近的Q学习（即线性Q学习）中被研究，使用切换系统模型及相关工具进行分析。尽管论文以确定性版本为例，但其框架可推广至随机强化学习场景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有深度Q学习中的周期性目标更新虽能提升稳定性，但缺乏对更新机制的深入分析与优化。本文旨在提出一种更灵活、连续的目标更新策略，以改善线性Q学习的收敛性与稳定性。

Method: 采用切换系统模型分析$\lambda$-target update机制，结合几何权重$(1-\lambda)\lambda^{m-1}$对多周期目标更新进行加权平均，构建连续参数化的更新路径，并在确定性环境下进行理论分析。

Result: 所提出的$\lambda$-target update机制在理论上表现出良好的稳定性，能够实现从快速更新（$\lambda=0$）到慢速投影迭代（$\lambda \uparrow 1$）的平稳过渡，且在线性Q学习中具有收敛保证。

Conclusion: $\lambda$-target update为深度Q学习中的目标更新提供了新的连续化视角，增强了算法的灵活性与稳定性，为未来设计更鲁棒的强化学习算法提供了理论支持。

Abstract: Periodic hard target updates are among the most common stabilization devices in modern deep Q-learning. Recent studies suggest that target updates can improve stability in Q-learning with function approximation, including linear function approximation. We introduce and analyze the so-called $λ$-target update, obtained by averaging the $m$-periodic target update maps with $λ$-geometric weights $(1-λ)λ^{m-1}$, $λ\in [0,1]$. The endpoint $λ=0$ recovers the one-period target update, while the continuous endpoint $λ\uparrow1$ recovers projected Q-value iteration. We study this mechanism for Q-learning with linear function approximation, namely linear Q-learning, using a switching-system model and related tools. For clarity, the paper treats a deterministic version; the formulation extends to stochastic reinforcement-learning settings.

### [368] [When Do Autoregressive Sequence Models Forecast Physical Wavefields? A Controlled Study on Synthetic Seismograms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10868)
*Waleed Esmail,Stuart Russell,Jana Klinge,Alexander Kappes,Christine Thomas*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了在长时序自回归预测中，针对振荡物理信号（如地震波形、引力波应变）的误差累积问题，通过合成三成分地震波形作为测试基准，分析SeismoGPT模型在自由滚动预测中的稳定性。研究表明，多标记预测是主要稳定因素，显著优于单标记基线；此外，时序嵌入混合预测头和跨时序STFT幅度一致性损失也带来小幅但持续的改进。性能对上下文比例阈值极为敏感，接近一个（即信号的完整P-S波段）时表现最佳，低于此阈值则泛化能力崩溃。主要残余失败为极性反转，而基于幅度的谱损失无法纠正此类错误，提示未来需引入相位感知的目标函数。研究聚焦于对滚动预测稳定性的受控分析，而非架构性能基准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长时序自回归预测在处理振荡物理信号时面临误差累积问题，导致相位漂移，传统点对点指标难以检测。因此需要系统评估模型在长时间滚动预测下的稳定性，以识别关键设计要素。

Method: 使用合成三成分地震波形作为物理结构化的测试数据集，采用SeismoGPT模型进行自回归预测。通过控制变量的架构消融实验，并结合配对显著性检验，评估各设计组件对滚动预测稳定性的影响。重点分析多标记预测、时序嵌入混合预测头、跨时序STFT幅度一致性损失的作用，以及上下文比例阈值的影响。

Result: 多标记预测显著提升滚动稳定性，贡献了几乎全部的性能增益（+0.040中位数NCC）；时序嵌入混合预测头与跨时序STFT幅度一致性损失分别带来小但稳定的改进；性能对上下文比例阈值敏感，临界点约为1（对应完整P-S波段），低于该值时泛化能力迅速下降；主要残余问题是极性反转，现有幅度谱损失无法抑制，表明需发展相位感知目标函数。

Conclusion: 本研究揭示了多标记预测在长时序振荡信号滚动预测中的核心作用，强调了上下文长度的重要性，并指出当前基于幅度的损失函数存在固有缺陷，未来应探索相位感知的优化目标以进一步提升稳定性。研究提供了一种受控分析框架，用于理解自回归模型在波场预测中的长期行为。

Abstract: Long-horizon autoregressive forecasting of oscillatory physical signals, such as seismograms, gravitational-wave strain, and similar wavefields is limited by error accumulation: as a causal model is fed its own outputs over hundreds of steps, small per-step errors compound into phase drift that pointwise metrics fail to detect. We ask when such rollout stays stable, using synthetic three-component seismograms as a physically structured testbed and the \textsc{SeismoGPT} autoregressive forecaster as the model under study. Through controlled, intra-architecture ablations evaluated on free-running rollout with paired significance tests, we isolate the contribution of each design choice. Multi-token prediction is the dominant stabilizer, accounting for almost the entire improvement over a single-token baseline ($+0.040$ median NCC); a horizon-embedding hybrid prediction head and a cross-horizon STFT-magnitude coherence loss each add a small but consistent further gain. Performance depends sharply on a context-ratio threshold near one, roughly the full P-S interval of observed signal, below which rollout generalization collapses. The dominant residual failure is a polarity inversion that a magnitude-based spectral loss cannot, by construction, penalize, identifying phase-aware objectives as the natural next step. We frame this as a controlled study of rollout stability on oscillatory wavefields, not a benchmark of forecasting architectures.

</details>


### [369] [Optimal Post-Training Quantization Scales and Where to Find Them](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10890)
*Juan Amboage,Pablo Monteagudo-Lago,Ian Colbert,Giuseppe Franco,Nicholas Fraser*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: PiSO是一种用于后训练量化（PTQ）的算法，通过校准数据精确高效地计算通道级权重缩放因子，在四舍五入量化下实现最优性能。它将缩放因子搜索空间划分为有限区间，每个区间内存在闭式最小化解，并扩展至组级量化，结合误差校正策略显著提升模型在Llama和Qwen系列模型上的困惑度与零样本准确率，尤其在低比特压缩时优势更明显。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有PTQ方法通常采用无数据启发式选择缩放因子，缺乏对量化网格的精细优化；本文旨在通过利用校准数据，精准计算最优缩放因子以提升低比特量化模型的性能。

Method: 提出PiSO（分段尺度优化）算法，将尺度搜索空间分段，每段内可解析求解最优缩放因子；通过设计合理的组级量化扩展机制及尺度优化与误差校正的交替策略，实现高效且准确的量化。

Result: 在Llama和Qwen系列模型上，不同尺寸和目标比特位宽下，均实现了更低的困惑度和更高的零样本准确率，尤其在低比特场景下改善更为显著，验证了方法的有效性与鲁棒性。

Conclusion: PiSO通过数据驱动的精细化尺度优化，显著提升了后训练量化性能，尤其适用于高压缩比下的模型部署，为低比特大语言模型的实用化提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: Post-training quantization (PTQ) compresses large language models by mapping weights to low-bit representations. The scaling factor that defines the quantization grid is typically chosen using simple, data-free heuristics. In this work, we present PiSO (Piecewise Scale Optimization), an algorithm that leverages calibration data to compute the optimal channel-wise weight scales exactly and efficiently under round-to-nearest quantization. PiSO partitions the scale search space into finitely many intervals on which the objective admits a closed-form minimizer. We extend PiSO to group-wise quantization via principled heuristics and propose effective strategies for interleaving scale optimization with error correction. Experiments on Llama and Qwen models across multiple model sizes and target weight bit-widths demonstrate consistent improvements in perplexity and downstream zero-shot accuracy, both standalone and combined with error correction. In particular, we observe increased benefits as the target bit-width narrows and quantization becomes more challenging.

### [370] [Flash-GMM: A Memory-Efficient Kernel for Scalable Soft Clustering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10896)
*Gal Bloch,Ariel Gera,Matan Orbach,Ohad Eytan,Assaf Toledo*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Flash-GMM 是一种高效的 Triton 内核，用于在单个 GPU 通道中对大规模数据进行高斯混合模型（GMM）计算。它通过避免在 GPU 内存中存储完整的责任矩阵，实现了比现有方法快 20 倍的性能，并使单设备上可训练的数据集规模扩大超过 100 倍。该技术被集成到 IVF 粗量化器中，使得软 GMM 聚类可作为 k-means 的直接替代方案，并能将边界向量分配给多个聚类。实验表明，在固定召回率目标下，距离计算量减少最多达 1.7 倍，或在相同计算成本下召回率提升 2–12。代码已开源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 GMM 实现受限于内存开销，难以处理大规模数据；同时，k-means 在近似最近邻搜索中存在聚类边界不灵活的问题，需要更高效的替代方案。

Method: 提出 Flash-GMM 融合 Triton 内核，通过避免显式存储责任矩阵，优化内存使用与计算效率；利用 GMM 责任值实现多聚类分配，改进 IVF 粗量化器设计。

Result: 相比现有方法，Flash-GMM 实现 20× 速度提升，支持 100× 更大数据规模；在 ANN 搜索中，可减少最多 1.7× 距离计算，或在相同计算成本下提升 2–12 的 recall@10。

Conclusion: Flash-GMM 显著提升了 GMM 在大规模数据上的计算效率，使其成为 k-means 的高效、灵活替代方案，适用于近似最近邻搜索等任务，且已开源，具有广泛的应用潜力。

Abstract: We present \textbf{Flash-GMM}, a fused Triton kernel for efficient computation of Gaussian Mixture Models (GMMs) over large-scale data in a single GPU pass. By eliminating the need to materialize the full responsibility matrix in GPU memory, Flash-GMM achieves a \textbf{20$\times$} speedup over existing implementations and enables training on datasets more than \textbf{100$\times$} larger than previously feasible on one device. To demonstrate its impact, we integrate Flash-GMM into the IVF coarse quantizer for approximate nearest-neighbor (ANN) search. We show that soft GMM clustering is now a viable drop-in replacement for $k$-means, and that GMM responsibilities can be leveraged to assign border vectors to multiple clusters. Our approach reaches fixed recall targets with up to $1.7\times$ fewer distance computations, or equivalently, yields $+2$--$12$ recall@10 at matched computational cost. We release the kernel as an open-source project.

### [371] [Conservation Laws from Data Symmetry in Neural Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10913)
*Jakob Galley,Vahid Shahverdi,Axel Flinth*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究神经网络梯度流训练过程中，数据内在对称性是否会导致守恒量。在损失函数为解析且非多项式的情况下，证明了数据对称性通常不会引入额外的积分不变量；但对于均方误差（MSE）损失，在数据增强情况下可能存在额外守恒量。作者提出基于张量可分解网络（tensorizable networks）的框架来描述该现象，这类网络包括线性、多项式网络以及Lightning Attention等结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究数据对称性在神经网络训练中是否产生守恒量，理解梯度流下的动力学特性，特别是在不同损失函数和数据增强策略下的表现差异。

Method: 基于解析损失函数的数学分析，结合微分几何与对称性理论，推导守恒量的存在条件；针对MSE损失，构建张量可分解网络框架以形式化描述数据增强带来的守恒量。

Result: 一般情况下，数据对称性不导致额外守恒量；但在MSE损失下，通过数据增强可诱导出额外守恒量；张量可分解网络有效刻画了这一现象。

Conclusion: 数据对称性在大多数情况下不会带来梯度流中的新守恒量，但特定损失函数（如MSE）配合数据增强时例外；张量可分解网络为理解此类现象提供了有效建模工具。

Abstract: We explore whether intrinsic symmetries of the training data lead to conserved quantities during gradient-flow training of neural networks. Under the assumption that the loss function is analytic and non-polynomial, we prove that data symmetries generically do not induce any additional integrals of motion. For mean squared error (MSE) loss, on the other hand, there are situations in which data augmentation yields extra conserved quantities. We build a framework, utilizing \emph{tensorizable networks} to describe this phenomenon. Tensorizable networks are a family of architectures whose dependence on parameters and inputs can be separated using an intermediate representation. They include linear and polynomial networks, as well as Lightning Attention.

</details>


### [372] [Recoverable but Not Stationary:Local Linear Structures in Weights and Activations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10929)
*Irina Piontkovskaia,Sergey Nikolenko*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 研究表明，模型行为可通过线性方向控制，但这些线性结构是局部且动态的，而非全局固定的方向。在合成多任务Transformer及LoRA适配器实验中，发现局部低秩任务梯度结构显著，但固定任务平面假设不成立；有效基底在100步内发生明显漂移。首次恢复更新形成轨迹前缀基，可捕捉77%的LoRA恢复位移。提出随机搜索理论与高斯局部线性定理，解释高维空间中随机参数搜索的有效性。此外，单步梯度更新与激活导向具有较强相关性（余弦相似度0.58），并在Qwen-0.5B BoolQ任务中验证。整体表明，线性结构为演化中的局部几何，部分保留在参数与激活空间中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究深度学习模型中线性结构的存在形式与尺度，理解任务行为如何通过参数空间中的线性方向实现控制，挑战传统固定任务平面假设。

Method: 结合合成多任务Transformer与真实LLM（DistilGPT-2/GPT-2）上的LoRA适配器，分析任务梯度的低秩结构；引入随机搜索理论与高斯局部线性定理；比较梯度更新与激活导向向量的相关性，并在多个模型上进行实验验证。

Result: 发现强局部低秩任务梯度结构，但固定基底无法捕获有效方向，基底随训练快速漂移；轨迹前缀基可解释77%的恢复位移；单步梯度更新与激活导向向量具显著相关性（0.58余弦相似度）；支持局部动态几何而非全局线性方向的观点。

Conclusion: 模型中的线性结构并非全局固定的任务方向，而是随训练演化的局部几何形态，在参数和激活空间中部分持续存在。这揭示了模型行为控制的内在机制，对高效微调与可控生成具有重要意义。

Abstract: Task vectors, LoRA, activation steering, and random search around pretrained weights all suggest that learned behaviour can be controlled by linear directions. We ask which linear structures actually exist and on what scale. In a synthetic multitask transformer and LoRA adapters on DistilGPT-2 / GPT-2 we find strong local low-rank task-gradient structure but reject the fixed-task-plane hypothesis: static bases miss the recovery direction, and the useful basis drifts substantially within 100 steps. However, the first recovery updates form a trajectory-prefix basis capturing 77% of the LoRA recovery displacement. We develop random search theory with a Gaussian local-linear theorem that justifies the effectiveness of random parameter search even in very high dimensions. We also study the relation between parameter perturbations and activation steering: a single gradient step produces an activation shift with 0.58 cosine to a labelled-contrast CAA steering vector, with a similar steering effect on Qwen-0.5B BoolQ statements. We validate our results with experiments on synthetic Transformers and LLMs. Our results suggest that linear structures in trained networks are not global task directions, but evolving local geometries that partially persist across parameter and activation spaces.

### [373] [CLP: Collocation-Length Prediction for Zero-Loss Adaptive Multi-Token Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10935)
*Xuezhen Xie,Zhiqiang Zhou*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为Backbone-as-Architect的新设计原则，以解决多标记预测（MTP）在大语言模型推理中因头部-主干竞争导致的输出质量下降问题。通过让主干语言模型始终生成首个令牌，而MTP头仅负责后续令牌，该方法有效避免了重复和不连贯输出。在此基础上，作者引入轻量级的CLP（共现长度预测器），仅用4.6K–7.7K参数即可实现高效的跨度级决策，显著优于以往需100万参数门控网络的方法。实验表明，在Qwen2.5系列模型上，CLP实现了1.14x–1.29x的加速，且无质量损失（重复率<0.02），而传统方法要么无加速效果，要么严重劣化输出。此外，研究发现较短的预测范围（k=2）可提升大型模型下MTP头的准确性，揭示了预测精度是加速的关键瓶颈，并为未来优化提供了清晰路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有MTP方法存在头部-主干竞争问题，导致首个令牌生成时出现冲突，从而引发严重的重复与不连贯输出，限制了其在实际推理中的应用。因此亟需一种能消除该冲突并保持高质量输出的新型架构设计。

Method: 提出Backbone-as-Architect设计原则，使主干语言模型始终生成第一个令牌，其余由MTP头处理；引入轻量级的CLP（Collocation-Length Predictor），采用单个线性层进行安全扩展长度预测，替代传统复杂门控网络。

Result: 在Qwen2.5 0.5B、1.5B和7B模型上，CLP实现1.14x–1.29x的推理加速，重复率低于0.02%，零质量退化；而基于门控网络的方法要么加速无效（1.07x），要么产生极高重复率（>0.5%）。同时发现短预测窗口（k=2）能显著提升大模型下的MTP头准确率，验证了预测精度为关键约束。

Conclusion: MTP头的预测准确性是当前加速方案的主要瓶颈。Backbone-as-Architect与CLP结合提供了一种高效、低开销且无质量损失的MTP加速框架，为未来高性能推理系统的设计指明了方向。

Abstract: Large language model inference is bottlenecked by autoregressive decoding, where each token requires a full forward pass. Multi-token prediction (MTP) offers a promising acceleration path, but existing approaches suffer from a fundamental architectural flaw: the MTP head for the first token competes with the backbone's own language model (LM) head, leading to severe quality degradation when predictions are accepted. We identify this head-backbone competition as the root cause of repetitive and incoherent outputs in prior MTP-based acceleration methods. To address this, we propose Backbone-as-Architect, a design principle where the backbone LM head always generates the first token, and MTP heads are responsible only for subsequent tokens. Building on this principle, we introduce CLP (Collocation-Length Predictor), a lightweight span-level decision layer that predicts how many additional tokens can be safely accepted at each decoding step. CLP uses only a single linear layer (4.6K--7.7K parameters), replacing the over-engineered 1M-parameter gate networks used in prior work. Experiments on Qwen2.5 models (0.5B, 1.5B, 7B) show that CLP achieves 1.20x--1.29x speedup on 1.5B and 1.14x--1.20x on 7B, with zero quality degradation (repetition ratio < 0.02), while gate-based approaches fail to accelerate (1.07x) or produce severely degraded outputs (repetition ratio > 0.5%). We further demonstrate that shorter prediction horizons (k=2) recover 24% higher MTP head accuracy on large models, establishing a scaling-aware design principle. We identify MTP head prediction accuracy as the binding constraint on acceleration and establish a clear roadmap for future improvements.

</details>

*Adam Nordling*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种系统化的轨迹数据增强框架，评估了五种选择策略（异常性、多样性、代表性、不确定性与随机选择），在多个数据集上验证其有效性。结果表明，系统性选择策略（尤其是异常性和不确定性）在稀疏数据中表现更稳定，能有效修复拓扑碎片；但在高质量密集数据中可能引入噪声，且高速域存在特征空间发散问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 设计并测试五种系统性选择策略，结合Optuna进行超参数优化，在四个不同领域的数据集上使用线性与非线性模型进行实验验证，并通过UMAP可视化分析增强效果。

Conclusion: 轨迹数据增强的效果高度依赖于数据特性与场景条件，系统性选择虽具优势但并非普适解，需根据数据密度与动态特性谨慎应用。

Abstract: Trajectory data augmentation is a promising approach to mitigate data scarcity in machine learning applications, but its utility has been limited by the complexity of preserving spatio-temporal coherence. Although prior work demonstrated the viability of geometric perturbation, it relied on naive random selection, leaving a critical gap in understanding which trajectories should be augmented for maximal benefit. This thesis addresses this gap by developing a systematic and scalable framework to evaluate five systematic selection strategies: Outlierness, Diversity, Representativeness, Uncertainty, and Random selection. These strategies were rigorously tested across four datasets covering animal behavior (Foxes and Starkey), maritime traffic (AIS), and urban traffic (Car) using a suite of linear and non-linear machine learning models. As part of this evaluation, an Optuna-based hyperparameter optimization loop was integrated to empirically identify the best-performing augmentation parameters for each dataset within the explored search space. The results indicate that, while systematic selection is not a universal solution, it offers distinct advantages over the random baseline. Systematic strategies, particularly Outlierness and Uncertainty, demonstrated higher stability and were less prone to performance degradation observed with random sampling in dense datasets. However, the findings also reveal that the value of augmentation is strictly conditional. Visual analysis via UMAP demonstrates that while systematic augmentation successfully repairs topological fragmentation in sparse datasets, it can act as a corrupting noise signal in high-quality, dense datasets. Furthermore, the study identified physical limitations in high-velocity domains, where standard perturbation techniques lead to divergence in feature space...

### [375] [Express Language Modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10944)
*Albert Gong,Annabelle Michael Carrell,Raaz Dwivedi,Lester Mackey*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Express 是一种新工具，可将非因果注意力近似转换为具有相同近似保证的因果注意力近似。结合 Thinformer 近似，Express 实现了最优的因果注意力误差（$\log^{3/2}(n)/s$），仅需 $O(s)$ 内存和 $O(s^2 \log^2(n))$ 压缩开销，适用于长度为 $n$ 的序列。配合高效的 I/O 友好 Triton 实现，Express 在多个场景中显著优于 FlashAttention 2，解决了语言建模流水线中的四个资源瓶颈：长上下文预填充、KV 缓存压缩、内存受限的长文本解码与计算受限的长文本解码。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有因果注意力近似在长序列处理中存在精度与资源消耗之间的权衡，尤其在内存和计算开销上难以满足大规模语言模型的需求。亟需一种既能保持高精度又具备高效实现的新方法来解决长序列建模中的资源瓶颈问题。

Method: 提出 Express 工具，将非因果注意力近似转化为因果近似，并与 Thinformer 技术结合，利用其低内存占用和可控压缩开销的特性，通过 I/O 优化的 Triton 实现提升实际性能。

Result: Express 实现了 $\log^{3/2}(n)/s$ 的近似误差，仅需 $O(s)$ 内存和 $O(s^2 \log^2(n))$ 压缩开销；在多种任务中显著超越 FlashAttention 2，有效缓解了长序列语言建模中的四个核心资源瓶颈。

Conclusion: Express 成功实现了高效且高精度的因果注意力近似，为长序列语言建模提供了新的技术路径，显著提升了系统性能与资源利用率。

Abstract: We introduce a new tool, Express, for converting a non-causal attention approximation into a causal approximation with matching approximation guarantees. When combined with the state-of-the-art Thinformer approximation, Express improves upon the best known causal attention guarantees, delivering $\log^{3/2}(n)/s$ approximation error with only $O(s)$ memory and $O(s^2 \log^2(n))$ compression overhead for a sequence of length $n$. We pair these developments with an efficient I/O-aware Triton implementation, demonstrate substantial speedups over FlashAttention 2, and use Express to overcome four resource bottlenecks in the language modeling pipeline: long-context prefill, KV cache compression, long-form memory-constrained decoding, and long-form compute-constrained decoding.

### [376] [Population-Aware Physics-Informed Neural Particle Flow for Bayesian Update](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10959)
*Batu Candan,Simone Servadio*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的物理信息神经粒子流方法（PA-PINPF），通过引入对粒子群体的感知，改进了传统PINPF中独立处理每个粒子的局限。PA-PINPF使用深度集合（Deep Sets）来编码整个粒子集的全局信息，包括粒子状态或完整的物理特征（如位置、伪时间、测量值、似然和梯度信息），从而增强粒子更新的上下文感知能力。该方法保持原有的无监督物理信息残差目标，无需真实后验样本训练。在测距和非线性到达时间差任务上的实验表明，两种群体感知变体均优于原始粒子级PINPF，尤其是基于特征的群体编码表现最佳，证明了群体级物理特征对贝叶斯粒子传输具有重要全局指导作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统物理信息神经粒子流（PINPF）虽能有效将先验分布映射至后验分布，但其速度模型独立处理每个粒子，缺乏对整体粒子群的上下文感知，限制了传输效率与精度。为提升粒子运输的全局协调性与适应性，需引入对群体结构与物理特征的显式建模。

Method: 提出两种群体感知的PINPF变体：PA-PINPF-State 和 PA-PINPF-Feature。前者通过深度集合编码粒子状态，后者则编码包含位置、伪时间、测量值、似然值和得分等在内的完整局部物理特征向量。两者均以置换不变方式整合全粒子集信息，用于增强每个粒子的更新决策，同时保留原始无监督物理信息残差目标。

Result: 在多个范围测量与非线性时差到达任务上，两种群体感知变体均显著优于标准粒子级PINPF；其中，基于特征的群体编码（PA-PINPF-Feature）表现最优，说明群体级别的物理特征能有效提供全局信息，促进更准确的贝叶斯粒子传输。

Conclusion: 引入群体感知机制可显著提升物理信息神经粒子流的性能，尤其当使用全面的物理特征进行群体编码时，能够有效利用全局上下文信息，实现更高效、精准的贝叶斯后验逼近。

Abstract: Physics-informed neural particle flow (PINPF) learns a deterministic transport field that moves particles from a prior distribution toward a Bayesian posterior while enforcing the governing probability-evolution equation. However, the standard PINPF velocity model processes particles independently and therefore does not explicitly condition its transport decisions on the empirical particle population. This paper introduces population-aware PINPF (PA-PINPF), which augments each particle update with a permutation-invariant Deep Sets representation of the full particle set. We investigate two population encoders. PA-PINPF-State summarizes the particle states, whereas PA-PINPF-Feature summarizes the complete local physics-informed feature vectors, including particle position, pseudo-time, measurement information, likelihood values, and score information. The latter allows the population context to represent not only particle-cloud geometry, but also the population-level Bayesian transport geometry. The methods retain the original unsupervised physics-informed residual objective and require no ground-truth posterior samples during training. Experiments on range-measurement tasks and nonlinear time-difference-of-arrival posterior transport demonstrate that both population-aware variants improve over particle-wise PINPF, while feature-population encoding provides the strongest performance. These results show that population-level physics features provide useful global information for learned Bayesian particle transport.

### [377] [Beyond Uniform Token-Level Trust Region in LLM Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10968)
*Renjie Mao,Xiangxin Zhou,Lvfang Tao,Yixin Ding,Yu Shi,Yongguang Lin,Yuheng Wu,Honglin Zhu,Qian Qiu,Wenxi Zhu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: CPPO（Cumulative Prefix-divergence Policy Optimization）提出了一种新的强化学习方法，用于改进大语言模型的推理能力。它通过引入位置加权阈值和累积前缀预算机制，解决了传统PPO方法在自回归生成中对所有标记采用统一阈值所导致的局限性。该方法能够更合理地处理早期与晚期生成阶段的偏差问题，有效防止前缀漂移的累积，从而提升训练稳定性和推理准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于PPO的强化学习方法在大语言模型推理中使用统一的阈值策略，忽略了自回归生成过程中的位置差异和累积前缀漂移问题，导致早期偏差未被充分约束而后期探索受限，影响模型性能和训练稳定性。

Method: 提出CPPO方法，包含两个核心机制：1）位置加权阈值，对早期生成位置施加更严格的约束以减少长期影响；2）累积前缀预算，动态追踪历史偏差并限制后续生成的偏离程度，防止错误累积。

Result: 实验表明，CPPO显著提升了不同规模模型的训练稳定性和推理准确率，相较于传统方法表现更优。

Conclusion: CPPO通过引入位置感知和累积偏差控制机制，有效缓解了传统强化学习中因静态阈值带来的问题，为大语言模型的推理优化提供了更高效、更稳定的解决方案。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) has become standard for improving LLM reasoning. However, existing PPO-style trust-region mechanisms remain position-agnostic by enforcing uniform thresholds across all tokens independently. This pointwise treatment conflicts with autoregressive generation in two critical ways. First, uniform thresholds ignore autoregressive asymmetry. Early-stage deviations produce compounding sequence-level drift, causing static thresholds to under-regulate early divergence and excessively constrain late-stage exploration. Second, evaluating token-level divergence in isolation overlooks cumulative prefix drift, granting the same divergence allowance regardless of how far the conditioning history has already deviated from the rollout policy. To address this limitation, we propose CPPO (Cumulative Prefix-divergence Policy Optimization), a token-level masking rule that aligns updates with a finite-horizon policy-improvement bound via two coupled mechanisms. First, a position-weighted threshold imposes stricter limits at early positions whose effects persist longer, relaxing constraints for late-stage tokens. Second, a cumulative prefix budget tracks historical deviations, dynamically restricting further token-level deviation to prevent compounding errors along the prefix. Empirically, CPPO enhances training stability and significantly improves reasoning accuracy across various model scales.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有分析变换（如DFT、DCT）虽高效稳定，但假设固定先验，难以捕捉特定信号类别的精细结构；需引入数据自适应变换以降低重构残差，同时平衡泛化能力与逼近误差。

Method: 基于不精确邻近方法框架，设计了一种由固定基矩阵与数据自适应稀疏修正部分构成的结构化变换，利用新推导的闭式投影算子实现高效优化。

Abstract: Finding convenient spaces in which certain hypotheses regarding an assumed sparse structure of natural signals hold true has become a desirable result in recent research, its implications being reflected in areas such as data compression, noise reduction and feature extraction. While the extensively used analytical transforms, such as DFT or DCT, already provide efficient algorithms and robust sparse representations, they assume a fixed prior about the data, failing to accurately capture the specific structure of more restrictive classes of signals. To address this, the concept of a data-adaptive, learnt transform has been introduced in the literature, allowing for the reduction of a residual term in the transform domain. More recent studies have shown that the condition number serves as a good metric in this context, where the desired outcome alternates between a generalizing tendency and one that achieves minimal approximation error. Motivated by these considerations, we introduce the learning of a structured, explicitly conditioned transform formulated as the product of a fixed canonical matrix and a refining data-adaptive sparse component. This approach seeks to preserve the advantages of fast and stable analytical transforms, while introducing controllable adaptivity to the data. No references that concern this specific formulation have been identified so far, indicating its novelty. The proposed algorithm is motivated within the framework of inexact proximal methods, leveraging a newly derived closed-form projection operator. Empirical observations demonstrate state-of-the-art results on the doubly sparse transform learning problem and comparable performance with its dense variant at significantly lower computational costs and sometimes faster convergence and better avoidance of bad local minima.

### [379] [Data-Driven Runway and Taxiway Exits Prediction of Landing Aircraft: A Case Study at Hartsfield-Jackson Atlanta International Airport](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11017)

Method: 采用两阶段机器学习框架：第一阶段预测航班选择的跑道出口，第二阶段预测在选定出口后是否穿越活跃起飞跑道或使用绕行滑行道。模型基于多源数据（包括ASDE-X表面轨迹、飞机类型、停机位、短时流量、天气）构建，并使用多个时间窗口进行特征提取。对比九种主流分类器（如随机森林、XGBoost、LightGBM、CatBoost），通过准确率、宏平均F1、PR曲线、混淆矩阵、Brier评分和期望校准误差等指标综合评估性能。利用t-SNE与UMAP可视化分析特征空间结构，结合特征重要性分析揭示关键影响因素。

Result: 在东西向航班流中，XGBoost与LightGBM表现最优。第一阶段预测准确率达0.86–0.89，宏平均F1为0.40–0.50；第二阶段准确率为0.70–0.74，宏平均F1为0.28–0.55。进近速度是出口选择的主导因素；出发率、穿越率、停机位目的地以及西向流中的出口选择显著影响穿越/绕行决策。少数类预测困难源于特征空间重叠，经由t-SNE与UMAP验证。模型输出具备良好校准性与可解释性。

Conclusion: 本研究提出的两阶段数据驱动决策辅助系统能够有效提升空中交通管制员对航班滑行路径的态势感知能力，提供可信、可解释的预测结果，同时保持人类在最终决策中的主导地位，适用于复杂机场环境下的高效、安全运行支持。

Abstract: Airport surface operations increasingly constrain performance at high-throughput hubs. This study examines arrival taxi-in decisions at Hartsfield-Jackson Atlanta International Airport (KATL) and proposes a two-stage, data-driven decision aid that mirrors controller workflow. Stage I predicts the runway exit selected by an arriving aircraft. Stage II predicts whether, given that exit, the aircraft will cross the active departure runway at a designated point or use the end-around taxiway. Models are trained using ASDE-X surface trajectories, aircraft characteristics, ramp destinations, short-horizon traffic rates, and weather across multiple look-back windows. We benchmark nine classifiers, including Random Forest, XGBoost, LightGBM, and CatBoost, and evaluate accuracy, macro-F1, precision-recall behavior, confusion matrices, Brier score, and Expected Calibration Error. Across east and west flows, XGBoost and LightGBM outperform Random Forest. Stage I achieves 0.86-0.89 accuracy with macro-F1 scores of 0.40-0.50, while Stage II achieves 0.70-0.74 accuracy with macro-F1 scores of 0.28-0.55. Feature-importance analysis shows that approach speed is the main driver of exit choice. Departure rate, crossing rate, ramp destination, and, for west flow, the selected exit are the strongest predictors of crossing versus end-around routing. Minority classes remain harder to predict because of feature-space overlap, as shown by t-SNE and UMAP analyses. The proposed framework supports controller situational awareness through calibrated, explainable predictions while preserving human responsibility for final routing decisions.

### [380] [Flow-DPPO: Divergence Proximal Policy Optimization for Flow Matching Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11025)
*Bowen Ping,Xiangxin Zhou,Penghui Qi,Minnan Luo,Liefeng Bo,Tianyu Pang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Flow-DPPO提出一种新的方法，通过用发散近似约束替代比例裁剪，以解决流模型中比例裁剪结构不适配的问题。该方法利用高斯分布的特性精确计算KL散度，并采用非对称发散掩码，仅在梯度更新同时远离信任区域并违反发散阈值时进行阻断，从而提升训练稳定性与多目标优化平衡性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法如Flow-GRPO和CPS使用比例裁剪来约束策略更新，但在流模型中，概率比是噪声较大的单样本估计，导致某些轨迹区域过度约束而其他区域约束不足，影响训练效果和模型稳定性。

Method: 提出Flow-DPPO，以基于KL散度的发散近似约束替代传统比例裁剪；利用流模型中每步策略为高斯分布的特性，实现高效且精确的KL计算；引入非对称发散掩码，仅在更新方向同时背离信任区域且超过阈值时阻止梯度传播。

Result: 实验表明，Flow-DPPO在获得更高奖励的同时，提升了KL近似效率，缓解了灾难性遗忘，促进多目标优化平衡，并支持稳定多轮次训练，而传统比例裁剪方法在此场景下性能下降。

Conclusion: Flow-DPPO通过更合理的约束机制改进了在线强化学习在流匹配模型中的应用，显著提升了图像与视频生成的质量与训练稳定性。

Abstract: Recent work has demonstrated that online reinforcement learning (RL) can substantially improve the quality and alignment of flow matching models for image and video generation. Methods such as Flow-GRPO and CPS cast the denoising process as a Markov Decision Process and apply PPO-style ratio clipping to enforce a trust region. However, we argue that ratio clipping is structurally ill-suited for flow models: the probability ratio between new and old policies is a noisy, single-sample estimate of the true policy divergence, leading to over-constraining in some regions of the trajectory and under-constraining in others. We propose Flow-DPPO (Flow Divergence Proximal Policy Optimization), which replaces ratio clipping with a divergence proximal constraint. A key observation is that the per-step policy in flow models is Gaussian, enabling exact and cheap computation of the KL divergence between old and new policies. Flow-DPPO employs an asymmetric divergence mask that blocks gradient updates only when they simultaneously move away from the trusted region and violate the divergence threshold. Experiments show that Flow-DPPO achieves higher rewards with better KL-proximal efficiency, alleviates catastrophic forgetting, promotes balanced multi-objective optimization, and enables stable multi-epoch training where ratio clipping degrades. Code and models are available at https://github.com/Tencent-Hunyuan/UniRL/tree/main/FlowDPPO.

</details>

Abstract: Neural population activity models can recover rich temporal structure from binned spikes, but their read-in and readout layers often remain tied to a fixed set of recorded neurons. This coupling limits reuse in long-term brain-computer interfaces, where recorded neuron identities, counts, and response statistics can change across days. We introduce GRAFT, a Transformer-based neural population activity model that separates reusable temporal dynamics from a recalibratable neuron interface. The neuron interface controls how recorded neurons enter and leave the shared backbone, and auxiliary gain and positional mechanisms support neural activity modeling inside the Transformer. On MC Maze under the standard NLB'21 protocol, GRAFT reaches 0.3866 co-bps as an ensemble, setting a new state of the art on the primary co-bps metric among public and reported NLB'21 results. In a cross-day protocol constructed from the NLB'21 MC Maze dataset series, GRAFT recalibrates from MC Maze to the scaled MC Maze datasets (Large/Medium/Small) by updating only 9.21% of parameters, reaching 0.3749, 0.3112, and 0.3152 co-bps with restricted target-day support sets. These results show that the same interface-backbone separation supports both strong Transformer-based neural population activity modeling and data-efficient cross-day recalibration.

### [383] [Exploring the Design Space of Reward Backpropagation for Flow Matching](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11075)
*Ruoyu Wang,Boye Niu,Xiangxin Zhou,Yushi Huang,Tongliang Liu,Chi Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出FlowBP框架，通过构建轻量级反向代理轨迹解决文本到图像生成中直接奖励反向传播的样本效率与梯度路径问题。该框架将采样与优化解耦，使用缓存的前向轨迹和选择性重前向速度构建反向代理，有效控制内存占用和梯度链长。三种变体（FlowBP-Sparse、FlowBP-Bridge、FlowBP-Lagrange）在多个基准上均优于基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出统一的代理轨迹框架FlowBP，将反向传播轨迹作为可设计对象；采样时缓存无梯度轨迹，优化时仅对选定部分重新前向计算速度，并基于此构建轻量级反向代理；通过四个设计选择（奖励输入、活跃集、积分权重、桥接耦合）实现灵活性，并恢复已有方法为特例。

Result: 三种变体（FlowBP-Sparse、FlowBP-Bridge、FlowBP-Lagrange）在SD3.5-M、FLUX.1-dev和FLUX.2-Klein-base上，在偏好、质量及组合性等指标上普遍优于直接梯度基线方法；内存消耗由活跃集大小决定，梯度链长度被限制至最多一个雅可比因子。

Conclusion: FlowBP通过将反向轨迹建模为可设计组件，实现了采样与优化的高效解耦，显著提升了文本到图像生成中基于人类偏好的训练效率与稳定性，为未来高阶扩散模型优化提供了通用且可扩展的框架。

Abstract: Aligning text-to-image flow matching models with human preferences via direct reward backpropagation is sample-efficient but hampered by two well-known pathologies: activations cannot be stored across the full sampling trajectory at modern model scale, and chained Jacobian products across steps inflate the reward gradient as it travels back to early indices. Connector-based methods, such as LeapAlign, address these issues by replacing the full backward trajectory with a short pinned path, highlighting a useful decoupling between sampling and optimization. However, the quality of the resulting gradient depends on how accurately this short path approximates the full rollout, especially over long intervals. We propose FlowBP, a unified surrogate-trajectory framework that treats the backward trajectory itself as the design object. FlowBP keeps a no-gradient cached rollout for sampling, then builds a lightweight backward surrogate from cached and selectively re-forwarded velocities. This view separates four choices: the reward-model input, active set, integration weights, and bridge coupling, and recovers prior direct-gradient methods as particular settings. Within this framework, we instantiate three variants: FlowBP-Sparse uses sparse Euler reconstruction, FlowBP-Bridge adds controlled bridge coupling, and FlowBP-Lagrange raises the order of leap quadrature. All three bound memory by the active-set size and limit gradient chaining to at most one Jacobian factor. Across SD3.5-M, FLUX.1-dev, and FLUX.2-Klein-base on preference, quality, and compositional metrics, the three variants improve over direct-gradient baselines on most metrics.

Abstract: Communication-efficient pre-training of LLMs is increasingly important as training draws on compute distributed across clusters, data centers, and lower-bandwidth links. Many practical methods reduce communication frequency but still rely on synchronous All-Reduce operations that maintain identical model states and tie progress to global collectives. This can become a bottleneck when bandwidth or worker speed is heterogeneous. We introduce GASLoC, a novel decentralized pre-training algorithm that generalizes the notion of communication acceleration to the recently popular "outer optimizer" to allow a practical gossip-based training framework that is compatible with adaptive optimizers, allows for local optimizer steps, and can utilize sparse randomized peer communication. Abstract: Expressive continuous control policies, such as diffusion and flow models, form the backbone of recent advances in scaling imitation learning for simulated and real robot control. While they are known to scale stably in the supervised imitation learning setting, incorporating them into reinforcement learning (RL) pipelines for policy improvement has proven more difficult. It often requires specialized training objectives or backpropagating through denoising processes, which cause well-known issues with stability and affect scalability. In this paper we study the question of whether simple policy improvement schemes at test time alone, leaving stable supervised policy training intact, can be a competitive alternative which sidesteps these issues. To this end, we propose QGF (Q-Guided Flow), an RL algorithm that performs policy optimization entirely at test time. QGF works by pre-training both a reference flow policy (via a standard behavioral cloning objective) and a value function critic and, at test time, using the value gradient to guide the reference policy to generate higher-value actions without any additional policy learning. Empirically, QGF outperforms prior test-time RL methods on single-task and goal-conditioned offline RL benchmarks with high-dimensional action spaces, and is competitive with state-of-the-art training-time algorithms while being much cheaper to run. ### [386] [Limitations of Learning Tanh Neural Networks with Finite Precision](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11104)
*Philipp Grohs,Matěj Trödler*

TL;DR: 本文研究在有限精度计算和$L^p$精度保证下，从点采样学习$	anh$神经网络的局限性。通过构造基于迭代$	anh$激活的尖锐局部化突起函数，证明在有限精度设置中，任何基于$m$个样本的自适应随机算法在$L^p$范数下的收敛率不可能超过蒙特卡洛速率$O(m^{-1/p})$，除非采样预算随网络参数规模和架构呈指数增长。该结果揭示了有限精度对包含局部化突起函数类可学习性的根本限制，并将先前针对ReLU网络的结果扩展至$	anh$情形。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出一种基于迭代$	anh$激活的新型尖锐局部化突起函数构造方法，利用该机制分析自适应随机算法在有限精度下的学习性能边界。

Conclusion: 有限精度显著限制了$	anh$神经网络的学习效率，尤其在处理局部特征时，现有算法难以突破蒙特卡洛速率，表明需重新考虑计算精度与模型复杂度之间的权衡。

Abstract: We investigate limitations of learning $\tanh$ neural networks from point evaluations under finite-precision computations and $L^p$ accuracy guarantees, building on Berner, Grohs, and Voigtländer (2023). Our approach is based on a novel construction of sharply localized bump functions via iterated $\tanh$ activations. Using this mechanism, we show that, in a finite-precision setting, no adaptive randomized algorithm based on $m$ samples can achieve a convergence rate higher than the Monte Carlo rate $O(m^{-1/p})$ in the $L^p$ norm, unless the sampling budget grows exponentially with the size of the network parameters and architecture. The results reveal fundamental limitations imposed by finite precision on the learnability of classes containing localized bump functions, extending previous results for ReLU networks to the $\tanh$ setting.

### [387] [Data-Driven Dynamic Assortment in Online Platforms: Learning about Two Sides](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11118)
*Rahul Roy,Nur Sunar,Jayashankar M. Swaminathan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了一个在离散时间框架下，具有不完全信息和异质客户的双边服务平台上的动态组合优化问题。平台在每期选择一组卖家展示给到达的客户，客户根据多项式对数选择模型从展示的卖家中选择最多一个进行交易。经过固定周期后，卖家根据另一多项式对数模型从收到的提议中选择最多一个客户，循环重复。平台事先不知道客户和卖家的选择模型参数。本文提出一种数据驱动算法，在学习这些参数的同时优化平台目标。通过使用后悔值衡量相对于已知所有参数和客户到达情况的全知基准的收入损失，证明该算法的最坏情况后悔值随时间呈多对数增长，并给出了匹配的下界，证明其速率最优性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究大多假设平台知晓客户或卖家的选择参数，但现实中这些参数往往是未知的。本文首次研究了双侧选择参数均未知的动态组合问题，旨在解决实际平台运营中的不确定性挑战。

Method: 设计了一种数据驱动的在线学习算法，通过逐步观察客户和卖家的行为反馈来估计选择模型参数，并在学习过程中持续优化平台收益。采用多对数形式的后悔分析方法评估算法性能。

Result: 所提出的算法在最坏情况下具有多对数增长的后悔值，且该结果达到理论下界，表明算法在速率上是最优的。

Conclusion: 本研究为双侧选择参数未知的动态组合问题提供了首个有效的数据驱动解决方案，证明了算法在长期运行中的高效性和最优性，对实际平台的智能决策具有重要指导意义。

Abstract: We study a dynamic assortment problem on a two-sided service platform with incomplete information and heterogeneous customers in a discrete-time setting. In each period, a customer arrives seeking service, and the platform chooses an assortment of sellers to display. The customer then proposes a transaction to at most one seller in the assortment according to a multinomial logit choice model. After a fixed number of periods, sellers review the proposals they have received and each chooses at most one customer according to another multinomial logit choice model, after which the cycle repeats. A key challenge is that the platform does not know the choice-model parameters of either customers or sellers in advance. To our knowledge, this is the first study of a dynamic assortment problem in which both sides' choice parameters are unknown. We develop a data-driven algorithm that learns these parameters while optimizing the platform's objective over time. We evaluate performance using regret, which measures revenue loss relative to a clairvoyant benchmark that knows all parameters and customer arrivals in advance. We show that the algorithm's worst-case regret grows polylogarithmically over time, and we derive a matching lower bound, establishing its rate optimality.

### [388] [Overcoming Rank Collapse in Feedback Alignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11123)
*Gauthier Boeshertz,Razvan Pascanu,Claudia Clopath*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了反馈对齐（Feedback Alignment, FA）在深层网络中表现不佳的原因，发现其误差信号的有效秩较低，导致参数空间探索受限。为此，提出了两种提升误差信号维度的方法：Muon优化器（通过正交化权重更新）和隐藏层激活归一化（促进激活正交性）。实验表明，这些方法显著提升了FA在大型架构（如ResNet-18）上的性能，在CIFAR100上准确率提高9个百分点。结果揭示低维梯度动态是限制FA扩展的关键障碍，并指出增强更新几何的维度是替代反向传播的重要方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 反馈对齐（FA）虽然避免了传统反向传播中需要权重转置的问题，但在深层网络中表现不佳，其主要原因是误差信号的有效秩较低，限制了参数空间的探索。因此，需要寻找提升误差信号维度的方法以实现更有效的学习。

Method: 对比分析了标准反向传播（BP）与反馈对齐（FA）在CIFAR10上的差异，重点考察误差信号的有效秩；引入两种机制：Muon优化器（正交化权重更新）和隐藏活动归一化（促进激活正交性），以增加FA误差信号的维度；在多个大型架构和基准测试中评估改进效果。

Result: Muon优化器和隐藏活动归一化显著提升了FA的表现，尤其在深度网络如ResNet-18上，于CIFAR100上实现了9个百分点的准确率提升，证明高维更新几何有助于克服低维梯度动态带来的瓶颈。

Conclusion: 低维梯度动态是制约反馈对齐（FA）在深层网络中扩展的核心问题。通过引入正交化机制提升误差信号的有效维度，可有效改善学习性能，为开发不依赖反向传播的替代训练方法提供了可行路径。

Abstract: Backpropagation (BP) is widely viewed as biologically implausible, in part because it requires feedback weights to be the transpose of forward weights for error propagation. Interestingly, when training a network with fixed random feedback weights to circumvent this issue, learning aligns the forward weights with the feedback weights, leading the backpropagated error signal to become an approximation of the standard gradient used by BP. This process, called Feedback Alignment (FA), occurs in MLPs and very shallow CNNs but does not scale well to deeper architectures. In this work, we first investigated differences between BP and FA models, trained on CIFAR10, specifically focusing on the effective rank of the signal. We found that the FA error has a considerably lower rank and hence is constrained to a lower-dimensional subspace compared to BP, limiting exploration of the parameter space. Motivated by this observation, we evaluated two mechanisms for increasing the effective dimensionality of FA: Muon, an optimiser that orthogonalises weight updates; and hidden activity normalisation, which promotes activation orthogonality. Across larger architectures and benchmarks, we find that these methods consistently improve over FA baselines, for example, on CIFAR100 with a Resnet-18, accuracy increases by 9 percentage points. Our results identify low-dimensional gradient dynamics as a key obstacle to scaling FA and suggest that inducing higher-dimensional update geometry is a promising route toward scaling alternatives to backpropagation.

### [389] [Robust Regression of General ReLUs with Queries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11130)
*Ilias Diakonikolas,Daniel M. Kane,Mingchen Ma*

TL;DR: 本文研究在高斯分布下，针对平方损失的广义ReLU函数的抗干扰学习任务。在主动学习设置中，提出了首个计算高效的算法，仅需 $d \text{polylog}(1/\varepsilon) + \tilde{O}(\min\{1/p, 1/\varepsilon\})$ 黑盒标签查询即可达到 $O(opt)+\varepsilon$ 的误差，且该查询复杂度在理论上近似最优。此外，证明了在池基主动学习中，除非使用超多项式数量的未标记样本，否则无法优于被动学习的标签复杂度。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 查询访问对于高效学习广义ReLU至关重要，本工作首次在主动学习框架下实现近乎最优的查询复杂度，且揭示了主动学习在无查询机制下的本质局限。

Abstract: We study the task of agnostically learning general (as opposed to homogeneous) ReLUs under the Gaussian distribution with respect to the squared loss. In the passive learning setting, recent work gave a computationally efficient algorithm that uses $poly(d,1/ε)$ labeled examples and outputs a hypothesis with error $O(opt)+ε$, where $opt$ is the squared loss of the best fit ReLU. Here we focus on the interactive setting, where the learner has some form of query access to the labels of unlabeled examples. Our main result is the first computationally efficient learner that uses $d polylog(1/ε)+\tilde{O}(\min\{1/p, 1/ε\})$ black-box label queries, where $p$ is the bias of the target function, and achieves error $O(opt)+ε$. We complement our algorithmic result by showing that its query complexity bound is qualitatively near-optimal, even ignoring computational constraints. Finally, we establish that query access is essentially necessary to improve on the label complexity of passive learning. Specifically, for pool-based active learning, any active learner requires $\tildeΩ(d/ε)$ labels, unless it draws a super-polynomial number of unlabeled examples.

### [390] [First-Order Trajectory Matching: Fast Ensemble Predictions of Chaotic, Turbulent, Stochastic Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11138)
*Shreya Jha,Timo Schorlepp,Nicholas Geissler,Jules Berman,Benjamin Peherstorfer*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: FTM是一种无需模拟即可学习概率质量局部传输的代理建模方法，通过匹配轨迹的一阶运动来直接估计概率流速度，从而在保持时间边缘分布的同时捕捉通量、环流等轨迹相关量。该方法避免了漂移、扩散和评分估计，且在适当平衡时间分辨率与样本量时具有稳定性。实验表明，FTM在多种随机动力系统和偏微分方程中实现了低计算成本的轨迹感知集合预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在估计概率流时依赖于漂移、扩散或分数估计，计算复杂且易受噪声影响。本文旨在提出一种直接从轨迹学习概率流速度的高效、稳定方法，以实现高精度的集合预测而无需复杂模拟。

Method: 提出第一阶轨迹匹配（FTM），通过匹配轨迹对称一阶运动来估计概率电流速度。利用一个无一步模拟的损失函数，直接从数据中学习当前速度，不需显式建模漂移或扩散项。

Result: 在多个随机动力系统和偏微分方程案例中，FTM成功实现了高保真度的轨迹感知集合预测，计算成本显著低于传统方法，且在合理设置下表现出良好的稳定性。

Conclusion: FTM提供了一种高效、稳定且无需模拟的替代方案，用于从轨迹中学习概率流，适用于复杂系统的集合预测，为动态系统建模提供了新思路。

Abstract: We introduce First-Order Trajectory Matching (FTM), a surrogate-modeling method that learns the first-order local transport of probability mass from trajectories of stochastic systems. By matching the symmetric first-order motion of trajectories, FTM learns the probability current velocity, whose flow preserves time marginals to match ensemble averages, while also capturing current-like trajectory quantities such as fluxes, circulations, and barrier-crossing currents. FTM learns the current velocity directly from trajectories, avoiding drift, diffusion, and score estimation. Our stability analysis separates discretization error from sampling variance and shows that the one-step simulation-free FTM loss is stable when temporal resolution and sample size are properly balanced. Across stochastic dynamical systems and PDE examples, we empirically demonstrate that FTM provides trajectory-aware ensemble predictions at low, deterministic-rollout cost.

</details>


### [391] [OncoTraj: a public benchmark for longitudinal resistance prediction in EGFR-mutant non-small-cell lung cancer on osimertinib](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11144)
*Abhijoy Sarkar,Aarchi Singh Thakur*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: OncoTraj 是一个公开的基准数据集，包含813名接受一线奥希替尼治疗的EGFR突变非小细胞肺癌（NSCLC）患者，来自三个真实世界临床基因组来源。该数据集定义了三个固定任务：(A) 12个月里程碑的进展二分类，(B) 首次进展时间的回归，(C) 主要耐药机制的六分类。研究提供了数据、经过审计的训练/验证/测试划分、开源评估工具和六种基线模型。使用单时间点组织NGS数据作为输入，所有模型在源内评估中均未超过随机水平，表明性能瓶颈在于输入模态而非算法。但数据仍揭示了文献一致的发现：TP53共突变使12个月进展率从29%升至59%。该基准为后续研究设定了可重复的基线，并明确了需通过串联ctDNA数据升级至v2版本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前缺乏公开基准用于训练和评估针对奥希替尼耐药的纵向患者轨迹的计算模型。尽管EGFR突变NSCLC对奥希替尼的耐药是受控克隆进化的典型例子，但现有数据多为分散且异构的，难以用于系统性建模。因此亟需一个标准化、可复现的基准来推动算法发展。

Method: 整合来自MSK-CHORD（672例）、AACR Project GENIE BPC NSCLC（34例）和FLAURA分子耐药补充数据（107例）的临床基因组数据，进行统一处理与标准化，构建包含患者轨迹的公共数据集OncoTraj。设计三类任务：二分类（12个月进展）、回归（时间到首次进展）、六分类（主要耐药机制）。提供严格无泄漏的数据划分、开源评估框架及多种基线模型（从简单多数类预测到深度学习模型如LSTM和多任务Transformer）。

Result: 在仅使用单时间点组织二代测序（NGS）数据的情况下，所有模型在内部源评估中均未能显著超越随机水平，表明性能上限由输入模态决定，而非算法本身。然而，研究成功复现了已知生物学关联：携带TP53共突变患者的12个月进展率从29%上升至59%，与文献一致。该结果验证了数据质量与基准的有效性。

Conclusion: OncoTraj建立了首个经审计、可复现的公开基准，明确限定了当前基于单时间点组织NGS数据的建模能力边界。其核心启示是：未来突破必须依赖于序列化液体活检（ctDNA）数据。本工作为下一代模型（v2）提供了清晰的设计方向——即引入动态、连续的分子监测数据以捕捉耐药演化过程。

Abstract: Resistance to first-line osimertinib in EGFR-mutant non-small-cell lung cancer (NSCLC) is the canonical example of predictable clonal evolution under therapeutic pressure, yet no public benchmark exists for training or evaluating computational models on the corresponding longitudinal patient trajectories. We introduce OncoTraj, a public benchmark of 813 EGFR-mutant NSCLC patients receiving first-line osimertinib, harmonized from three real-world clinical-genomic sources: MSK-CHORD (672 patients), AACR Project GENIE BPC NSCLC (34 patients), and the FLAURA molecular-resistance supplement (107 patients). OncoTraj defines three locked tasks: (A) binary classification of progression by a fixed 12-month landmark, (B) regression of time-to-first-progression in days, and (C) six-class classification of the dominant resistance mechanism. We release the harmonized dataset, patient-level train/validation/test splits with an audited no-leakage guarantee, an open-source evaluation harness, and six reference baselines spanning a majority-class predictor, logistic regression, random forest, XGBoost, an LSTM, and a multi-task transformer. With v1's single-timepoint snapshot features, no task clears chance on clean within-source evaluation: the uniformity of this ceiling across every model class localizes the limit to the input modality (single-snapshot tissue NGS rather than serial ctDNA), not the algorithm. The benchmark does recover a reproducible literature-consistent association: TP53 co-mutation raises the 12-month progression rate from 29% to 59% cohort-wide. OncoTraj establishes a reproducible, leakage-audited baseline and converts the modality limit into concrete design requirements for a serial-ctDNA-enriched v2.

### [392] [Efficiently Learning Drifting Halfspaces with Massart Noise](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11149)
*Mingchen Ma,Guyang Cao,Jelena Diakonikolas,Ilias Diakonikolas*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 研究在线学习中存在Massart噪声的漂移概念问题，针对可分间隔的线性分类器（半空间），提出一种计算高效的算法，实现误差 $η+ \tilde O(Δ^{1/3}/γ)$；在可实现情况下，改进了先前工作。同时证明了信息-计算权衡的下界，表明 $Δ^{1/3}$ 的依赖关系对低次多项式测试是不可避免的，暗示算法性能几乎最优。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决在动态目标概念和噪声标签共存下的在线学习挑战，尤其关注具有几何结构的线性分类器类，旨在设计高效且误差接近理论最优的算法。

Method: 设计一种基于稳健统计估计与在线优化结合的方法，利用历史样本中的噪声结构进行偏差校正，并通过引入漂移率与间隔参数的平衡机制提升鲁棒性。在可实现情形下进一步优化算法结构以降低误差。同时采用低度多项式假设下的复杂性分析方法，建立信息-计算权衡的下界。

Result: 提出算法在一般情况下达到 $η+ \tilde O(Δ^{1/3}/γ)$ 的误差上界；在可实现设置中优于已有方法；并证明了在低度多项式模型下，$Δ^{1/3}$ 的依赖无法避免，说明该性能已逼近最优。

Conclusion: 本研究揭示了在漂移概念与噪声共存场景中，学习效率与误差之间的本质权衡。所提出的算法在计算效率和误差界之间取得了良好平衡，其性能被证明在一定限制下是几乎最优的，为在线学习理论提供了重要新见解。

Abstract: We study the problem of learning a drifting concept in the presence of Massart noise. In this framework, an online learner has access to a history of independent samples whose labels are noisy versions of a target concept that may change from round to round. The goal is to output, in each round, a hypothesis with small prediction error. We study the complexity of this learning problem for the fundamental class of margin-separable linear classifiers (halfspaces). On the positive side, we give a computationally efficient learner achieving error $η+ \tilde O(Δ^{1/3}/γ)$, where $η$ upper bounds the Massart noise rate, $Δ$ is the drift rate, and $γ$ is the margin. Interestingly, in the realizable setting, an adaptation of our techniques yields an efficient learner with an improved error rate over prior work. On the lower-bound side, we provide formal evidence of an information-computation tradeoff, strongly suggesting that our algorithm's performance is essentially optimal. Specifically, while the information-theoretically optimal error scales with $Δ^{1/2}$, we prove that $Δ^{1/3}$-scaling is unavoidable for low-degree polynomial tests, even in the special case of random classification noise.

### [393] [COGENT: Continuous Graph Emulators with Neural Ordinary Differential Equations for Long-Term Physical Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11162)
*Zesheng Liu,Maryam Rahnemoonfar*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: COGENT 是一种基于神经微分方程的连续图模拟器，用于在不规则地理空间网格上进行长期物理预测。它通过图结构的历史编码器捕捉系统状态和外部强迫的历史信息，生成节点级上下文向量，并以此初始化条件化的潜在神经微分方程。该模型利用插值后的未来强迫和显式的时间滚动来驱动动态，实现任意时间点的连续时间预测，避免了固定时间步长的限制。残差解码器将潜在轨迹映射回物理状态，支持直接多步预测。为稳定长时程训练，提出滚动时间跨度采样和渐进式调度策略。在冰盖模拟数据上评估，COGENT 在长时程稳定性方面优于自回归图基模型，表明连续图神经微分方程在不规则网格上的可扩展物理预测中具有潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在不规则地理空间网格上的长期物理预测中存在时间离散化限制、长期依赖建模困难以及预测不稳定等问题，尤其在需要任意时间点查询的应用中表现不佳。因此，亟需一种能够实现连续时间演化、稳定长时程预测且支持灵活时间查询的建模框架。

Method: COGENT 采用图结构编码器对历史状态和外部强迫进行编码，生成节点级别的上下文向量；使用神经微分方程（Neural ODE）作为潜在动力学系统，以插值未来强迫和显式时间变量为驱动；通过残差解码器将潜变量轨迹映射回物理空间，实现无需递归反馈的多步预测；引入滚动时间跨度采样与渐进式调度策略以提升训练稳定性。

Result: 在冰盖-海平面系统模型生成的瞬态冰盖模拟数据上，COGENT 显著提升了长期预测的稳定性，相比自回归图基模型在长时间尺度下表现出更优的精度和鲁棒性，且支持任意时间点的预测查询。

Conclusion: 连续图神经微分方程为不规则地理空间网格上的物理系统模拟提供了高效、稳定且灵活的建模方式，特别适用于需要长时程预测和任意时间点查询的场景，具备良好的可扩展性和应用前景。

Abstract: In this work, we present COGENT, a continuous graph emulator with Neural Ordinary Differential Equations for long-term physical forecasting on irregular geospatial meshes. COGENT encodes a finite history of system states and associated forcing fields and external forcings with a graph-based history encoder, producing node-wise context vectors that capture both local spatial interactions and temporal evolution. These context vectors initialize and condition a latent Neural Ordinary Differential Equation whose dynamics are driven by interpolated future forcings and explicit relative rollout time. By modeling the forecast trajectory as a continuous latent dynamical system, COGENT can generate predictions at arbitrary future times rather than being restricted to a fixed temporal discretization. A residual decoder maps the resulting latent trajectories back to future physical states, enabling direct multi-step forecasting without repeatedly feeding predicted states back into the model. This formulation combines graph-based spatial representation, history-conditioned latent dynamics, and continuous-time rollout in a unified framework for mesh-based physical simulation emulation. In order to stabilize training with long-horizon supervision, we also propose effective rollout-horizon sampling and a progressive rollout-horizon scheduling strategy. We evaluate COGENT on transient ice-sheet simulations generated by the Ice-sheet and Sea-level System Model, demonstrating improved long-range stability over autoregressive graph baselines. These results suggest that continuous graph Neural ODEs provide a promising methodology for scalable physical forecasting on irregular geospatial meshes, particularly in applications that require stable long-horizon predictions and the ability to query system states at arbitrary times.

### [394] [Algorithmic and Minimax Complexities in Kernel Bandits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11171)
*Yunbei Xu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过算法信息语言统一了GP-UCB与DEC方法，提出一种结合两者优势的防护型主算法，并在核强化学习带中表明算法复杂度可能比类级极小极大或DEC证书更具信息量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将看似属于不同理论框架的GP-UCB与DEC方法置于同一分析框架下，揭示其本质差异与互补性，以提升对过参数化模型中算法复杂度的理解。

Method: 引入统一的MAIR框架与异质正定算法先验，结合算法轨迹复杂度与计算可处理性，推广了GP-UCB分析并改进了MAMS算法，提出一种融合优势的防护型主算法。

Result: 证明了在核强化学习带中，算法信息可提供比类级极小极大或DEC证书更优的性能界限，凸显算法复杂度与类级极小极大系数所回答问题的本质差异。

Conclusion: 算法信息与类级极小极大系数解决不同问题，导致不同差距；核带模型为这一区别提供了清晰的数学呈现场景。

Abstract: Gaussian-process upper confidence bound (GP-UCB) and decision-estimation-coefficient (DEC) methods may appear, at first sight, to belong to different theories. This paper places the two viewpoints in a common algorithmic-information language for frequentist RKHS bandits. GP-UCB fixes an algorithmic, rather than true, Gaussian-process prior and exploits realized-trajectory complexity together with computational tractability, whereas MAMS optimizes a robust class-wide MAIR/DEC envelope. Through the unified MAIR framework and heterogeneous positive-semidefinite algorithmic priors, we generalize both the GP-UCB analysis and the MAMS algorithm, propose a safeguarded master that combines their advantages, and provide a kernel-bandit construction showing that algorithmic complexity can be more informative than class-wide minimax or DEC certificates in overparameterized models. The resulting message is that algorithmic information and class-wide minimax coefficients answer different questions and can lead to different gaps; kernel bandits provide a clean setting in which this distinction becomes mathematically visible.

### [395] [Predicting Future Behaviors in Reasoning Models Enables Better Steering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11172)
*Evgenii Kortukov,Piotr Komorowski,Florian Klein,Paula Engl,Gabriele Sarti,Seong Joon Oh,Sebastian Lapuschkin,Wojciech Samek*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种新的文本级控制方法Future Probe Controlled Generation（FPCG），通过训练激活探针预测大模型在后续推理步骤中的行为可能性，从而实现更精准的输出控制。相比传统基于隐藏表示干预的方法，FPCG避免了输出质量下降问题，并在多个评估场景中表现优于已有技术。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有测试时控制方法依赖于已生成文本中的行为检测特征，但这些特征无法有效预测未来行为，导致控制效果不佳且可能降低输出质量。

Method: 训练激活探针以从中间推理步骤中预测未来行为的发生概率；基于该预测结果，在生成过程中采样多个候选句子并选择最符合预期行为的输出。

Result: FPCG在不同任务中对行为预测准确率达64%-91%，显著提升控制精度，同时几乎不损失输出质量，且在激活控制失效的场景中仍可成功应用。

Conclusion: 区分行为检测与行为预测内部特征，有助于实现更精细、高效的大型语言模型行为控制。未来工作应聚焦于探索和利用这类预测性内部表征。

Abstract: Deployed large reasoning models (LRMs) often behave unexpectedly. Test-time steering controls LRM outputs by intervening on their hidden representations, but it can degrade output quality. We argue that prior steering work implicitly relies on internal features that detect behavior in already generated text. We show that these detection features are poor predictors of future behavioral outcomes, and thus not the natural intervention target. Instead, we train activation probes to predict future behavior likelihoods from intermediate reasoning steps. These probes predict the most likely behavior with 64%-91% accuracy, revealing a separate type of internal prediction features. Building on these prediction features, we introduce a text-level steering method, Future Probe Controlled Generation. FPCG samples multiple candidate sentences and chooses the best one according to a probe predicting the future behavior likelihood. This enables steering with almost no output quality degradation. FPCG also enables steering in several evaluations where activation steering fails. These results show that distinguishing detection and prediction features enables a more nuanced approach to controlling LRM behaviors.

### [396] [EEVEE: Towards Test-time Prompt Learning in the Real World for Self-Improving Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11182)
*Weixian Xu,Shilong Liu,Mengdi Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: EEVEE 是首个面向 LLM 代理的多数据集测试时提示学习框架，可在真实任务流中实现测试时提示学习。针对现有方法仅适用于单数据集、难以应对异构输入流的问题，EEVEE 引入路由器将输入划分到不同任务簇，并分配至合适的提示配置，通过路由器与提示协同进化策略优化二者关系。实验表明，该框架在异构数据流下显著提升鲁棒性，同时保持单基准学习能力与效率，相比 Qwen3-4B-Instruct 和 DeepSeek-V3.2 平均多基准得分提升 10.38 和 24.32 点，优于 SOTA 方法 GEPA 与 ACE 最多 37.2% 和 48.2%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有提示学习方法主要针对单数据集场景设计，难以适应真实世界中来自多个数据集、领域和任务分布的异构输入流，限制了其实际应用。需要一种能处理多源异构任务流的测试时提示学习框架，以增强模型在复杂现实环境中的适应能力。

Method: 提出 EEVEE 框架，引入路由器将输入按任务特性划分为不同簇，并匹配相应提示配置；采用路由器与提示协同进化策略，通过交替优化路由器与提示模块，缓解跨数据集干扰，解决两者间的相互依赖问题。

Result: 在多个数据集上的实验显示，EEVEE 显著提升模型在异构数据流下的鲁棒性，同时保持高效性和单基准学习能力；相较于 Qwen3-4B-Instruct 与 DeepSeek-V3.2，平均多基准得分分别提升 10.38 和 24.32 点；优于 SOTA 方法 GEPA 与 ACE 最多 37.2% 和 48.2%。

Conclusion: EEVEE 作为首个支持多数据集测试时提示学习的框架，有效解决了真实任务流中跨数据集干扰问题，具备更强的泛化能力和实用性，为 LLM 代理在复杂动态环境中的部署提供了有力支撑。

Abstract: In this paper, we propose EEVEE, the first multi-dataset test-time prompt learning framework for LLM agents, enabling test-time prompt learning under real-world task streams. Existing methods are largely designed for single-dataset settings, while real-world applications require models to handle heterogeneous input streams drawn from multiple datasets, domains, and task distributions, limiting their practical applicability. To mitigate cross-dataset interference, EEVEE introduces a router that partitions incoming inputs into task clusters and assigns them to suitable prompt configurations. This design is optimized via a router-prompt co-evolution strategy, which employs interleaved router and prompt learning phases to address their mutual dependency. Experiments across multiple datasets demonstrate that the framework improves robustness under heterogeneous data streams while maintaining single-benchmark learning capability and efficiency. Specifically, EEVEE improves average multi-benchmark scores by 10.38 and 24.32 points over Qwen3-4B-Instruct and DeepSeek-V3.2, surpassing SOTA methods GEPA and ACE by up to 37.2% and 48.2%.

### [397] [When to Align, When to Predict: A Phase Diagram for Multimodal Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11190)
*Ilay Kamai,Hugues Van Assel,Aviv Regev,Hagai B. Perets,Randall Balestriero*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一个统一的线性框架，系统分析跨模态对齐（CA）和跨模态预测（CP）在多模态表征学习中的适用性。通过在结构化跨模态干扰相关性的尖峰信号加噪声模型下推导分离比，揭示了两种方法的互补失败模式：对齐会白化各模态，在跨视图干扰强相关时失效；预测则通过单侧白化编码可交叉预测的信息，其恢复能力取决于源模态质量。由此构建的相图将多模态问题划分为四个区域：两者都有效、仅CA有效、仅CP有效、均无效。研究提出一种数据驱动的方法，利用少量标注样本定位真实数据集在相图中的位置，从而在训练前确定最优目标与预测方向。实验在合成数据、立体视觉基准、图像-文本对及真实天体物理数据上验证了非线性场景下的预测，包括‘均无效’情形——此时跨模态训练反而有害。该框架使从业者能诊断问题并选择合适目标，避免盲目训练。代码已开源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前跨模态对齐（CA）和跨模态预测（CP）是多模态表示学习的主流范式，但缺乏对二者何时成功、何时失败，以及跨模态训练是否真正有益的系统理解。尤其在生物医学、天体物理等科学领域，数据具有异质性、多层次组织结构和测量方式，导致标准方法表现不佳，而现有方法无法解释原因。因此亟需一个理论框架来指导实践。

Method: 基于尖峰信号加噪声模型，引入结构化的跨模态冗余相关性，推导出CA与CP的分离比，分析各自在不同条件下的性能边界；构建四象限相图以划分多模态任务的四种类型；设计数据驱动流程，利用小规模标注样本估计数据在相图中的位置，从而决定优先采用的目标与预测方向。

Result: 理论推导揭示了CA与CP的互补失败机制：对齐在跨模态干扰强相关时失效，预测依赖于源模态质量；相图成功划分出四种任务类型；实验验证了在合成数据、立体视觉、图文对及真实天体物理数据上的预测准确性，包括在‘均无效’区域中跨模态训练反而有害的现象；所提方法可在无训练前提前诊断并选择最优策略。

Conclusion: 本研究建立了一个统一的理论框架，能够系统诊断多模态学习问题的性质，明确指出何时应使用对齐、预测或放弃跨模态训练，为科学领域的多模态应用提供了可解释、可操作的决策支持。

Abstract: Cross-modal alignment (CA) and cross-modal prediction (CP) are the dominant paradigms for multimodal representation learning, yet there is no systematic understanding of when each succeeds, when each fails, and when cross-modal training helps at all -- a gap that leaves practitioners, especially in scientific domains like biomedicine or astrophysics, with heterogeneous instruments and multiple levels of organization and measurement, unable to diagnose why standard methods underperform the best single modality. We develop a unified linear framework that addresses both questions. Under a spiked signal-plus-noise model with structured cross-modal nuisance correlation, we derive separation ratios for both objectives that expose complementary failure modes: alignment whitens each modality and fails when nuisance is strongly correlated across views; prediction encodes whatever is cross-predictable through a one-sided whitening, with recovery governed by source-modality quality. The resulting phase diagram partitions multimodal problems into four regimes: Both, CA only, CP only, and Neither. We present a data-driven procedure to locate real-world datasets in this diagram using a small labeled subsample, identifying the preferred objective and prediction direction before any cross-modal training. Experiments on synthetic data, stereo-vision benchmarks, image-caption pairs, and real astrophysical data validate the predictions in the nonlinear regime, including the Neither regime where cross-modal training is actively harmful. Our framework lets practitioners diagnose their multimodal problem and choose the right objective before committing to training. Code to reproduce the results is available at https://github.com/IlayMalinyak/mm_align_vs_pred.

</details>
